# 29-sai Dokushin wa Isekai ch.88 -

~Back to the Elven Village~

It’s Taichi here.  

We’re on our way home after finishing a trade at the Penguin Village――no, the Birdkin Village. On our way home… I noticed that Elmina-san and Rifana were acting strangely.

[What are you looking at?]

[I’m not really looking. And why are you acting so pissed?]

[You’re annoying! It’s nothing!]

I’m planning to stop by the Cait Sith Village, camp in the forbidden area today, and spend the night at the Harpie Village tomorrow, but Rifana’s mood is getting worse and worse. She would bite me just because I made eye contact with her. What did I do?

[Don’t bite on him like that, Rifana. If you act so pissed, he’ll only be scared of you.]

Elmina-san got between me and Rifana and gently meditated. Or rather, what is this subtle body contact? Elmina’s hands moved from my chest to my stomach. I looked at her wondering what it was, and she replied with a look that said “It’s nothing.”  

Seeing this, Rifana frowned even more and ground her teeth. Stop it, a girl shouldn’t make that face. Breeda, Breeda, help me. Whoa, that guy is making his face look dazzling.  

What on earth is going on? What caused it?

『Not my faultー』

No, it’s you. It’s definitely you. What did you do this time? I can’t just ignore that people around me are seemingly trying to hit on me, can I? Especially since one of them is my stepmother, and the other is a girl who actually hated me. Isn’t that going a bit too far?

『No, no, really, I didn’t do anything to them. I swear.』

You’re lying. Something’s clearly wrong with the two of them.

『I’m not lying. I didn’t do anything to them.』

Then what’s with this mini-battle situation? The two of them have been acting strange ever since they decided to leave Penguin Village.

『I wonder why? Maybe it was something about your pheromones?』

There’s no way something so strange could happen.

『The heart is complicated and strange. Maybe she saw the image of her late husband in you, or maybe she was attracted to the way you faced dangerous monsters without caring about yourself, or maybe she was touched by your innocent appearance, or maybe she was fascinated by the way you were so absorbed in something and devoted yourself to it.』

That’s so specific.  

But you, is something so… so easy to do? Can’t it? No, it can’t. I don’t think it can… but looking at the past. With Marl, it was just love at first sight. Fram… well, that’s what it is, but Tina… well.

『There’s no such thing as impossible! (sternly)』

You say that with your own mouth? I mean, you said you didn’t do anything to those two, but you didn’t say you didn’t do anything to me, did you? What did you do?

『……whistle, whistle』

Why are you whistling? Hey, what did you do? Spit it out.

『I didn’t do anything important. I just tweaked the conditions for gaining access to your library.』

Library? Conditions for gaining access? I don’t get it, explain.

『Is the library like the root of the skill system? It’s a place that accumulates, integrates, and manages the experience and knowledge of the user. It’s not a real place, it’s more like a phase or a dimension, so humans can’t see or recognize it directly.』

Like Akashic Records?

『Yes, that’s it. It’s like the source of knowledge and experience. The skill system allows constant access to the information and experience accumulated in the library according to the user’s experience and proficiency. Access to programs called “skills” is opened by actions and experience, and you can take a certain level of action without even thinking about it. That’s what it means to acquire skills.’』

I see? It’s like cloud computing for knowledge and experience. The skill point system forcibly intervenes in the system and makes it possible to use the service by force, right?

『Bingo. So, what I did this time was to make the conditions for gaining access to the library more lenient, so in short, it made it possible to acquire skills with fewer actions and experiences. To put it simply, I have tampered with your ‘talent’ so to speak』

Hmm. You can do that and get away with it without them finding out?

『Don’t worry, there are plenty of people with this level of talent. Or rather, there was a person right next to you who was extraordinarily talented, right? Someone who learned skills at an extraordinary speed.』

Ah… that was Marl. Her skill acquisition speed was extraordinary. When I first met her, she was so timid she could barely swing a sword, but after just a little training she had mastered dual-wielding. She also improved at an incredible speed in wind magic and alchemy.

『That kid is a bit strange. She’s Real’s hero. If she really trained, I think she’d probably be stronger than you.』

What’s that? It’s scary. If she turns into a beast, there’ll be nothing I can do but be sucked dry. Scary.  

By the way, Real-san?

『Yes, your eternal lover, Real-chan here☆』

Can you tell me about the causal relationship between what we’ve said so far and the current situation?

[Gugigigigi.]

[Ufufufufu.]

While I was interrogating the useless god in my head, Rifana was desperately pulling on my arm, trying to pull me away from Elmina-san, but Elmina-san continued to hold my body without moving. As a result, my arm hurts a lot.  

Stop it already! I’d cry because my arms felt like it’s about to come off!

『Elves are very perfect as living creatures. They have long life spans, so basically they don’t need to have many children.』

Hmm, so?

『Well, if they’re left to breed naturally, it’s difficult for the population to recover if there’s an unexpected accident that reduces the population. That’s why they have a mating season.』

I see.

『But, that mating season lasts for quite a long time. If you meet a superior individual and can’t have children because it’s not mating season, that’s a problem in itself.』

Ah, okay.

『So if they meet an individual that is superior to them, they’ll be forced to go into mating season. Maybe it was stimulated by me messing with Taichi’s ‘talent’?』

Put it back. Put it back now. Hurry! Hurry!! Hurry!!

『Well, it was pretty hard to manipulate it so they wouldn’t notice, right? It’s also very useful in terms of acquiring skills, isn’t it?』

But even so! You really should stop doing this! It’s just making things awkward!

『Actually, even if I put it back now, it’s not like the mating season will stop. Well, have fun』

This damn evil god… I’ll remember this.

『I won’t remember this☆』

The god was silent after that. She must be grinning and enjoying the current situation. What a really bad taste.

[Ah… Let’s get on with our work for now, shall we?]

The two of them turned towards me.

[… Right, this is no time to play.]

[…Fuuh.]

The two of them left me and started preparing for camp. I sighed quietly. My wives who got along so well despite me having that many were really good wives.

================

My nightwatch shift today was decided to be done together with Breeda. It was decided by the two women. The men had no say.  

After dinner, I waited until the two women were asleep and then I turned to Breda.

[For elves, what about widows starting new families with other men, or polygamy?]

[It’s not impossible. Our lives are long enough that we can end our partnerships and find new partners without being separated by death. Also, there are fewer men, so in rare cases, one person can have multiple partners at the same time.]

[I see.]

[Still, I’ve never heard of someone having a daughter and the mother at the same time.]

[Is that bad?]

[If the man is not directly related by blood with the women, it’s fine. It’s not uncommon for elves to partner with other races, so it shouldn’t be a problem. It seems that many elves partnered with humans when we lived outside the Great Forest.]

As he said this, Breda threw a twig into the bonfire. The crackling and popping sounds of the bonfire could be heard. The light of the bonfire and the floating phosphorescence created a fantastical scene.

[Well, it’s no wonder they’re attracted to you. You’re… to put it bluntly, cute.]

[Haa? Cute? Me?]

I don’t know how to respond to Breda saying that with a straight face… What on earth is this, Breda! Explain it to me!

[Well, how should I put it… We elves can see a person’s heart through their eyes. The eyes of those with evil hearts look dirty, and on the other hand, the eyes of those with honest hearts look beautiful. Your eyes… Well, it looks like you’re deliberately disguising yours as dirty to hide your beauty. That’s what we elves find so irresistibly cute.]

[I don’t get it at all.]

[It’s hard to explain in words. It’s something you feel in your heart.]

Breda shrugged and stopped talking.  

Well, it was good that I wouldn’t be criticized by elves for having a relationship with either Elmina or Rifana. The rest would depend on how I responded. Should I reject it or accept it? If I accept it, what would I do next? How would I explain it to my wives?  

Whatever choice I made, it was depressing just thinking about it. Should I just not choose anything and just disappear? No, that would be terrible. Whatever choice I made, I should face it head on. But, but, hmm.

『YOU! Just do it without thinking too much, YO! Let’s pursue fleeting pleasure.』

You’ve been trying to hide your evil god-like side lately, haven’t you? What’s your goal?

『You and I are literally one and the same, aren’t we? I thought I’d expose everything and build a relationship of trust.』

That sounds like a lie. Are you hiding something from me?

『I am most definitely not』

Damn, that sounds so obvious I can’t tell if it’s true or not.

[Haa…]

I let out a deep, deep sigh. There’s no point in worrying about it. I’ll find a good time to have a long talk with them.  

But… What should I do? Should I accept it, or reject it? No, it’s no good to agonize over it. Let’s just go with the “come what may” mentality. There’s a saying that it’s shameful for a man to not eat the food that’s set before him. I should get used to this world soon, yeah.  

However, I won’t lose sight of where I should return to. Let’s swear to myself and keep going. I will definitely leave the Great Forest. Absolutely. There’s only one place for me to belong.

After changing nightwatch shifts, we woke up and returned to the elf treetop village, passing through the harpies settlement and the beastkin village. At the harpies settlement, I was able to meet Piruru’s family. Piruru’s mother and sister were very grateful, and I received a letter and their feathers. Now I have one more reason to go home.  

By the way, I didn’t sleep with the harpies this time. Yes, it’s a shame. Seriously?  

At the beastkin village, we just dropped off supplies and nothing particularly noteworthy happened. Just like last time, I slept with Breda at Tiga’s house. Elmina-san and Rifana seemed calmer since camping in the forbidden area. I wonder if they had a discussion while I was sleeping.

[Ah… we’ve arrived.]

[Right.]

[Shopping this time was easy.]

[I didn’t have to carry heavy luggage though]

Looking up at the treetop village from directly below. It seemed they had already noticed our return, as several elves were looking down at us. With Elmina-san at the front, we all jumped up to the treetop village. I jumped up as well as the three elves.  

After spending the night with Harpie, I got used to using wind magic, and was able to rise up as smoothly as the other three. The elves looked at me with admiration. Hehe, I’m making progress too.

[Welcome back.]

[I’m glad you made it back safely.]

[I’m glad you’re safe.]

As I listen to their words of appreciation, I spit the salt and other goods we’d exchanged into the square. Elmina-san said she managed to secure a fair amount of salt and goods this time. She got about 80% of the other items she requested, and turned the rest into salt.  

I guess it can’t be helped that you can’t always get what you want in the Great Forest, where there aren’t many things. The client seemed to understand that this couldn’t be helped. Or rather, everyone understands that it’ll be a stroke of luck to get everything, so it wasn’t a problem.

[Well then.]

With that, Breda walked off with one of the elf women who’d come to greet us. Was he married? Rifana stared at me for a while before walking off somewhere without a word. Ah, no, she’s back.  

Rifana returned and walked straight towards me. Wow, her face was scary. She grabbed me by the collar.

[Let me see your face for a second.]

[Yes, ma’am.]

I feel like I’ll get punched if I refuse, so I nod obediently. Why is Elmina-san smiling and waving her hand as she sees me off? This sort of sequence seems familiar.  

Rifana brought me to a house. From the looks of it, the layout seems a size smaller than Elmina-san’s house. I was invited inside, so I went in first.  

This house was also carved out of a giant tree, and the inside had a strong woody scent. Mixed in with that was the scent of flowers? A fresh scent tickled my nostrils. There was some kind of rattling going on behind me, what was it?  

I turned around, but there was only Rifana glaring at me with a sullen expression. There was a tool bag filled with salt and travel equipment, as well as a bow and arrow at my feet, so I thought it was the sound of her putting them down.

[Sit down.]

[Yes.]

She glared at me, the intensity leaving no room for argument. I had no choice but to be quiet like a cat on a stray. I sat obediently in a strange chair with a log back, watching Rifana as she headed to the kitchen. It seemed that she’d be making tea or something. She’s going to treat me as a guest.  

While waiting, I’m getting bored, so I look around the room, despite knowing it’s rude of me to do so. It’s a rather plain room, how should I put it. Most of the furniture is simple and practical.  

However, it’s impressive to see that various dried flowers are displayed here and there, as if making dried flowers is a hobby of hers. The refreshing scent I can faintly detect among the scent of wood must come from the dried flowers.  

After a while, Rifana approached the table with a tray of what appears to be tea. Glasses were filled with a deep red liquid. Judging from the lack of steam, it appears to be cold tea.

[Here you go.]

[Thanks.]

I stared at the crimson liquid in front of me. The sunlight streaming in through the window makes the tea sparkle and look very beautiful.

[What? It’s not poisonous.]

[No, I just thought it was pretty. Thank you.]

I took a sip of the crimson liquid. A soft, refreshing floral scent wafted through my nose. The taste was neither particularly sweet nor bitter, it’s refreshing. But, this scent was wonderful. It’s a tea that you enjoy for its aroma rather than its taste.

[It smells good.]

[R, really?]

For some reason, Rifana was staring at me as I drank the tea. When she noticed my gaze, she hurriedly took a sip of the tea herself.

[So, what’s this about?]

[Nothing really… I just wanted to talk. Hey, how did you and Melchina spend your time together?]

[Well, I was pretty busy with work sometimes, but when we were together we’d walk in the forest together, or hang out in the room together, or go out to eat to find something tasty.]

We often did some jiggling exercises in bed or in the bath, but I’m afraid I’ll get in trouble if I say that, so I’ll keep quiet.

[Umm, there were others, right? What were they like?]

You’re asking me that? Well, whatever.

[I think their relationships were generally good. There were some women she didn’t get along with, but even then it was more like playing around than being serious.]

Melchina didn’t get along with Marl very well, but it wasn’t like they really hated each other. Kusuha was always there to keep things under control.

[R-Really…]

After that, Rifana bowed her head and fell silent. Not sure if I should bring up the topic, I took another sip of tea. Mm, this scent is addictive.  

But, what should I do about this situation? I could tell from Rifana’s fidgety behavior, but I couldn’t decide whether I should be the one to go for it. No, should I take the initiative here?

[I’m planning on leaving this village soon.]

[…Eh?]

[I’ve wandered around the Great Forest this time and gotten to know the way around. Once I’m ready to leave, I’m going to wander around the Great Forest looking for something. It’ll also serve as training.]

Rifana put her hand over her mouth, her eyes wide open and trembling. Watching her, I took another sip of the red tea Rifana made for me. The refreshing scent that tickles my nose calmed my mind.

[Well, I think I’ll come back to this village from time to time. To replenish food and supplies, gather information, or simply to rest. I’ll probably visit other villages as well.]

If I use a shelter made of earth magic, I won’t have any problems resting, and I can probably get some food by hunting in the forest. However, I have no idea how to tell the difference between edible wild plants and fruits, and I can’t completely relax and rest in a shelter made of earth magic. I’ll need to maintain my equipment in a place that’s relatively safe, so it’s probably difficult to survive completely alone in the Great Forest.

[I don’t know how long it will take to find what I’m looking for, but once I’ve accomplished my goal, I’ll leave the Great Forest. I have to return to my wives.]

I looked Rifana in the eye and declared this. This is absolute. I’m returning to Marl and the others. Because that’s where I should be.

[…Why don’t you just stay here forever?]

Rifana muttered.

[I don’t know why you came here, but you should stay here forever. You can hunt here, run through the forest, carry salt, and live a leisurely life.]

[That kind of life might be fine. Having a cute wife in addition, it might be a happy life.]

[Then, do that.]

[No. I’ll end up not being myself. There are so many people I’ve decided to carry on my shoulders. I have to go back to them, and I want to.]

Rifana and I exchanged glances, and a tense atmosphere flowed.

[You’ll die if you keep carrying everything on your shoulders like that.]

[If I carry it all on myself and end up destroying myself, then that means I was not what that is meant to be. Or something along that line.]

I want to do something about those within my reach, within my sight, and within my ears. If the current situation is the result of gaining strength with that single-minded desire, then Rifana may be right.

[It’ll be alright even if you run away. No one will blame you for pursuing only your own happiness.]

[That may be true.]

If it came down to it, I would run away with my wives. I was sure I had made that decision in my heart, but before I knew it, I had taken on more than I could carry on my own. It would have been okay with three wives, but with ten wives, it’s not so easy. There were more people I had to protect besides my wives, and places I had to protect. There was no way out, and I had no choice but to fight.

[I wanted to live freely, but before I knew it, I was entangled with ties.]

When I came to this world, I wanted to enjoy a different world freely. Where did I go wrong? When I think about it, meeting Marl was the beginning of it all. I don’t feel like regretting it at all. Was this also fate?  

Generally speaking, to live freely and without being tied down by anything means to live alone, without any ties to anyone. That way of life is terrifying.

[But still, I’m going back to everyone.]

Marl’s grinning happily, Fram’s quiet smile, Tina’s elegant smile, Kusuha’s relaxed smile, Deborah’s cheerful smile, Karen’s sleepy face, Sherry’s shy smile, Seetan’s wagging tail and joyful whole body, Neela’s loud laughter with her hands over her mouth, and the smiles of everyone living in Clover all flash through my mind.

[That’s where I belong.]

Remembering everyone’s smiles, a sense of loneliness welled up in my chest. I want to go home soon, to everyone.

[I see.]

Rifana muttered as she lowered her gaze to the glass filled with red liquid.  

There’s no right or wrong answer, but this is all I can say.

[But, that’s for your convenience. I have my own.]

Rifana said as she lowered her gaze to the glass, and gulped down the contents. Then she slammed the glass on the table and stood up with a bang.

[Damn! Why did I have to go to this human, of all people…!]

Rifana’s hand reached out with incredible speed and grabbed me by the collar. She looked very angry. I wondered if she was going to hit me, she was stronger than I thought, and I was thinking this, when I saw her face already in front of me.

[Hmph?!]

[Ouch!]

Our lips collided, or rather our teeth! It hurts! Of course it’ll hurt if you collide head-on with that much force!

[It hurts.]

[Shut up! Shut u—hmm?]

Rifana’s face was red and she was about to scream, so I held her head and covered her mouth with my lips. My kissing expertise has naturally been honed since I kissed my wife so much.  

Rifana stopped struggling and her eyes started to get glassy, ​​so I stopped kissing her. Our lips parted, and a bridge of saliva was formed. Her saliva smelled like fresh flowers.

[That is how you kiss.]

As if she had come to her senses after hearing my words, Rifana stepped back with a startled look on her face, then got caught on the chair she was sitting on and fell spectacularly.  

What was she doing? She must be surprisingly clumsy. Scratching my head, I went around the table to where Rifana had fallen, her face bright red, and picked her up. From what I could see, she didn’t seem to be injured.

[I, I, I…]

[You look like you don’t know what’s going on.]

Rifana was breathing heavily and looked like she was about to get dizzy, so I held her to my chest and patted her back. After a while, she seemed to calm down, and her breathing became quieter. She timidly put her arms around my back and hugged me tightly.

[As I said before, I’ll be leaving the forest soon.]

[Do you really have to?]

[I do have to.]

Rifana’s grip on me tightened. It was almost painful.  

After holding me tightly for a while, the strength in her arms suddenly relaxed. Then she stroked my back a few times, and hugged me tightly again.

[Fine then. I’ll come with you.]

[Are you sure?]

[Yes, I really am.]

[If you really say so.]

[Yes.]

+++

**89 – Exploration of the Ruins Begins**

I woke up.  

The first thing I saw was an unfamiliar ceiling. It’s a wooden ceiling with intricately carved annual rings. Then my sense of smell picked up the scent of sweat and lovemaking. I couldn’t sense any warmth in my bed except for my own. My presence detection was definitely working. It seemed that I woke up first.  

I rubbed my eyes, sat up, and looked around. As expected, the room didn’t look very familiar. But the pleasant fatigue and lethargy, along with the state of my bed, brought it all back to life.

『You had fun last night, didn’t you?』

Yeah, yeah, that’s a classic. Ah, hmm… yeah, I messed up. Yeah.

『That was quite a commotion, wasn’t it?』

I ignore the vulgar chirping in my head and bask in the afterglow. Yeah, it won’t make much difference now that I have to deal with one or two more people. I just have to work harder than ever.  

As I was about to purify my body and bed, a thought occurred to me. Hmm, maybe purifying my body aside, but purifying the bed as well? I guess I’ll ask first. Dressed only in my underwear and pants, I headed to the living room where I had tea yesterday.  

Rifana seemed to be preparing breakfast in the kitchen attached to the living room. She jerked back, perhaps startled by the sound of me appearing.

[Good morning.]

[M, mor, morning!?]

[Calm down.]

She looked as if she was about to brandish the knife in her hand, so I quietly approached her and gently restrained her wrist.

[N-no, I’m fine! It’s okay!]

[Really? Don’t hurt yourself with the knife, okay?]

[It’s okay! It’s okay! Just stay seated and wait politely!?]

It felt more dangerous being so close, so I decided to obediently follow her orders.  

Rifana was standing in the kitchen, her silver hair tied in a ponytail, dressed casually and wearing an apron. I stared at her blankly as I thought about what to do next.  

First, I had to prepare for my trip. I needed to bring a set of bedding, even if it was just basic, cooking utensils, shelf-stable food, and seasonings, also a few changes of clothes, which I’d acquired from the beastman village during the salt trade, so that should be enough. Fuel and water can be substituted with fire magic and water magic, so that should do for now. I could use the life magic light to provide light, but it would be better to at least prepare a torch.  

I’d have about a week to get all that equipment ready, and then I’d begin my search for the pseudo-deity.  

It’s probably in the ancient ruins scattered throughout the Great Forest, so I should also gather information on the forbidden areas. I might also have to do something about Elmina. I’d like to take it easy for a day, but it would be rude not to say hello to her and Delfida.

[You have a troubled look on your face.]

[I’m thinking about what to do starting today. I can’t afford to take it easy.]

[I see.]

A large fried egg and a naan-like bun were placed in front of me. What kind of egg is this?

[Looks delicious.]

[It’s a harpie egg.]

[What!?]

[Don’t worry, it’s unfertilized.]

[The problem is…]

I couldn’t help but stare at the fried egg in front of me. A harpie egg… This is from Harpie-san.  

Do I eat it? This? Should I eat it? Is it even fine?

[What’s wrong?]

She’s eating it! She’s putting it on a naan-like bun and eating it like it’s normal! Is it weird that I’m worried? Yeah, I’m sure it is. An egg is an egg no matter what it comes out of. Yeah, I shouldn’t mind.  

Following Rifana’s example, I put the fried harpie fried egg on top of a naan-like bun and took a bite. The fried eggs had been sprinkled with just the right amount of salt, giving them just the right amount of saltiness.

[Delicious.]

[R, really? It’s not even really a dish though, considering it’s so simple.]

As she spoke, Rifana’s ears twitched busily. Oh, she’s so cute. While munching on the fried egg naan, I quenched my thirst with the same refreshing flower tea she’d made me yesterday.  

Ah, I feel the most relaxed I’ve been since coming to the Great Forest.

[You look so relaxed.]

[Because I am.]

[Really?]

Rifana smiled. She could make such a gentle face. I wish she’d always smile like this, without being so mean.

[What is it?]

[Nothing. I just want to see your face.]

[Stop it, it’s embarrassing.]

This time, she blushed and looked away. She was kind of cat-like, to be honest. Just when you think it’s grown attached to you, it turns away, which is very cat-like.

[By the way, about the bed. Can I purify it?]

[W-What…?! You’re not allowed in that room! It’s forbidden! I’ll do it!]

[O-okay.]

Rifana’s face turned red and she stood up, howling. Hmm, it wasn’t a cat, but some kind of wild animal. No, it wasn’t a howl, it was more like a hiss, so it was definitely a cat. However, her body seemed fine. Recovery magic is incredible.

[W-well then! We’ve eaten and I’m going to clean up, so you can get out!]

[Huh? We made so much love yesterday, and you’re going to just kick me out?]

[Y, yes?! No!? N-never mind! Hurry up!]

[Ah, I get it, I get it, so don’t pull, don’t push, don’t push.]

I was pulled and pushed, forced to stand from my seat and towards the exit. Maybe I’d teased her a little too much.

[W-what are you… what are you planning to do tonight!?]

I wonder why this girl sounded half-angry.

[Well, I stayed out overnight without telling Elmina-san. I owe her everything, so I feel like I need to talk to her. I also need to prepare for exploring the Great Forest.]

[Y-yes, that’s true… I don’t know what you’re looking for, but I’m here too.]

[I appreciate the sentiment, but I’m not sure what to say. I’m planning on entering and leaving the restricted area.]

[W-why…]

[I’m looking for something in the restricted area. It’s definitely dangerous, so I’d like to go alone. I’m not a travel novice, but I’ll consult with Elmina-san and Delfida-san about it.]

Even though I have fighting skills, I can’t say I’m an experienced traveler. This is the Great Forest, and it’s different from traveling along the relatively peaceful highway. It’d be best to ask the opinion of someone with more experience living in the Great Forest.

[Don’t worry, I won’t just leave without telling you. Be at ease.]

[I’m not really worried or anything.]

[I see. Well, I’m off then.]

[H-have a nice trip.]

With a blushing face, Rifana saw me off, and I headed off to Elmina-san’s house.

=======================

[Staying out overnight without permission is a bit much.]

[Yes, sorry.]

[You look so much better, don’t you?]

[Yes, sorry.]

[I wonder why you’re apologizing? Did you do something that warrants an apology?]

[I mean]

[You hurt Melchina and then cheated on me with another girl… You’re a bad boy, aren’t you, Taichi-kun?]

[Well… You saw me off with a smile yesterday.]

[Come again?]

[No, never mind.]

I glanced at Delfida-san, pleading for his help, but he shook his head, saying it was impossible.

[I’ll be out for a bit. I’m going to see Garnida for the first time in a while, so I won’t be back for about three days.]

[Wait.]

Delfida-san abandoned me! I trusted you! Delfida-san brushed my accusing gaze aside, then quickly grabbed the bow and quiver that were by the entrance and left.

[Now, the obstacle’s gone.]

[Uh…]

Elmina closed the distance between me and me, who was sitting upright. Those eyes were those of a ravenous beast, no, a demonic beast.

[Don’t you think that sloppy Taichi-kun needs some education?]

Elmina licked her lips. Some sergeant once said that licking your lips in front of prey was a third-rate thing to do, but this was incredibly intimidating.

[Eh? Hey, no! Stop! Don’t step on that spot!? Ah…ahhh!?]

[Ahh, so satisfying.]

[Uh, huh…]

Elmina-san’s skin was shiny, as she sapped everything out of me. I was experiencing a lot of new things for the first time. Or rather, I was never able to take the offensive… Elmina-san is too strong. Marl in her beast form seems like a kitten now.

[There’s no need to cry. Wasn’t it great?]

[Of course, but pride, dignity…]

[It’s the difference in experience. You are fifty years too soon to try to beat me.]

Elmina-san said this so nonchalantly, showing no sign of any anguish over the circumstances.

[But, after all this, was this really okay? Everything.]

[It doesn’t really matter. It’s nothing to devote fifty years or so of my long journey to Taichi-kun.]

[Ah, that’s also what Melchina said.]

[She and I are alike. Besides, you have already ten, so what’s wrong with one or two more joining in?]

[Yeah, it’s fine, but there are a lot of things, you know?]

[Don’t worry, it’s okay. Leave it all to onee-chan. I’ll take care of Taichi-kun’s wives. Including Melchina.]

Elmina said this with a bright smile. She’s so reliable. She’s so cool, I could fall in love with her. What is this sense of security? This is the charm of adulthood.

[Your current goal was to become stronger, right? Do you have any plans?]

[Yes. Apparently there are tools to restore your divine powers in the forbidden area, so I’m planning to go and collect them for now.]

[The forbidden area? I don’t really recommend it.]

[I heard it’s dangerous, right? I suppose that’s true, but it seems like it’s the only option. It would take decades to regain my former powers using normal methods.]

[If you leave your wives alone for that long, they’ll get fed up with you.]

Elmina-san gave a wry smile.

[Well, you need to be fully prepared to head to the restricted area then. I’ll help you.]

[I’m glad to hear that, but I’m planning to go alone?]

[That’s no good. If the elves from other villages find you, you’ll be killed. The villages we stopped at to get salt this time will probably welcome you, but if anyone from any other village finds you, it’ll be a big fuss.]

[Ah… I see.]

Come to think of it, I’d forgotten that the people living in this Great Forest are actually quite exclusive. The only reason I was welcomed so warmly was because I was accompanying Elmina-san and the others.

[I’ll go with you. Besides, traveling alone is hard, isn’t it? You can’t take turns keeping watch, and if you are incapacitated by a minor injury or illness, you’ll definitely die of starvation.]

[I guess that’s true.]

I thought I could manage the sleeping arrangements with earth magic, but maybe I was a little too optimistic.

[Leave it to me. And you’ll need a guide to the restricted area, right?]

[Yes, that’s right. That would be a great help.]

[That’s fine. I’d love to see inside the restricted area too, if that were possible.]

With that, Elmina rose from the bed and stretched. Her back was to me, but her pale skin and beautiful butts were a dazzling view.

[Well, if that’s the case, let’s get ready right away.]

[You look energetic.]

[Taichi-kun has given me so much energy.]

Elmina-san turned around, tying her hair up with a string, and smiled seductively. Ah, no, no, ma’am. I’m getting energized too.

[I thought you’d drain me dry.]

[Oh, did you hate it?]

[It was amazing.]

[That’s so frank of you.]

With a kiss on my cheek, Elmina-san left the room. Even with my stamina, this continuous battle is tough. I feel like I can’t stand up.

『Way to go, you seem to be enjoying yourself there.』

Yeah, I thought you’d be coming out by now. Are you satisfied that everything’s going the way you wanted?

『I’m very satisfied. Aren’t you satisfied?』

I’m very satisfied. But that aside, I don’t like the fact that I’ve been playing around in your palm. Who do you think you are?

『A Goddess?』

I know. Fuck you.

『Anytime! Maybe!』

That’s not what I meant. It was an insult. Sigh, good grief.

『But this will make your quest easier, right?』

I hate that about you. That you don’t give a damn about twisting other people’s fates for your own purposes.

『Mm, that’s hurtful. It’s all for your own good, you know?』

I know. In the end, I guess it’s just the weight of having other people’s fates twisted for my own sake that hurts. I’m just taking my anger out on you, sorry. Thank you.

『Hmph… I don’t know how to respond when you thank me so honestly.』

And with that, the useless Goddess—Rheal—fell silent.  

Now that things have come to this, I guess I should just accept it. After all, I’m up against the gods. If I agonize over things like this when I’m trying to get close to him, I’ll just get caught off guard. I’ll take back my place, no matter what. I made up my mind.

==========================

I spent about a week preparing for the trip—though I relied almost entirely on Elmina-san. I probably couldn’t have gathered everything on my own: bedding, food, seasonings, cooking utensils, and other miscellaneous tools and equipment.  

Of course, I wasn’t just playing around. I practiced building shelters using earth magic and did some blacksmithing work in the elven treetop village in exchange for procuring various tools. I mainly worked on maintaining blades, crafting arrowheads, and servicing other metal products, but it was well received.

[Well, shall we get going?]

Elmina smiled after checking her bow. Her golden hair sparkled dazzlingly in the sunlight filtering through the trees.

[Yes.]

Rifana nodded with a determined expression. Like Elmina-san, she was dressed as if she’s going to hunt, carrying a bow and quiver on her back. Like Elmina-san, she’s also equipped with a large knife at her waist, which seems to be the basic style for elven hunters.  

I asked if it was okay, as her attire exposed a lot of skin. She told me that she always keeps a windshield up while out in the forest, so there’s no need to worry about being stung or bitten by poisonous insects. I asked if she was worried about getting tangled in twigs, and she said that hunters wouldn’t make such a mistake.

[What is it?]

[Nothing, I figured you’d follow me anyway.]

[What’s wrong? I’m a hunter after all. I won’t hold you back.]

[I’m not worried about that.]

I’m well aware of Rifana’s abilities after spending about two weeks working with her. She has the stamina and magic power to move around all day using wind magic, and her archery skills are top notch. Still, I’m worried considering where we’re going.

[More importantly, are you ready?]

[Of course. I’ve made a solid weapon.]

Saying this, I twirled the stick I’d crafted from sacred wood.  

In the end, I wasn’t able to prepare a large metal weapon, but I was able to strengthen the sacred wood stick using Behemoth claws, bones, skin, and a small amount of metal parts. The sacred tree branches already had good magic conductivity and high magic capacity, but by using Behemoth material, it also gained physical strength. Now, the weapon is better balanced than a crude metal weapon. There’s nothing to worry about.

[Are you sure that stick is enough?]

[It’s fine, it’s fine. With this, I can smash even a huge boulder to pieces with a single blow.]

[If you say so, I believe it.]

As she said this, Rifana didn’t hide her suspicious gaze. Well, it was probably only natural for her to be concerned, knowing how it was originally just a stick.

[Well, shall we get going? Our first destination is this, the forbidden area known as Nightmare’s Claw Mark.]

Saying this, I pointed to a spot on a simple map.  

This map was a map of the Great Forest drawn from Elmina-san and Delfida-san’s memories. Centered around the elven treetop settlement, it also marked the locations of the major settlements they knew, the forbidden areas, places to rest, water sources, and landmarks to use while traveling.

[See over there? There’s nothing there, just a bunch of craters and nothing to be found. It’s a magical pool, so monsters won’t come near.]

[Yes, so let’s camp there, and our main destination is this, the Great Sealed Door.]

=====================

The first place we headed to was the forbidden area known as Nightmare’s Claw Mark.  

As Elmina said, it was a desolate place, with only numerous craters. Plant life was scarce, and there was barely any sign of small animals.

[I always have nightmares when I sleep here.]

[Really?]

[When I have business in the villages around here, I sometimes stay here, and I often have nightmares. It’s not really harmful, but it’s a place I’d rather not stay for long.]

Elmina-san gave a wry smile as she looked around the phosphorescent, forbidden area. Rifana, listening to Elmina-san’s story, looked around with a slightly uneasy expression.

『There’s no reaction from any pseudo-divine beings at all. I think this place was probably a divine cannon base or something back then. It looks like it was blown away completely in the counterattack.』

Do you have any idea regarding the nightmares?

『I think the power source of the Divine Cannon that blew this place apart with the counter attack was some kind of Evil God controlling nightmares. I can sense a faint trace of divine power, but it’s difficult to tell.』

I see. I agreed, and shared Rheal’s theory with Elmina-san and Rifana.

[Using a God as the power source for a weapon… I mean, humans back then were pretty amazing.]

[That’s a truly barbaric act that shows no fear of God.]

[The fact that they were wiped out without a trace in the end is probably a case of karma.]

I searched the area to see if there was anything there, but I couldn’t find anything. It was a complete waste of effort. The only real harvest I managed to get was some precious medicinal herbs that grow only in a magic-rich environment.

[They’re an ingredient for a magic potion, so they’re quite valuable.]

[They’d probably sell for a lot if we took them outside the Great Forest.]

[Maybe. But it’s difficult to preserve them well, so I think it’d be difficult to take them.]

[I see. But if that’s the case, wouldn’t that defeat the purpose of picking them?]

[They’ll last for a few days, and they’re pretty effective even if you eat them as is. I picked a few to keep in case of an emergency.]

By the way, I tried munching them and they were quite tasty, so I picked a few more and served them as a salad for dinner. It was quite well received.

======================

『Ta-da-ta-da♪』

A silver-haired Goddess appeared.

[As expected, the scars of a nightmare are the worst.]

『Are you suddenly trying to pick a fight?』

Rheal finally appeared, veins bulging from her forehead. Well, it’s been a while, but I’m sure I’m in the same dreamscape as before. Maybe it would have been kind enough if we hadn’t suddenly merged.

[So, it’s been a while, but what’s the matter today? I just want to get to sleep.]

『I told you there’s a faint remnant of divine power. It affects the minds of sleeping people and gives them nightmares. I came out today to protect you from that, so I hope you’re grateful.』

Rheal crossed her arms, puffed out her cheeks, and pretended to be angry. Damn, she looked so cute, I can’t believe it.

『Huh? Did you think I was a little cute? You did, didn’t you? Yeah, it looks like you’ve finally noticed my charms.』

[If you just kept smiling and stayed quiet, you’d be perfect. What a disappointment.]

『It’s not a disappointment! You can praise me more, come on, come on.』

The useless Goddess grinned and briefly lifted the hem of her elegant white dress. It almost revealed something, but just barely. Damn, my eyes were being guided… so frustrating!

『Hahaha, it’s working! Wow, all that trouble tweaking of the parameters was worth it!』

The old me would have ignored her and punched her in the stomach, but for some reason, I can’t bring myself to do that. Is this what it means to be teased?

[This is a nightmare.]

『You’re still saying that!?』

[Enough with the nonsense. What do you want?]

『Let’s just enjoy our conversation a little more. We could even do a naked shove, if you like.』

[I’ll politely decline. It’s kind of scary.]

I can’t help but feel that if I open my heart to this guy and let myself get lost, I’ll never be able to escape. The thought of stepping into a bottomless abyss is too terrifying.

『Hmm, that sounds interesting in its own way, doesn’t it? You don’t mind drowning inside me forever, right?』

The silver-haired Evil Goddess rubbed against me. I caught a faint girlish scent and my reaction to the sensation almost hit me. This guy’s dangerous after all.

[That’ll be a shame.]

『That’s unfortunate. Well, I didn’t want it to happen, either.』

I mustered all my willpower and glared at her, but the bad Goddess surprisingly let go of me.

『Well, I don’t have anything special to do today. I just came out because I thought you might throw me away if we didn’t hang out like this every once in a while.』

[If I was going to throw you away, I would have done it a long time ago.]

『Haha, see ya.』

My real body melted into a white world, dissolving into particles of light as if dissolving into the air. I woke up.

====================

[This is the Great Sealed Door.]

[It’s smaller than I imagined.]

The next morning, we woke up without having any nightmares and arrived at our destination. It was about three hours’ travel through a rocky mountain from the Nightmare’s Claw Mark. Following Elmina-san’s guidance, we went around the southern side of the rocky mountain, and came across a door made of a white, ceramic-like material, the same one I’d seen in the white abandoned city some time ago.  

The door was about three meters long and three meters wide, and had no handle. Or rather, was it even a door? A complex geometric pattern was carved into the white door-like structure, but it was difficult to imagine how it would open.  

There were several rusty pieces of iron lying in front of the door, likely the remains of tools sacrificed in attempts to pry it open.

[What are you going to do with this? Are you going to pry it open?]

[I once shot a mithril arrow imbued with wind magic with all my might, and it didn’t even leave a scratch.]

[Hmm, wait a moment.]

I patted my hands around the door-like object, checking for any sort of unlocking mechanism. All I could think of was a slot for passing a card or something, or some kind of input device.

[I’m at a loss.]

I couldn’t find anything like that anywhere. And I wasn’t even sure if this object was a door.

『This is definitely a door. It’s the anti-God shelter’s blast door. Wait a moment, I’ll unlock it now. Keep your hand on the door.』

Rheal said, so I held my hand against the door, and suddenly, a geometric pattern carved into the door began to emit a green light. Soon, a clanging sound rang out, and the white door slid open, like a puzzle had been solved.

『There’s no vibration from a pseudo-Divine being, but it seems to be powered by something, so there might be information inside. At first glance, it looks like a civilian shelter, so I can’t expect much, though.』

[No, no, that’s enough.]

I blurted out my response to the useless Goddess without thinking. Turning around, I saw both Elmina-san and Rifana, their mouths hanging open in shock.

[H-how did you do that?]

[It’s like the Goddess inside my head opened it for me.]

[Y-you see… I was skeptical, but it’s true.]

Anyway, the door was open, so I decided to explore inside.  

The interior of the shelter appeared to be made of the same white, ceramic-like material as the door. It’s unclear how much time had passed, but not a speck of dust had accumulated. It must have some kind of air conditioning.  

The ceiling wasn’t very high, maybe about two and a half meters? It was just barely out of my reach, so I guessed it was about that high. Light sources were installed at regular intervals, making the interior quite bright. The white light, like LED lighting, reflected off the white, ceramic-like material on the walls and floor, making it a little blinding.  

I took the lead and continued on, cautiously keeping an eye on my surroundings. The only thing that caught my attention was our presence; no sign of any living creatures. After walking a little further and turning a corner, I saw what looked like a door again. This door was an automatic sliding door, like those often seen in science fiction. Just approaching it made a clicking noise and it slid open.  

Surprised by the sound, Elmina-san and Rifana were about to draw the large knives they had been holding, but when they realized it was just the door opening, they both sighed deeply.

[That was a surprise.]

[It moved so suddenly.]

From there, the exploration went smoothly. There were no particularly troublesome security measures, and not a single living thing in sight.

[Is this… a frozen, dried-up corpse?]

[It seems so. Maybe it was a cryosleep capsule or something.]

[Cryosleep capsule?]

[The device can emulate something like a bear in long hibernation, I guess?]

[I see.]

Rifana seemed satisfied with my brief answer. My presence detection didn’t react to the body at all, so it must be completely dead. There were various tools nearby, but they all seemed to have deteriorated over time and were no longer usable. Even if they still worked, many of them still looked useless. All I found were tablets, laptops, and smartphones. Any organic matter seemed to have decayed to dust.  

During the exploration, I found a map of the shelter, so I decided to follow it to another room.

[There are so many things I don’t understand.]

[I wonder what this is?]

[Who knows.]

At first glance, all I could tell were a few magic crystals, what appeared to be some kind of metal ingot, some kind of cable of unknown material, and pipes, bolts, and nuts that looked like they might be used to repair the shelter. There were also some tool-like items, but I had no idea how to use them.  

Also hanging on the wall were several spacesuit-like costumes. They looked like they’d be quite difficult to move in.

[Shall I take the magic crystals, the mysterious ingots, and the cables? The pipes, bolts, and nuts also seem useful, so I’ll take them.]

Magic crystals are processed from magic cores and act like batteries that store magic power. They can be used to power magic tools, making them quite versatile. If you charge it with magic power beforehand, it can also be used as an external magic battery when casting spells.

[I wonder if this is enough here?]

[That’s right. Shall we check out this other room next?]

Looking at the map, there’s a symbol resembling a knife and fork, so I think it’s probably a dining hall or food storehouse.  

I don’t know how long it has been, but it’s definitely been thousands of years. I can’t expect to get anything, but it might be worth a visit. After all, time-space vaults seem to be commonplace, so whatever is stored inside might actually be safe.  

When I arrived in front of the room, I was surprised to find that it was protected by a door that seemed much sturdier than the previous warehouse-like room.

[This door looks quite impressive.]

[Does this open?]

[Let’s try opening it.]

For some reason, I can’t find the inside of this room using my sensory senses. Is it under some kind of special magic? There was something next to the door that looked like a control panel, so I fiddled with it and opened it. It only had two buttons, so it was easy.  

The heavy door slid open with a whoosh, like air was escaping.

[Oh, there are cans lined up neatly.]

It seemed to be a food storage room.

[Cans? What are these? Are they really food?]

[Maybe. Let me take a few out.]

I took out two of the cans neatly arranged on the shelf, each in its own package, and left the room. As soon as I did, the door automatically closed and locked. It seemed like they had measures in place to prevent the door from being left open.  

The can-like objects I brought were mostly plain, with only one or two lines of unreadable text printed on them. I was sure the writing was the name of the food inside.  

I took out two of each of four types: a large, slightly heavy cream-colored can; a light, light brown can; a yellow can; and a plain, white, long, thin can. Each one had what appeared to be a pull tab, so it looked like they could be opened without any special tools.

[Let’s start with this cream-colored one… no, let’s open this light brown one.]

None of the cans were strangely bloated or rusty, so the contents were probably fine. I can’t guarantee the taste, though.  

The light brown can was opened with a cracking sound. A faintly sweet scent wafted through the air. Looking inside, I saw a pile of round cracker-like objects. I slowly took one out and put it in my mouth.

[Hey!?]

[Taichi-kun!?]

I chewed and swallowed it. Yes, this is a cracker. Or maybe a biscuit? It didn’t feel damp, and it was just plain delicious.

[A biscuit, huh? This is just plain delicious.]

I took a biscuit out of the can and offered it to Rifana, who timidly accepted it and put it in her mouth. It was kind of cute to see her holding it in both hands and munching on it.

[Huh, it doesn’t taste strange, does it? It’s, delicious? Maybe?]

[I’ll pass. It’d be dangerous if we all ate it and got sick.]

Elmina-san took a step back and gave a wry smile.

[You’re right. Let’s move on to the next one.]

I opened the cans one by one. The cream-colored can contained a white stew-like dish with vegetables and what appeared to be chicken, while the yellow can contained a yellow peach-like fruit preserved in syrup. The long, plain white can seemed to be something like an oral rehydration solution. It tasted very similar to the sports drinks I often drank in my original world.

[This fruit preserved in syrup is quite tasty.]

[The stew is a bit greasy, though. I’ll take it all for now. As long as it doesn’t make me sick, I won’t have any food problems.]

[Okay, but if you get sick, who cares?]

I opened the pantry again and put all the cans and boxes inside into the treasure box. I’ll leave the detailed inspection for later.  

The rest were just a few small living spaces and a toilet, so I didn’t find much. And finally, there was a door that was locked with an unusually tight lock. It had a gun-like marking on it, so I thought it might be an armory.

[It won’t open.]

[Let me ask the thing in my head.]

So, hey! Open up.

『It’s fine, but I don’t think there’s anything special here. It looks like a private family shelter. Can you touch the door for now?』

Just like when I first opened the shelter’s door, I touched the closed door and waited a moment, and heard the sound of the door unlocking.  

Nice, good girl.

『You can praise me more often, you know?』

Mentally saying my praise to Rheal, I opened the unlocked door.

[What is this?]

[Probably a weapon.]

[This?]

Arranged neatly on the shelf were probably some kind of weapon, similar to a gun. If their bodies are built the same as us, their weapons will also be similar in shape. There were two types of weapons: four pistol-like weapons and four rifle-like weapons. All I could find were the guns themselves, no bullets to be seen. That meant they probably weren’t weapons that fired solid projectiles.  

I collected everything and put it in a treasure box.

[Aren’t we going to try them out?]

[If we’re going to test them, we’d better find a larger area. It’d be terrible if something exploded.]

[That’s true. We’ve explored the entire building now, right? Let’s get out.]

At Elmina-san’s urging, I left the shelter. I made sure to securely close the entrance, as it might serve as a hideout in case of an emergency.

=====================

What I found during this shelter exploration was a large amount of canned food, some materials of unknown use, four pistol-like weapons, and four long rifle-like weapons. I laid out my loot on the ground and inspected it.

[There seem to be 360 cans of each type, including the opened ones.]

[There were four cryosleep pods and four weapons, so that means each person gets 90 cans of each. If they consumed one can per day, that would be enough for 90 days.]

[That little bit of water won’t last a day.]

[Maybe there was a separate water purification facility. Or maybe they assumed they’d replenish it with magic?]

There might have been tools for making water in the room that looked like a supplies storehouse.

[In conclusion, this facility was probably some kind of shelter for four people.]

As I said this, I picked up the pistol-shaped weapon and began fiddling with two of them.  

The shape itself was simple. It was made of something like white ceramic, likely the same material as the structural material of the shelter they’d been hiding in earlier. Isn’t it a bit heavy for a pistol? There was no magazine of any kind, and it had few moving parts. It didn’t even seem designed to be disassembled for maintenance. How good is it as a weapon? Is it maintenance-free?  

Two safeties seem to prevent accidental discharge: a grip safety that is released by gripping the gun tightly, and a manual safety located within reach of your thumb. I released both safeties, aimed at the tree in front of me, and pulled the trigger.

With a sharp “whoosh!”, a pale blue bullet of light fires from the muzzle, punching a fist-sized hole in the trunk of the tree I was aiming at. There’s very little recoil. I pulled the trigger repeatedly until I could no longer fire after about 30 shots. Looking more closely, I see a circular indicator on the rear of the gun, where the hammer would be on a pistol in my world, gradually restoring its gauge. It seems to indicate the number of bullets remaining. I wonder what powers it?

[It’s got some impressive power, doesn’t it?]

Three of the trees I was aiming at had been knocked down by the massive amount of light bullets. I wait for the indicator on the pistol to recover and begin firing again. Yeah, I think I could fire about 40 shots in a row as long as I don’t fire at an insanely fast rate. It’s probably not something you’d fire so indiscriminately, and it should be more than adequate for self-defense against minor monsters or other people.

[Well, magic is sometimes superior in both power and ease of use, but overall, it’s a good weapon.]

Next, I sprayed light bullets from the dual pistols. This is quite fun.  

I taught Elmina-san and Rifana how to use them and have them actually fire them. I made sure to thoroughly instill in them the bare minimum rules: don’t point the gun at teammates, don’t look down the barrel, and don’t put your finger on the trigger unless you’re going to fire.

[It’ll be fine. You’re used to using bows and arrows and magic.]

[That’s true, I suppose. But try not to get complacent.]

[I know. But you’ve figured out how to use it well, don’t you?]

[There was a similar weapon in my original world.]

As the two begin pistol practice, I pick up a long-gun-like weapon. It’s basically the same way, but it’s more powerful and has multiple firing modes to choose from.  

It can be switched between rifle mode, which allows you to choose between single shot, triple burst shot, and rapid fire; sniper mode, which has a longer range and higher power but is less effective at rapid fire; and shotgun mode, which has an extremely shorter range but fires multiple light bullets simultaneously. I was amazed that the barrel length changes length and length when transformed into each mode. A transformable rifle is just too romantic.  

However, considering that it’s equipped with a system that seems prone to wear and tear, I’m unsure how it’s maintained. Is it really maintenance-free?

[That one… seems strong, too.]

[Well, it’s powerful enough to deal with normal monsters. But it might be a bit difficult to use against the likes of Behemoths, don’t you think?]

[Well, in terms of single-hit power, an arrow imbued with wind magic would probably be better. But this one might be easier to use than a bow, since you only have to aim and fire.]

[It might be okay to use it as a talisman, though.]

It’s just not satisfying to me at all. It would be an effective weapon against ordinary monsters, but it’s far too weak against a god. This peashooter wouldn’t even scratch them. If it were ten times more powerful, it might be useful as a deterrent.  

After all, those guys are fine even when hit directly by a super explosion or a close-range magical explosion.  

After completing our inspection, we camped in front of the closed large door and prepared for the next day’s journey.  

By the way, Rifana and I didn’t get sick. As a result, from the next day onwards, we would be eating canned food for our meals.

++++

# Someday Will I Be The Greatest Alchemist? - 616 - Light Sword 5

The next morning, I woke up feeling great. I washed my face and brushed my teeth, then when I went to the dining room, Maribelle promptly served my breakfast.

Sophia, Maria, Marnie, Laeva, Akane, Lulu-chan, and Kaede gathered in the dining room. We normally eat together with our employees, but Charlotte and the others were taking a little longer.

「You were confined to your smithy the entire day yesterday, weren’t you?」  

「Yup, you were so into it that you forgot about the time.」  

「Please make sure to take proper meals.」  

「Gotcha.」

It seems I’ve worried Sophia and the others. I should keep that in mind.

「So how is it going?」  

「I still haven’t enchanted it, but one sword is complete.」  

「Oh, I would love to see it.」  

「I asked Golan-san and Doganbo-san to do its fittings, so it’s not with me right now.」  

「Is that so? Then I will pay Golan-san a visit at his workshop.」

Laeva showed interest in the sword, so it seems she would make the trip to Golan-san’s house.

I quickly finished my meal and headed to the smithy.

Gnome hadn’t arrived yet. Salamander said he was coming in the evening. Since Doganbo-san and Golan-san were busy in their own workshop making the fittings, I was alone in the smithy right now.

Continuing my work from yesterday, I wouldn’t use the magic furnace. I lined up the three types of orichalcum alloy ingots on the workbench, then brought out mana potions that I could drink at any time.

And in front of the ingots, I visualized the single-edged sword I was about to forge.

The image I had in mind was a sword that had the same parts as a kabutowari, a type of jitte[[1]](https://www.euricette.com/greatest-alchemist-chapter-616/#GA-G1).  

The Kabutowari has no edge to kill with, but it is extremely thick. It wasn’t as short as an armor piercer, but because it was shaped more as a sword than a kabutowari[[2]](https://www.euricette.com/greatest-alchemist-chapter-616/#GA-G2), it may as well be called an armor piercer.

I solidified the image in my mind and shaped the ingot.  

Combining the core steel, skin steel, and edge steel, I used Smithing magic and Synthesis to turn it into the shape of a thick sword with a wide body.

I took breaks to recover my magic power using mana potions and continue with the process.

Midway through, Sophia, Maria, and Marnie brought my lunch.  

The reason why the three of them came was because they had brought Etoile, Haruka, and Flora with them.  

As could be expected from having been holed up in my smithy for a while, I missed seeing my children. I couldn’t be happier.

Now then, the shape was nearly complete. As with the armor piercer, the tang was made longer.  

I designed this with the hope that it wouldn’t lose in toughness against swords, but even though this form prioritizes sturdiness over sharpness, it’s a sword made of orichalcum alloy, also known as god steel. I’d be glad if its sharpness was out of the ordinary too.

I adjusted the shape using Smithing magic, and by the time I finished the rough polish, Gnome and Salamander arrived at the smithy.

「Ou! We’re right on time.」  

「Fumu, that’s quite the interesting sword. Shall we start with the tempering right away?」

Before I knew it, the sun had already set and darkness descended.  

Since appearances matter, I used the same type of clay to draw another blade pattern to match the previous sword .

「Then, if you would.」  

「Ou, then I’ll heat it up.」

Once the clay had dried, I asked Salamander to heat up the second blade.

Salamander began heating up the thick sword blade.  

Gnome watched intently, as if it ascertain the color of the blade.

「Now!」

Kshhhhh!!

I dunked the blade into Spirit Spring water and steam rose.

I pulled it out of the water and inspected it.

Then I silently showed it to Gnome and Salamander.

「Umu, it’s well made.」  

「Ou, it is worthy of the assistance we have provided.」  

「Thank you. It would have been a lot harder without you guys.」  

「What, you would have been fine by yourself too if you had enough time.」  

「Indeed. It might be challenging with this magic furnace, but you could have probably made your own.」

After checking to make sure there was no warping on the blade after the quenching then sharpening it with Smithing magic, a sword of the same tinge as the one I had left in the care of Doganbo-san and Golan-san became apparent.

Even though it should have a rugged feeling because of its function as an armor piercer or helmet breaker, it felt refined and beautiful, likely because of the god steel.

「What are you going to do with its fittings? Leave it to Doganbo and Golan?」  

「No, I will make it. I plan for this to be on my waist at all times for self defense. I don’t want it to stand out too much.」  

「Then all that’s left is what to enchant it with.」  

「Yeah, that’s the thing. ……I’ll have to think carefully about that.」  

「Umu, that’s fine.」  

「Well then, we will head back.」  

「Yeah, thanks, you two.」

Gnome and Salamander vanished from my workshop. I stood in front of the complete, still bare blade, wondering what enchantments I should apply to it.

Well, whatever it may be is a matter for tomorrow. I’m tired today, so I’ll go take a bath and sleep.

+++

# 617 - Completion

Since the morning after, I’ve been making the fittings for the sword while thinking about what to enchant it with.

I made the tang long, so if the blade is 40cm long, the hilt is also long.

I used Elder Treant for the hilt, dragon leather to coil around it, and then I twisted together string processed from mithril as well as with strong threads that I asked Kaede to produce and then coiled them on the hilt.

Both the wood and string on the hilt had high magic power conductivity, and they were strong and durable too.

The scabbard was synthesized using the ribs and membrane of dragon species. I tried to not decorate it, so an observant person might notice that the materials were expensive, but at a glance, it looks nothing out of the ordinary.

Even though I had completely assembled this sword, I had spent the entire day thinking about what to enchant the two swords until it had gotten dark.

Just past noon the next day, Doganbo-san and Golan-san finished crafting the fittings of the sword a day early and had brought it to me.

「That was quick.」  

「Ou, we were so excited we worked harder than we should have at our age.」  

「Doganbo, first thing’s first, show it to Takumi.」  

「Ohh, you’re right.」  

「Then let’s head to the workshop.」

Since there was also a matter of enchantments, we headed to the workshop.  

Since we’re only doing enchantments today, it wasn’t the smithy that we headed to, but rather the workshop where Laeva and I always go to.

When we arrived at the workshop, I received the cloth-wrapped sword from Doganbo-san.

「Oooh…… it’s like, maybe it’s because of my lacking vocabulary, I can’t say anything except it’s amazing.」

The sword that was unveiled from the cloth was simply beautiful.

The white scabbard was adorned with silver decorations, and toned down colors of white and silver emanated elegance.  

The white base was likely dragon fangs or bones. Delicate engravings carved its surface.  

The silver on the hemming and pommel were likely mithril alloy. It was a beautiful and elegant color characteristic of that material.

A magic crystal was embedded into the pommel, likely to enhance magic power.

The guard was sculped intricately too, and I could tell it was also mithril alloy based on its color.

「Amazing! Golan-san! Doganbo-san! You’ve made something too beautiful that I’m unworthy of it!」  

「Considering the quality of the sword that you forged, it needed to be of this quality at the very least.」  

「Mhmm, I’m glad you like it. We had fun making it too.」

It seems it was also a satisfying creation to Doganbo-san and Golan-san, and they looked happy at my reaction.

「Okay, then I’ll enchant it.」  

「「Ou!」」

Since it seemed like they wanted to observe it to the end, I was going to finish bestowing the enchantments on the swords.

I unsheathed both swords and arranged them on my workbench.

I’ll prepare the catalysts and enchant the spells one by one.  

For the long sword, I applied the Light attribute and the same Lightning attribute as was in Tsukiyomi. Then I enhanced the swords abilities.

As for the shorter sword, I bestowed the Fire attribute to it in addition to Light attribute.

After that, I enchanted 『Physical Attack Resistance』 on both the scabbard and hilt.  

Given how both the scabbard and the hilt had top quality materials, they were much sturdier weapons compared to swords sold in stores. but I still applied 『Physical Attack Resistance』 and 『Self Repair』as a precautionary measure.

・Holy Sword Vajra

『Self Repair』 『Light Attribute』 『Lightning Attribute』 『Enhanced Slash』 『Enhanced Durability』 『Dark Resist』『Lightning Resist』

Named『Vajra』 after the Ancient Indian Wisdom King Vajrayaska, who possessed the holy power to pierce through all obstacles.

・Holy Sword Fudou

『Self Repair』『Light Attribute』『Fire Attribute』『Enhanced Slash』『Enhanced Durability』『Physical Attack Resist』『Dark Resist』『Fire Resist』

Considered to be an incarnation of the Vairocana, it embodies the Garuda Flames that purges impurities, its name was『Fudou』.

Holy Sword Vajra emits purifying lightning when infused with a large amount of magic power.

Holy Sword Fudou generates a purifying flame when infused with a large amount of magic power.

「I name them Holy Sword Vajra and Fudou.」  

「……mm, I’m speechless.」  

「……yeah, I’m glad I was a part of such an amazing piece.」

Doganbo-san and Golan-san took turns holding the Holy Sword Vajra and Holy Sword Fudou, inspecting them as if they were ingraining it into their memory.

「Thanks, Takumi. I’m drinking good tonight.」  

「Ou, Golan-aniki, let’s take out the ones we’ve been saving.」  

「Umu, let’s have a banquet.」

Surprisingly, Doganbo-san and Golan-san said they wanted to borrow Vajra and Fudou. They planned to display them on an altar and have a feast with the Dwarves.

「These are national treasures made from god metal. To Dwarves, it holds special meaning. We’ll return it tomorrow, so do you mind?」  

「Not at all. Doganbo-san and Golan-san, you both helped, so it’s fine if it’s until tomorrow.  

「Umu, don’t worry, they won’t get even a single scratch on them.」

Golan-san and Doganbo-san carefully wrapped Vajra and Fudou in cloth, then left triumphantly.

Dwarves love finding any reason to drink alcohol.

Well, I’ll take my time to think of ideas for other equipment.

+++

# 618 - Romance Weapons

It’s great that the Holy Sword Vajra and Holy Sword Fudou were complete, but since I’ve always used swords as well as the spear as my main weapons, I thought about making something a bit different.

The spear I mainly used was the Ice Bringer.  

As for swords, I had the Demon Sword Tsukiyomi, Holy Sword Vajra, and Holy Sword Fudou, three in total.

I have enough swords and spears.

That’s why I thought I’d play around a bit.

Yes, I was supposed to do it for a little bit, but……

Looking at the weapons before her eyes, Sophia tilted her head. Marnie wondered if they were for farm work. Akane seemed to have some understanding though.

「Umm, is that a scythe?」  

「…………」  

「This isn’t for harvesting, is it?」  

「Ha, haha, I guess it doesn’t come across as the grim reaper’s scythe?」  

「Who would even use a Death Scythe? Wouldn’t a normal spear be easier to use?」

Sounds about right. The Death Scythe was a romance weapon, but it was heavy, had poor balance, and it was difficult to handle, so there was no one who raised their hand wanting to use it.

「This isn’t for us.」  

「Perhaps it would work if it was Titan.」

I pulled myself together and the next thing I showed them was a gauntlet integrated with a Pile Bunker.  

Sophia and Maria immediately shook their heads and said that could also be used by Titan.

「As I thought, Titan, huh?」  

「Since one wouldn’t want to lose balance from the recoil from bunking the pile in, I believe only Titan could use it.」

With exception to Titan, our entire party’s fighting style focused on evasion. Even Sophia, who had a shield, used it to parry attacks in the flow of battle.

「It definitely has strong recoil.」  

「Yes. The recoil after the stake hit the enemy is immense.」

The mechanism for driving the pile in was by detonating it using magic. There was no recoil at the moment of activating the weapon, but the moment it hit the enemy, the recoil was insane. It’s a pile, after all.

In the end, we decided that the Pile Bunker would be rebuilt for Titan’s use.

I don’t know if Titan would be pleased to use it though.

「Next is…… is this a weapon?」  

「A gigantic tool?」  

「Umm, there’s no such thing as a wrench mace, right?」

Yup, it has really bad balance.  

I guess I shouldn’t have used a certain robot anime, after all.

A giant wrench with a lever by the grip to move the wrench.

「Yotto, it’s heavy, but it’s not to the point of being unusable nya.」

Lulu-chan swung it around, but as expected, it had horrible balance.

「Is this a metal whip?」  

「It’s a chain whip. I also tried making a chain mace.」

The thin metal rods were conjoined, and a weighted tip was attacked to increase the striking force or in some cases, a dart.

「This is…… difficult to handle, but it’s useable.」  

「Indeed. It requires much practice, but it will likely help improve our skills.」

Sophia tested out the chain whip, and Maria tried out the chain mace which was easier to handle.

It’s extremely terrifying how well the whip-like weapons suited Sophia.

「Like the chain mace, I also made a tri-segment staff.」  

「Ah, I can imagine how to use this more easily.」

I handed the Tri-Segment Staff to Maria who was trying out the chain mace.  

Upon accepting the Tri-Segment Staff, Maria began swinging it around and practiced to try to get used to it.

Perhaps thanks to her Taijutsu Skill, or perhaps affected by her Spear Handling Skill, Maria could freely manipulate the Tri-Segment Staff.

For a while, Sophia and Maria practiced their weapons of choice, then they returned it looking satisfied.

「Perhaps I will focus on mastering this chain whip.」  

「I will try something else because this overlaps with my spear.」

Sophia seemed to like the chain whip. She already had it coiled up and hanging on her hip.  

Maria wanted to try a different weapon because it was too similar to her spear.

「Is that a dagger attached to a rope?」  

「Yeah, it’s a rope dart. That rope was mithril alloy processed into fibers, which was weaved together with Kaede’s threads to make it, so it can’t be cut so simply.」

Marnie showed interest in the Rope Dart.

This weapon has a dart-shaped spearhead attached to a long rope and was hard to handle, with Marnie’s high skill level and proficiency with daggers, it could serve as a weapon against mid-range enemies.

「May I use it?」  

「Of course, I made these for everyone to use.」

Marnie took the rope dart and went off to practice.

Both Sophia’s chain whip and Marnie’s rope dart needed ample space for practice.

「I’ll have to think of another weapon that doesn’t overlap with the spear for Maria.」  

「Thank you very much. I’m excited to see what you’ll do.」

Now then, I have to think of something for Maria and the expectant Lulu-chan.

Incidentally, Akane was practicing to use an iron fan for self defense.  

Of course, the ribbed fan wasn’t made of iron but rather cloth woven from mithril alloy and Kaede’s durable silk.

And Laeva said she was making her own weapon.  

I completely understand how she feels as a craftsman myself, so I didn’t say anything. I’ll be here if she ever wants a consultation, though.

+++

# 619 - The Start of Winter and Interviews

Even the Sanctuary has four seasons.

Winter was not especially unforgiving, and neither was summer excessively hot.

Having a space heater in winter would be nice, but some people could get by with thicker clothing.  

Summer could be hot, but it wasn’t the sweltering, humid heat, so it was comfortable in the shade.

Now then, what I wanted to say was that days have passed since the harvest festival and the temperature in the Sanctuary has finally started dropping.

Was it just me or did autumn feel short?

Snow rarely ever piles up in the Sanctuary. I’ve only spent a few years here, so while I can’t be absolutely certain, you can’t freeze to death as long as you have a house and clothing.

Beastkin were especially resilient to the cold.

Marnie and Lulu-chan who weren’t covered in fur like the Cat Siths were just as resistant to it. I suppose this is just how it is.

I had provided heating magic tools to the humans Vanga-san, Martha-san, and anyone else who requested it.

I was sitting on the one-seater in front of the fireplace at home while reading a picture book to Flora who was on my lap.

It was still a bit too early for Etoile and Haruka, but because Flora was a beastkin baby, her growth was much faster.

I was told that in 5-6 years, the speed of her growth would be no different to that of Humans and Elves. Or more accurately, human and elves catch up.

Even so, Flora was still unable to speak, so she was just happy looking at the pictures.

Then Maribelle came with a tray for tea.

「Master, please have some tea.」  

「Ahh, thanks, Maribelle.」

After Maribelle left, Sebastian came over.

「Master, there was a correspondence by way of the Capital workshop. Lord Portfort wishes to schedule the interviews for the civil servant positions.」  

「Ah, we’re finally in the interview phase, I see.」  

「Well, competent people are wanted everywhere.」  

「I suppose. I know very well just how important civil servants are.」

Sebastian’s task was concerning the civil servant matter I had requested of Lord Simon.

「The Great Spirits and I are okay to go at any time, so we’re fine matching Lord Simon’s schedule.」  

「In that case, I shall coordinate with Lord Portfort on your behalf.」  

「Thanks.」

I entrusted Sebastian with scheduling the civil servant interviews.  

He has a knack for negotiating with nobles.

Around 10 days later, the civil servant interviews were held in a room in our Wedgefort base.

「Hmm, could it be that there are not that many exemplary people?」  

「My, Madam Rosary, these are the talents that Lord Porfort had selected though?」  

「Though he may be my husband, it would not do us well if we are lenient on them during the interviews.」  

「Hey hey, what do you think of this child? He seems excellent for his age, and while he has commoner origins, that should not be an issue.」  

「…………」

The Gate that teleports directly towards the Wedgefort base was more or less confidential.  

Three people gathered to look at the files with the information of the interview candidates and stated their opinions. How did it come to this? Madam Rosary, Madam Elizabeth, and Madam Lumia became the interviewers.

Of course, regarding the Teleport Gate, it was confidential for reasons of national defense, so I’ve decided that it would be a matter of utmost secrecy to children and parents.

It doesn’t take much time for Tsubaki to pull her carriage if it’s to Wedgefort, but we had to use a carriage despite having a Gate.

「Well, isn’t that fine? Someone with plenty of life experience could be of help to Takumi.」  

「Certainly, that could be the case.」

Undine seemed like she wasn’t the worried in the slightest.  

In the first place, living in the Sanctuary meant that they weren’t the kind of people who would cause harm to it.

As it turned out, Lord Simon had arrived with the civil servant candidates. Lord Simon was guided into the room.

「Iruma-dono, I apologize for keeping you waiting…… why is Rosary……」  

「My, I’m relieved to see you well, dear husband.」

Lord Simon was surprised to see that Lady Rosary was in the interviewer’s seat.

「……eh, Madam Elizabeth is beside you? And on the opposite side is Queen Lumia!?」  

「How do you do, Lord Portfort?」  

「Lord Portfort, please do not address me as the Queen. I am but a civil servant of the Sanctuary.」  

「A-a civil servant……」

Lord Simon was at a complete loss of words. Yup, it couldn’t be helped.

「I’m sorry, Lord Simon. We must proceed with the interviews today in this manner.」  

「Ah, yes, indeed. The civil servant interviews take precedence.」

Lord Simon instructed the candidates enter the room one by one, and the civil servant interviews began.

+++

# 620 - Interviews Begin

「Well then, the first person, please come in.」

The person I called in was clearly in his late fifties.

When I glanced at Lord Simon, he turned his head away.

Hmm, I do think that a person with plenty of life experiences is valuable, but in Japan, he would soon be in retirement.

Madam Rosary sent an icy glare towards Lord Simon. I could see sweat rolling down Lord Simon’s brow.

「L-let’s start with your name…………」

I guess we have no choice but to start the interview.

「My name is Lucifuges. I have worked as a civil official for a lengthy time.」  

「……I see, is that so?」

When my gaze fell onto the document, he definitely has had a long career as an civil servant.
