However, we wanted a younger candidate who could work actively and were still early in management.

Madam Rosary tapped on one section of the paper I was reading and urged me to read on.

(A habitual perpetrator of sexual harassment, workplace harassment, and was let go after being caught in a bribery scandal.)

Despite how impressed I was by how well they conducted their investigation, I turned towards Lord Simon questioning why he would bring them in for the interviews with my gaze, and he put his hands together in an apologetic gesture.

I take it that even Lord Simon must have reasons why he couldn’t refuse.  

Well, there’s no way a man like this would ever be accepted by the Great Spirits, so it must have been easy to bring them with him.

When I later asked Lord Simon, he explained that there were several people that he could not refuse because of their connections.  

Lord Simon was also aware that these people wouldn’t pass the Great Spirit’s check, so even though they would waste travel supplies, he still brought them along.

Well, that’s what I thought, anyway.

Others like this man were also here.

「My name is Torgny von Taragne. Third son of the Taragne Barony.」  

「……mm, I see.」

My eyes fell onto the document. As it was likely that the third son would not inherit the household, he tried to establish himself as a civil official.

In reality, he was far too prideful and lacked cooperation, and despite not being particularly outstanding, he blamed others for his shortcomings.

He had apparently caused trouble for those at his workplaces, often changing jobs.

Yeah, rejected.

「My name is Tomas[1]! The second son of a merchant family. I am unskilled with the sword and magic, but calculations are my specialty! Pleased to meet you!」  

「Tomas-san, how old are you?」  

「Yes! I am turning 16 this year!」

The lively, baby-faced, bespectacled boy said he was 15 years old.  

Since the age of adulthood in this world is 15 years old, so I guess he’s like a fresh graduate from this spring on a job hunt?

When I glanced at Undine, she nodded, so he must be okay.

My eyes fell onto the document again.  

It was clear that he would not inherit the family business as the second son of the small merchant in the Capital, so he apparently took the civil servant exam for the Royal Castle.

According to the information from Lord Simon, he had excellent grades, but as to be expected, you need connections to become a civil servant.  

Sons and daughters of influential nobles took precedence, then the sons and daughters of lesser nobles, then sons of wealthy merchants, and finally, commoners like him.  

Lord Simon also thought it to be ridiculous, but there were various obstacles that he could not disregard.

Madam Rosary, Madam Elizabeth, and Madam Lumia also had a good impression of him.

For the time being, I drew a circle on his name as a passing mark.

I thought the interviews were going well at the start, but there were many talented individuals by the end.

According to Lord Simon, those that I wouldn’t accept would be assigned to cities Wedgefort or Valor.  

Jobs were aplenty in both Wedgefort and Valor, after all.

Now Madam Rosary, Madam Elizabeth, and Madam Lumia were going to discuss who to recruit.

「This Tomas boy would be a safe hire.」  

「Indeed. And this Maple kid also seems diligent.」  

「Yes. These two are young and earnest, they gave impressions. Ah, and this Priscilla girl also looks promising.」  

「Madam Lumia, Priscilla is no child. She is a fine lady.」

I also had no objections to hiring Tomas. Maple is a girl of the same age as Tomas and is just as diligent, her parents were knights, and it is normal for daughters who were neither the eldest daughter nor of noble birth to lead independent lives.  

The last name that Madam Lumia brought up, Priscilla, had opened a store with her husband, but her husband died of an illness, so she liquidated her store in the Royal Capital and applied to become a civil servant in the Sanctuary for a fresh start.

The three names mentioned were those that I had marked with a circle, so I was impressed by their varying life experiences.

In the end, we made a tentative offer of acceptance to five people, then tomorrow, after we explain the terms of employment to them again, we’ll hire them officially.

Apparently, the people that the Madams and I decided to hire were also those that Lord Simon recommended.

It might be a good idea to leave matters of employment to Madam Rosary, Madam Elizabeth and Madam Lumia from here on.

+++

# 621 - A Day In Winter

The civil servant exams held in Wedgefort ended smoothly, and the new recruits’ moving process has finished.

The new recruits immediately began working in the government building alongside Madam Rosary, Madam Elizabeth, and Madam Lumia.

They also seemed very happy with their employment conditions.

I was busy making various things in the workshop.

「『Transmute』!」

Light enveloped the wood and bamboo materials, turning into a round steaming basket.

「This many steaming baskets should be enough.」

As for why I was making a large quantity of steaming baskets was because I thought winter meant mochi.

Ever since I was a kid, we had mochi before the new year every year.

It was also rare since we used firewood to steam the glutenous rice.

And so, I accidentally let it slip that I suddenly felt like eating mochi.

「When winter comes, it really makes you want mochi, huh?」  

「Ahh, mochiiii. That’s nice. Now I want sweet bean mochi.」

My innocent mumbling in the living room made Akane nod nostalgically.

However, when the rest of our members heard this, they reacted differently.

「Mochi nya?」  

「Mumu, I’m getting a feeling that it’s something tasty.」

Beastkin ears are amazing. Lulu-chan and Laeva did not fail to hear the conversation between Akane and I.

「Akane-sama, is mochi something delicious nya?」  

「Takumi-sama, what kind of food is it?」  

「What color nya?」  

「Is it a snack? Or could it be some dessert?」

Surprisingly, the two bombarded Akane and I with questions and we were taken aback by their enthusiasm.

「Hey, hey…… calm down you two.」  

「Really, wouldn’t it be faster to just make it? If we ask Dryas, we might be able to produce glutinous sticky rice.」  

「Oneechan was called~!」  

「Uwah! You scared me! Don’t show up all of a sudden like that!」

The moment Dryas’ name was mentioned, she appeared out of nowhere.

「Perfect timing. Dryas, do you know of any glutenous rice?」  

「Of course, I know~ But it’s not grown in the Sanctuary~」  

「Ahh, about that, we want a large amount of it, can you do it?」  

「It’s Takumi-chan asking~ Leave it to this oneechan~」

Since it looks like we’ll get a supply of glutenous rice, it’s been decided that we’ll be pounding mochi soon.

It would be impossible to have everyone in the Sanctuary participate, but we need enough to be able to share a bit with everyone.

Perhaps we could have the Catkin siblings, Cat Sith sisters Miri and Lala, Human sisters Colette and Shirona, Elven family Melty-san, Melanie, and Malorie, Vanga-san, Martha-san, and the Dwarves Doganbo-san and Golan-san join us.

With that being the case, we will be pounding the mochi.

The other things I will need aside from the steaming baskets was a type of rice pot with a wooden lid known as a hagama, cotton cloth, a table to work the mochi…… oh and we also need potato starch to coat it and prevent it from sticking.

The reason not everyone in the Sanctuary would participate in making the mochi was because sometimes preparations can’t be made in such short time, but since I didn’t know if the people of this world would accept mochi, this also serves as a trial run.

I quickly transmuted a mortar and pestle from wood.  

We need a lot, so being able to do this all at once was very convenient.

In the plaza at the Central district of the Sanctuary, several sets of firewood stoves with hagamas and steaming baskets were lined up.

Similarly, there were mortars and pestles set at specific intervals.

Quite a number of people assembled in the Central District plaza.

「Is the glutinous rice enough?」  

「It should be? It’s helpful having more hands around.」

More people gathered than expected, so I was worried if there was enough glutinous rice, but Maria was glad that there were more helping hands.

The grains were soaked in water overnight, so it would be impossible to add more if it wasn’t enough.

I added firewood to heat the water inside the hagama.

I laid down the cotton cloth on the steaming basket, then poured the rice onto it and began steaming it.

Everyone seemed to be enjoying their roles watching the fire and pounding the rice to mochi.

Now then, I should start pounding the mochi too.

+++

# 622 - A Day in Winter 2

The lively voices of children resounded in the plaza.

「Heave-ho! Heave-ho!」

Wappa, Sara, Miri, Lala, Colette, Shirona, Melanie, and Malorie alternated pounding the mochi rice.

Of course, it was only enough to experience it.

As Vanga-san, Golan-san, Doganbo-san and I took turns, the rice slowly started turning into mochi.

It wasn’t terribly cold, but steam emitted from the mochi as we aggressively pounded with pestles outside in winter.  

Once it started coming together, we started pounding it lightly.

How many batches have we done now? Because of my high status level, this much wasn’t enough to tire me.

The freshly pounded mochi was rolled into small mochi balls by Sophia, Maria, and Marnie.  

Akane made the red bean paste mochi with Lulu-chan.

The slightly hardened red bean mochi were delicious roasted on a grill.

It reminded me of the filling my grandma used to make.

Surprisingly, Madam Rosary, Madam Elizabeth, and Madam Lumia, ate the freshly made mochi with grated daikon, roasted soybean flour, and sweet soy sauce.

So she eats grated daikon. It might just be me who thought that the image of Madam Lumia, an elf, eating grated daikon didn’t fit. The person in question was enjoying it, after all.

Miss Mimir and the priests from the church were helping as well.

Today, our three aides were having fun pounding mochi too.  

I believe that people need days like this to unwind otherwise they’d become too stifled.

Near where the mochi was being rolled into small balls, there was a wooden box fileld with noshimochi[1] in flour.

Seeing the freshly made rice cakes, the Cat Sith Miri was astonished.

「Woahnya! It’s red nya!」  

「Miri, that mochi has little dried shrimp mixed into it. It’s a bit salty, so it’s delicious even as is.」  

「Miri wants to eat it nya!」  

「Lala too! Lala too!!」  

「Ah! Cheater! I also want one!」

Lala and Wappa started causing a ruckus, so even though I was planning on rolling all of the shrimp filled mochi into flat ones, I decided to roll a few into small portions for them to eat.

「Can you help me with this?」  

「Yes. Everyone! Make sure you wash your hands properly! We’re all going to start rolling it!」  

「「「「Yay!」」」」

Maria led the children to a work table.

This time, aside from the normal white mochi with no filling, we have shrimp-filled mochi, and bean-filled mochi for three types of it.

In my childhood days in my previous life, we made mochi at home because my dad was great at making kagami mochi[2].

Back then, it was common to decorate the house with kagami mochi.

Well, even so, the only ones to steam glutenous rice in wood fire in the neighborhood was my family.

「Takumi-san, we’ve brought the nori.」  

「Oh, Fluna-san.」

The one to bring the nori was the Mermaid Fluna-san.

I had asked the mermaids for various sea-related things.

They, of course, fish, but I also built salt making facilities for salt production, and the person in charge of that industry was a member of the mermaids. People other than the mermaids work there now, but the supervision was left to the merfolk.

And since I was originally Japanese, I was able to have rice in the Sanctuary because of Dryas. Seasonings like soy sauce and miso were also accepted by the Sanctuary residents, so a stable supply chain was established.

And so, if there’s a sea, I’ll want nori too.

Cultivating laver needed a lot of trial and error, but Fluna-san didn’t make a single reluctant face and cooperated.

And the nori we somehow produced was also accepted by the residents of the Sanctuary.

Nori is essential for onigiri, after all.

Fluna-san and the others began challenging themselves with nori tsukudani.

「You’ve come at the perfect time. It’s just been freshly pounded, so please eat it with soy sauce and nori.」  

「Yes. Thank you for the meal.」

The nori that Fluna-san brought was brought to the table that Madam Rosary, Madam Elizabeth and Madam Lumia were seated at.

The sharp-eared trio overheard me talk about another way of eating it by wrapping it in nori and dipping in soy sauce, and so they beckoned Fluna-san over.

Vanga-san, Golan-san, and Doganbo-san continued to steam glutenous rice.

They felt awkward about it at first, but after a few times, they had gotten used to it, and had built up a good swinging tempo.

Well, the one who pounded most of it was me though.

In the end, we made more mochi than I expected.

And it makes me happy that the Sanctuary people liked mochi more than I expected too.

It would be nice to make it a winter tradition.

+++

# 623 - Growth and Reduction

A ghost town in the border region of the former Divine Empire of Sydnia which once existed in the center of the continent. There was a change in the Flesh Tree that grew in that abandoned church.

The dark child embraced by the outstretched hands protruding from the Flesh Tree appeared to be a three year old only several months ago, but now it had grown to be around a six to seven year old.

Though it still embraced the child, the size of the Flesh Tree had decreased in contrast to the growth of the dark child.

「It is going well.」  

「Yes, the child is growing favorably.」

The aged man, Agares, was smiling, content at the growth of the Goddess Anat’s child whom was cradled by the Flesh Tree.  

Once a human priest in a border town, the man had now outgrown his human shell and become a leader of the demon kind.

A man observing the child protected by the Flesh Tree spoke with Agares. The bespectacled nervous man who was once the governor of the town had changed his name to Buer.

They both looked human as they had no extra limbs.

However, what sets these two apart from the rest was their grey skin which did not match any other race.

「What of Gamigin and the others?」

Buer asked Agares without looking away from the child.

「Ahh, Horsehead and Lionface? They had gone hunting with their underlings.」  

「Hmph, those two must really have muscles for brains……」

Buer noticed that one other name had not come out of Agares’ lips.

「Hm? What of Gremory? Now that I think about it, I haven’t seen her in a while.」  

「……Gremory?」

Seeing Agares’s face turn sour, Buer shook his head, looking fed up.

「That woman is fishing for men again? Good grief, how bothersome.」  

「Yeah, I’ve told her not to make much of a spectacle though.」  

「I don’t give a damn about the guys she would squeeze dry, but if she were to move too conspicuously, it would put us in danger.」  

「Gremory was a former harlot, after all. It’s our fault for expecting her to have any sense of decency.」

Agares and Buer frowned in unison.

「That woman is a demon, though not a succubus.」  

「Buer, succubi do not kill men. Only someone like Gremory would suck the life out of men.」  

「Fumu, is that so? I’m not all too familiar with the mode of life of the Devilkin.」

Buer and Agares were Demonkin, vastly different from Devilkin. The Devil race fall within the realm of people, Demons were a class of monsters that didn’t classify as people.

Just as Agares corrected Buer’s misunderstanding, the Succubi of this world did not have the power to enter people’s dreams, nor do they have the ability to absorb life force and kill through sexual activities or anything of the sort.

As Buer and Agares conversed, loud footsteps could be heard approaching.

The loud footsteps came from the Horse-headed Gamigin and the Lion-headed, four armed Malbas.

「Ou! We’re back!」  

「We have returned.」  

「Be quiet, you are in front of God’s Child.」

Agares reproached Gamigin for his loud voice, but Gamigin was completely unfazed as he gazed at the Flesh Tree.  

Malbas, on the other hand, seemed unconcerned as he simply gave a brief report of his return.

Their behaviors may have been influenced by their previous lives as humans.  

Gamigin was once a rough lumberjack, and his disposition hadn’t changed very much.  

Malbas was previously a temple knight, so while he had become more ferocious as a Demon, he still had the air of a disciplined warrior somehow.

「Did the Great Tree grow a tiny bit smaller?」  

「Hoh, so even someone as crude as you can tell?」  

「Shut it! Even I can tell that much!」  

「Umu, the development of God’s Child is proceeding favorably.」

Gamigin and Malbas also noticed that the Flesh Tree had become slightly smaller.  

And so, Buer asked Gamigin and Malbas about the current situation.

「Now, Malbas what of your subordinates?」  

「They are definitely monsters, so it can’t be helped that they aren’t that smart, but they can still be commanded.」  

「Are there a few individuals that can evolve to a higher being?」  

「A few emerge here and there, but you know their origins. They still have a long way to go.」  

「Hmph! I don’t need your weak monster subordinates!」  

「Ignore that meathead Gamigin, Buer. More importantly, you should tell Gremory to come back more often.」  

「What do you mean meathead!? Tch! How boring!」

With noisy, heavy steps, Gamigin left.

「Good grief, that man will drag us down.」  

「I have no problem killing him if that time comes.」  

「Killing a companion would also be problematic too, though.」

Buer and Agares shook their heads in disbelief.

The Flesh Tree pulsated, and the Evil Spirit’s child grew steadily.

+++

# 624 - Winter Makes Me Want Hotpot

The mochi making event in the Central District Plaza was definitely a hit.

We shared a bit with the Sanctuary Residents, and their feedback was really good, and since there was quite a few people who wanted to rent a mortar, pestle, and steaming basket, we gave some advice before lending.

As for the mochi rice, we’re getting help from Dryas for now, but we decided to grow it starting next year.

We’ll have to cut the noshimochi soon. Should I make a mochi cutter?

Some thinly sliced okaki(mochi cut thin, dried then cooked[[1]](https://www.euricette.com/greatest-alchemist-chapter-624/#GA-G1)) would be nice too.

I remember that in my grandma’s house, we placed it on a hibachi and grilled it.

I wonder if there’s any other way to eat mochi.

Since I can’t just grill mochi and eat it with sweet soy sauce and nori, I tried thinking of other methods.

As for why I’m doing this, Sophia and the others asked if there’s any other ways to eat it, but neither Akane nor I were able to give an answer.

So Akane and I brainstormed it.

「We made okaki and placed it in ochazuke(rice in tea).」  

「I usually grilled it like normal and ate it with sweet soy sauce.」  

「Shrimp mochi and bean mochi are grilled as is too.」  

「Ah, oh yeah. There’s also zenzai(chunky red bean soup with mochi) when you break open the kagami mochi[[2]](https://www.euricette.com/greatest-alchemist-chapter-624/#GA-G2), right?」  

「Ahh, zenzai was a thing.」

I liked sweet things, so I remember eating zenzai and oshirukop[[3]](https://www.euricette.com/greatest-alchemist-chapter-624/#GA-G3) a lot.

「Didn’t we put it in gratin and pizza?」  

「I’ve never tried it but I think those did exist. But we definitely had okonomiyaki with cheese and mochi, right?」  

「Grilled cheese mochi. The girls would definitely like that. It’s also delicious if you add potatoes to it.」  

「Okonomiyaki would work.」

If it’s okonomiyaki, we can cook it with the things they like. This is definitely a good idea.

「Hey, it’s winter so we can add mochi to hotpot.」  

「Ah, hotpot with mochi~ I’ve never tried it.」

I’ve added ramen and udon to hotpot but never mochi.

「It’s delicious.」  

「I think I’ve seen thin cut mochi for shabu shabu in a supermarket before.」  

「Nice. Mochi shabu shabu. Let’s do that.」  

「Then should I make a pot?」  

「When it comes to hotpot, it has to be a donabe(earthenware pot). Takumi, please make one.」  

「I guess there’s pots made of metal, but it has to be a donabe for a Japanese.」  

「You’re not Japanese anymore though.」

Ignoring Akane’s remark about not being Japanese, I should get to making that donabe.

Making it the normal way without any magic would have been difficult, but it’s simple with magic.

There’s earth everywhere, but I asked Gnome where I can find good clay, then I went to collect some in the mining area in the South District.

I transmuted the clay that I mined using alchemy, then I shaped it into a pot and fired it up using magic.

After confirming there were no leaks, I made several donabe of the same size.

「Next, I’ll have to talk to Fluna-san.」

When it comes to hotpot ingredients, there’s seafood, chicken, and pork, but I’m in the mood for fish.  

So let’s go ask the mermaid Fluna-san if there’s any fish that would work for hotpot.

When I went to the seaside in the Western District, Fluna-san was right there.

「Fluna-san, I have something to ask, but do you have time to spare?」  

「Ah, Takumi-san, of course it’s okay.」

I talked about wanting fish that would suit a hotpot.

「A hotpot?」  

「Yeah, a hotpot is……」

She didn’t seem to know what a hotpot was. I guess that would be the case. Just “hotpot” could be misconstrued as just a cooking utensil.

「Ahh, it’s the name of a dish, is it? And it’s a general term for various types. Intriguing.」  

「That’s right. So, meat is alright, but I was thinking of making hotpot with fish as the main ingredient. But I don’t know what fish is in season here. So I thought you would know.」  

「Leave it to me! ………in return, may I also eat?」  

「Of course, I’ll invite you.」  

「Hooray! Then I’ll show you the fish that was caught today!」

Following Fluna-san, we arrived at the cold storehouse.

This cold storehouse has two sections, a 5℃ fridge and a -20℃ freezer to temporarily store the caught fish.

「What do you think of this one? It’s a white-fleshed fish, but it’s fatty and tastes good.」  

「T-that’s huge.」

What Fluna-san pointed to was a fish probably the size of an adult human. I guess it resembles a longtooth grouper? If so, then it’s really gotta be delicious.

「I guess we’ll go with this fish. Also, could we get some shellfish too?」  

「Yes. The shellfish are over here.」

I got some of the shellfish that Fluna-san recommended, then I went back to the mansion with her.

Now then, I suppose preparing that gigantic fish is my job. At that size, I guess “dismantling” it would be more appropriate.

+++

# 625 - Udon or Rice to finish?

Back at the mansion, I tackled the dismantling of fish.

During that time, I had tasked Akane with procuring the vegetables.

「Akane, could you get the veggies we’ll use for the hotpot?」  

「Leave it to me. I’ll buy them right away.」  

「Lulu will come with nya.」

Akane and Lulu-chan left to get the ingredients.

The Sanctuary now has a monetary economy as well, so it’s become possible to buy all sorts of things.

The fish that Fluna-san recommended was so big it could already be called a monster, so I gave up on using a knife and processed it using a larger knife meant for dismantling.

「T-these bones are hard.」  

「Yes. Despite how large it is, I guarantee that it tastes refined and is incredibly flavorful.」  

「I’m excited about that, but it’s going to be a lot of effort turning these into fillets.」

I’ll fillet them for the time being.

「I was going to use these bones to make stock, but…… I wonder if these will turn out okay.」  

「You can make stock from bones?」  

「Yeah, I was going to grill it and then use it for dashi. But these bones are bigger and harder than I thought………」

A fish of this size can’t be eaten in one sitting, so I took from different parts as I filleted it.

「I suppose this much is fine?」  

「That seems like it would fill us up.」

I stowed away the fillets into my Item Box for the time being, then I quickly washed the bones in hot water and grilled them to give it a nice char.

Now to make the dashi. I placed water into a large stock pot, then let the kombu soak in it. I then placed the grilled bones and heated them together.

I skimmed off the scum from the dashi, removed the bones and kombu before it boiled, then checked for the taste.

「Okay, it isn’t fishy anymore so this is done.」  

「This kombu dashi has a pleasant flavor of fish. It’s delicious.」

If Fluna-san, a mermaid, says it’s delicious, then it’s probably okay.

I added a bit of soy sauce and sake to the dashi and increased the heat.

As I headed to the kitchen with the stock pot filed with dashi, Akane and Lulu-chan came back with a lot of vegetables.

It was then that Maria and Sala, a maid, came to help.

「We’ll prepare the vegetables, so Takumi, could you prepare the mochi, udon, and rice?」  

「Eh, it’s not just mochi? We’re also having udon and rice as a porridge?」  

「We may as well, having just one isn’t enough, so it’d be more enjoyable having multiple ways to eat it, right?」  

「You do have a point.」

What Akane said was reasonable, so I left the veggie prep to them, and took charge of cooking the rice and making udon.

「I’ll cut corners with the udon.」

I prepared the wheat, water, and salt.

「『Transmute』!」

Kneading and rest would have taken time, so I made udon in an instant using magic.

I skipped the rolling and cutting processes and the thin udon was ready.

I boiled the udon once and stored it.

「Takumi, do we have some portable cooking stoves?」  

「I think Laeva can bring some out of you ask her.」  

「Gotcha.」

Large platters piled high with vegetables were carried by Maria and Sala to the dining room.

Fluna-san had gotten the fillets from me and arranged them on platters.  

Akane then came back.

「Wow, that’s fish looks delicious.」  

「Right? It’s the white fish that Fluna-san recommended. It looked like a monstrous grouper though.」  

「If it’s grouper then I’ll have high expectations.’ Ah, Fluna-san, let me help you with those.」  

「Thank you.」

Akane and Fluna-san carried the large platters lined with fish fillets and shellfish.

I also brought plates of thinly sliced noshimochi to the dining room where there were three donabe(clay pots), and platters of vegetables, fish, and shellfish, as well as individual plates.

I retrieved the stock pot and poured dashi into the three donabe.

「I will light the fire now.」

A maid ignited the portable stoves.

The maid, Maria, and Fluna-san placed vegetables, fish fillets, and shellfish into it.

「Takumi, the mochi?」  

「Coming, there’s no rush.」

Urged by Akane, I placed the plate of thinly sliced mochi on the table.

Maria and Akane placed the ingredients into the hotpot.

I’m no hotpot master, so I don’t know when to place the ingredients in.

The dashi and ingredients simmering together was starting to waft a wonderful aroma.

「Ooh~ It smells delicious nya~」

Lulu-chan could wait no longer and looked like she was about to start drooling.

「Lulu, this part should be good now.」  

「I’ll have it nya!」

Akane handed a portion over to Lulu-chan.

We all then started taking the ingredients that we liked and ate.

「……so good.」  

「……yes, this method of eating is also quite nice.」

It seems hotpot was well received by everyone.

We continued to eat, and after throwing in the mochi, it was about time to finish when Akane spoke up.

「To finish, we have udon and rice porridge. Let’s have the two pots on the side with rice and the middle one will have udon.」  

「……we’re really eating well.」

Just like what was said, rice was placed in two of the donabes, and one was filled with udon. We whisked eggs into the three hotpots, then topped with green onion. Chopped nori was sprinkled on top of the rice porridge, and it was complete.

I thought we’d have a lot left over, but the three donabes were completely empty.

# 626 - This Winter Feels Especially Cold

The deliciousness of winter hotpot had spread to everyone, and the variation of dishes that use mochi had increased, so there probably won’t be any mochi leftover this season.

That said, though it’s the season for hotpots, winter this year is colder than expected.

「Of course. The climate can’t be absolutely identical year after year.」

I must have voiced out my thoughts. Sylph said that it was nothing to worry about as it wasn’t strange.  

Thinking about it more, even when I lived in Japan, I did hear the terms “warm winter” and “cool summer”, and it did feel like there were differences in the temperature during summers and winters yearly.

And so, there was one item that I wanted.  

I wouldn’t be allowed to place it in the living room, so I’ll use it in my room.

I moved to my workshop and took wood out from the Item Box.

I transmuted a square low table.

I then made a matching tabletop for it.

Up until this point, the shapes had been pretty simple, so it was fine to just transmute them without much thought.

「That table is quite curious.」  

「Yeah, I suppose the low table looks weird.」

Laeva’s curiosity seemed to have been piqued.

「Moreover, isn’t that height strange?」  

「Well, this height is just right.」

Low tables must not exist in this world.

The people of this world basically walk into their houses with their shoes on.  

They had room shoes that were easy to put on and take off, after all.

Ah, if this is the case, maybe I should have a no-shoe policy in the room with the kotatsu.

Yes, I was making a kotatsu, which the Japanese need when it gets cold.

I remember sitting in a kotatsu and eating so many mandarin oranges that my hands turned yellow.

I installed a magic device to heat it up.

It needed a temperature control feature. I also had make countermeasures against toasted skin syndrome.

「Could this perhaps be a heating device? Wait, if that is the case, the shape of the table is strange.」  

「Now, now, I’ll let you try it out when it’s done, so just watch for now.」

Laeva was constantly puzzled.  

I don’t have a quilt cover for the kotatsu right now, so even if they knew it was a heating element, no one from this world would intuitively understand how it would work.

I still need the quilt cover and a thin mat underneath.

And so, I was enlisting Kaede’s help.

「Master, you called?」  

「Yeah, I have a request.」  

「Mm, okay!」

Maybe she was happy to have finally gotten a request from me for the first time in a long while, but Kaede was hyped up.

I immediately asked her for a cover that I could jam cotton into.

「Hey, hey, Master. are you not going to put stuffing made from my threads inside it?」  

「Eh, you can do that?」  

「Yup, I can!」  

「Then please do.」

Kaede quickly extracted her silk and weaved it into cloth.

After a while of watching her, I noticed that Kaede was weaving several pieces of fabric.

「Hm? Do we need that many pieces?」  

「That’s not it, Master. I’ll dye them into different colors!」  

「I see, so it’s like a patchwork quilt?」

It probably wouldn’t be exactly like a patchwork quilt, but I understood Kaede’s image.

Still, a patchwork quilt would work for the mat underneath.

「Okay, now we just need to dye it!」

Kaede took out several barrel-like containers from within her own Magic Bag.

When she opened the lid, it was filled with liquid.

「Are those dyes, by any chance?」  

「That’s right~ I collected all sorts of colors!」  

「Woah, since when?」

When I asked how she got that many types of dye, she mentioned discussing how to acquire dyes of various colors

Given how she mentioned Dryas, these had to be plant-based dyes, and I just remembered those existed.

As that was happening, Kaede dipped the fabrics in various dyes.

「Master, dry these with magic please.」  

「Ah, yeah, okay.」

After asking me to dry it, Kaede then started cutting and sewing the dyed fabrics together. She was lightning fast.

Before we knew it, the mosaic-patterned cloth was complete.

Kaede weaved another cloth of the same size to line the mosaic fabric and dyed it a strong grey.

She then produced the threads that would be used as stuffing.

Come to think of it, was it called silk wadding? In that case, Kaede’s threads were more than enough.  

It does feel just a bit luxurious, though.

As I was thinking that, the kotatsu quilt cover was completed.

Then, just like before, I asked Kaede to make a mat that felt like the quilt cover too.

「It’s done!」  

「Ohh, thanks Kaede.」

I lifted Kaede and gave her my thanks.

「So what are you going to use this for?」  

「Ahh, shall we head to my room to try it?」  

「Yup, let’s go!」  

「Can Laeva also join?」  

「Of course, that’s fine.」

I stored the kotatsu and the quilt cover into my Item Box temporarily, and we moved to my room.

「Now then, I’m going to purify the room just in case.」

The maids clean it up well, but I purified it using magic to make sure.

I then laid out the mat, then put the kotatsu table on top of it then covered that with the quilt.

「Oh, you put it over the low table from a while ago?」

Laeva was curious, but I placed the tabletop over it without minding her.

「Okay, that should do it. Try copying me.」

I removed my shoes, entered the kotatsu, and switched on the magic heating device.

「Ooh! Is this a home heater for a small number of people!?」  

「Yaaay! Looks fun!」

Laeva and Kaede mimicked me and entered the kotatsu, so I took out the mandarins from my Item Box and placed them in the Item Box.

「You go in the kotatsu then eat mandarins like this.」  

「Kaede will eat mandarins too!」  

「Laeva will also partake.」

In the end, the two really enjoyed the kotatsu, and the three of us lost track of time enjoying ourselves.

Seeing this, Maribelle scolded us, but why were we being scolded?

+++

# 627 - Occupied Room

For some reason, I was scolded by Maribelle for placing the kotatsu in my own room.

Apparently, it was going to make cleaning difficult.

Well, if it’s just that then they could tolerate it.

Winter was still getting colder, after all.

Thinking so, I returned from the living room to my room, only to be surprised.

「Wha!?」  

「Sorry for the intrusion nya.」

There, I saw Lulu-chan had come into the kotatsu placed at the center of my room. She was also lying down lazily. She was like a true cat.

That wasn’t all. The Cat Sith sisters Miri and Lala, as well as the Catkin siblings Wappa and Sara were also there, occupying the kotatsu.

「……isn’t this a cat festival now ?」

There were some eating the mandarins in the basket, some were lying down like Lulu-chan, and some were just doing what they want.

Well, cats definitely liked kotatsus, but I guess Cat Siths and Catkins are basically cats……

As to be expected, I felt hesitant squeezing in with the kids and going into the kotatsu, so I spoke and left the room.

「You can’t sleep in the kotatsu.」  

「「Yes nya!」」  

「Understood.」

If I remember correctly, Laeva did say that she was making her own kotatsu.

I knocked on the door to Laeva’s room.

「Yes, who is it?!」  

「Laeva, it’s me.」  

「Please come in, the door is unlocked.」

At Laeva’s permission, I opened the door to find her inside the kotatsu and writing some ideas down, Marnie was there with Flora on her lap, Maria was cradling Haruka, and for some reason, Laeva’s familiar Seru was deep in the kotatsu.

「…………umm, sorry for the intrusion.」

I turned about and headed to the living room.

When I sat down on the sofa, Maribelle served me some tea.  

With timing and consideration like this, the other maids were no match for Maribelle. She was a real veteran, I have nothing to complain about.

「Fuu, the living room isn’t even cold.」  

「Takumi-sama, is something the matter?」

Was she lulling Etoile? Sophia was alone in the living room.

「Ahh, the kotatsu in my room was taken over by Miri, Sara, and the others.」  

「Ah, that home heater. It seems quite popular with the Catkins and Cat Siths.」  

「The target audience was too little, huh?」

I considered making a kotatsu for my room in the Volton mansion, but the thought of being in a kotatsu alone in Volton was too sad, so I gave up.

Eventually, the kotatsu in my room was liberated after the children went home for the night.

「Fuu, tea is delicious.」

I was enjoying some dried, thinly sliced noshimochi and toasted okaki alongside some green tea.  

It really felt like back in the old days in Japan.

I was still alone in the kotatsu even in my room at the Sanctuary mansion though……

It was then that Akane and Lulu-chan arrived.

In Lulu-chan’s hand was a basket of mandarins. Akane was carrying a teapot and teacups.

「Sorry for the intrusion nya.」  

「I brought seconds of tea.」  

「You’re back.」

Lulu-chan laid down on her stomach, eating mandarins as she began reading a book.

After Akane steeped enough tea for her and I, she ate my okaki and started sketching winter designs.

Okay, I think I understand why Maribelle disliked the kotatsu.

It makes people a bit, no, quite lazy.

A heating device that corrupts people.

It could be dangerous if time in it is not limited.

「Hee, so cats do really like the kotatsu.」  

「Yeah, I never thought my kotatsu would be occupied.」  

「Lulu also likes the kotatsu nya.」

Lulu-chan’s tail swayed as she spoke while lying down.

「Isn’t it fine to sell kotatsus in the Sanctuary shops?」  

「Will it sell?」  

「Lulu would definitely buy it nya!」  

「O-oh, is that so?」

Lulu-chan raised her hand with voracity. She did that still lying down though……

「You’ve made one, so it’d be easy to make it with alchemy, right?」  

「Well, I can make it, but the quilt is impossible.」  

「Can’t the person who bought the kotatsu make it themselves?」  

「That could work too. Considering the structures of the housing in the Sanctuary, I don’t know if there would be much demand for kotatsus here.」  

「I think it will be with the Cat Siths and Catkins, at least.」

Let’s think of it that way.

I should send one as a present for Miri and Lala’s home, as well as to Wappa and Sara’s. In doing so, they wouldn’t stay around in my room.

「Okay, I’ll make a few.」

I psyched myself up and left the kotatsu, then transmuted 20 sets of kotatsus in the workshop.

I brought them to a store straight away, then to the kids’ houses as presents. There was no quilt cover, so I also handed a thick, large square cloth.

The next day, there were additional orders for kotatsus.

It appears the kotatsu really is well accepted by certain people.

+++

# 628 - Winter Play

I got scolded. Then I got scolded again.

The kotatsu corrupts people.

If I lounge around in my room, Maribelle scolds me.

It couldn’t be helped, so I thought about playing with Flora.

“No, you have to work.” being shoved at me is unacceptable.

Unlike Etoile and Haruka, who were elf and human respectively, Flora who was a rabbitkin could already stand up by herself and had been walking bit by bit.

I was both happy and a little bit sad about how fast she was growing, and I had to get myself together and focus on playing with her.

Basically everything I wear, from my underwear to my casual wear to my coat, were all made from fabrics weaved from Kaede’s threads.  

These outfits were enchanted to maintain a comfortable temperature, so unless I am in extreme colds or scorching deserts, it would mostly feel like a normal summer heat or winter cold that pose no obstacle when I wear my jacket.

Naturally, the winter chill in the Sanctuary this year was no problem at all.

And of course, Flora’s outerwear was also enchanted.

And so we were able to play outside.

I arrived at a completely vacant space on the south side, still in the central district.

This area in the direction heading towards the south mining district still had plenty of vacant space.

In this one area, I used magic to create a large amount of snow.

「Oh my, just as I was wondering what you were doing, these piles of snow appeared.」

I adjusted the firmness and sloping of the snow, Undine showed herself.

「Yup, I’m going to play with Flora in the snow.」  

「Is that so? Playing in the snow is not a concept to the people of this world, is it?」  

「That may be the case.」

Undine and the other Great Spirits were aware that I was reincarnated into this world by Goddess Norn, so they often express how the people of this world were like.

Playing might only be a possibility if you had enough time to spare in your life.

「I wonder if skiing or skating exists in this world?」  

「Hmm, I don’t know. Sylph, what do you think?」

When Undine said that, Sylph suddenly appeared.

「Skating and skiing? There is a tool for walking in places where snow gather. It’s so that you don’t sink into the snow. But what Takumi mentioned is probably not that.」  

「If you both don’t know it, then it might not exist.」

What Sylph was talking about was likely snow shoes.

Since it’s faster to show it than explain with words, I took out enough Treant Wood and mithril alloy from my Item Box, and then I invoked my alchemy spell.

「『Transmute』!」

I transmuted skis and snowboards right there.

「I have to make the boots too.」

I took out monster leather and a small amount of mithril alloy from the Item Box and transmuted it.

「『Transmute』!」

I created ski boots and snowboard boots.

「is that the ski tool?」  

「The shape is different.」  

「The two planks are the skis, and the single plank is the snowboard.」

Undine and Sylph picked up the skis and snowboard to examine them.

「Ohh, it’s well made. So these boots fasten to those metal fittings.」  

「Yeah, it’s designed to release when a certain amount of force is applied, so it’s safe.」

I reproduced the foot bindings of skis and snowboards too. It was a trial product only meant to show these two, so it had no lining on the bottom side meant to reduce friction with the snow.

「Can this even be used by children?」  

「Of course, I just have to change the size.」

The size of the snowboards and skis aside, I’d have to make various sizes of boots too.

「How intriguing. It would be nice to play in winter.」  

「You would catch a cold if you don’t wear warm clothes, you know.」  

「Ah, that was a thing.」

We would need ski-wear, huh. How thoughtless of me.

「If you have to make the clothing too, that would be a lot of work.」  

「What fun things do you plan to do with Flora for now?」  

「Building snowmen and playing on a sled, I guess.」

Since I’d be playing with little Flora, I hadn’t even considered skiing and snowboarding.

「Sled?」  

「Hold on a sec.」

Since it’s a sled, it can be made with easily with a little bit of wood.

I took Treant Wood out of my Item Box for a second time and began the transmutation process.

「『Transmute』!」

What I transmuted was a sled that could fit one adult.

「Ah, a sled. There’s a slightly larger one like this. Its use is different though.」  

「Indeed. In places where snow piles up, they use it to transport luggage.」

Apparently, there were sleds drawn by horses and Demon Horses in the northern regions of this world where snow accumulated.

「This one won’t be pulled by a horse, it’s meant for sliding down a slope.」

I already made the sled, so I should play with Flora.

「Wait a moment.」  

「That’s right. Why are you leaving already?」  

「You haven’t explained what skating is yet.」

Undine and Sylph grabbed my shoulder.

「I wanna play with Flora though…… okay fine.」

It couldn’t be helped, so I gave a simple explanation of skates.

「It’s shoes attached with a blade that let you glide on ice.」  

「Wait a moment.」

It would be much easier to understand if they see it, so I will quickly transmute one.

I’ll use the design of a figure skating shoe, I guess?

「『Transmute』!」

I didn’t make the edge too sharp so it shouldn’t be dangerous.  

I handed Undine the completed skates.

「Woah, how intriguing. I want to glide too.」  

「Ah, me too, please.」  

「Sigh, fine.」

Sylph said she wanted her own, so after I created another, then moved away from the snowy playground, then used Earth Magic to flatten the ground.

I surrounded the area with chest-high walls and created a thick layer of ice within it.

「Whew, this is a skating rink. Try skating inside this.」

Before I could even finish my sentence, Undine and Sylph already wore their skates and started gliding.

「How fascinating.」  

「Uwaa! This is fun!」  

「……you’re skating even without any practice.」

Anything goes with the Great Spirits, I guess.

「Takumi! Make sure to prepare a few sleds!」

I heard Sylph yell as I was heading back.

I raised my hand in acknowledgement.

I want to play with Flora as soon as possible.

# 629 - The Cats That Came Out of the Kotatsu

Having made the snow hill and skating rink, I left Undine and Sylph to skate, then returned to the mansion.

When I went directly to the children’s room, Etoile and Haruka were asleep, but Flora wasn’t in her baby bed.

When I went to the living room because of that, Flora who had been playing with Marnie and Maria came tottering over to me when she saw me.

「Daa~, Daa~」  

「Yoisho.」

I picked up Flora who clung tightly to my leg.

「What’s up Flora? You’re in a good mood.」  

「Flora loves Papa.」  

「Beastkin babies grow up so fast, huh?」  

「Maria, Haruka will grow big before you know it. Children are like that.」

If they grow up too fast, they might hit their rebellious phase sooner.  

Well, Beastkin grow fast until they’re three years old, so Etoile and Haruka would soon catch up.

「What’s the matter then?」  

「Ahh, about that. I was looking for Flora because I was thinking of going sledding with her.」  

「Sledding?」  

「Takumi-sama, snow doesn’t accumulate in the Sanctuary.」

Hearing sledding, Marnie looked puzzled, and Maria pointed out that there was no place to sled.

「Of course, I created a snow hill.」  

「A snow hill?」  

「Snow mountain nya?」  

「Eh, Miri, since when have you been here?」

Then I suddenly heard Miri’s[[1]](https://www.euricette.com/greatest-alchemist-chapter-629/#GA-G1) voice.

I don’t always check for presences in my own home, so I didn’t notice her.

It may be because Miri is a Cat Sith that her presence was hard to sense.

The Cat Sith were a timid race, so it’s possible that they have a naturally weak presence.

「Hey hey, Takumi-oniichan, what’s a snow hill nya?」  

「I made a mountain of snow in a vacant lot. I thought it would be fun to go sledding.」  

「Really nya!? I need to tell everyone!」

Saying so, Miri ran…… to my room.

「Then I will prepare mittens and a jacket so Flora doesn’t get cold.」  

「I’ll take Sara and the others’ mittens.」

Marnie and Maria left the living room, so I cuddled Flora while waiting.

「Is the snow hill real!? I want to go sledding too!」  

「Oniichan! Sara too! Sara too!」

The Catkin siblings, Wappa and Sara were talking on and on excitedly.

「Wappa, we’re preparing mittens for you, so wear a warm coat and come over. At the same time, could you also invite Colette, Shirona, Melanie, and Malorie?」  

「Okay! I’ll go right now!」  

「Wait, oniichan!」

Wappa ran out of the mansion.

「Lala and Miri will also get jackets nya!」  

「Okay nya, Oneechan!」

Miri and Lala hurriedly followed after Wappa.

「It sure is lively over here.」  

「I brought the jacket and mittens.」  

「Everyone went home for a bit. We’re going to have to take these with us.」

After everyone left, Marnie and Maria returned.

I got the jacket from Marnie and dressed Flora.

「Okay let’s put one arm in this sleeve~. Very good, now let’s put the other one in~」  

「Daa~」  

「Flora, give mama your hand. Yes, that’s great. Let’s do the other hand too…… okay, this will do.」  

「Let me put these warm shoes on your little feetsies okay~」

Marnie put mittens on Flora, while Maria had warm boots for her.

「Yes. Once her hat is on, she’s good to go.」

Lastly, Marnie put a woolen cap on Flora.

I’ve been thinking about it recently, but when did they make the coat, mittens, boots, and woolen cap?

The children’s clothing had been increasing more and more than I realized.

Even without that, Etoile had her grandparents, Dante-san and Freesia-san, who always brought something for her to wear at any possible occasion, and Madam Lumia would always come by with a present.

Haruka and Flora were also like Madam Elizabeth and Madam Rosary’s own grandchildren and were apparently sent all sorts of gifts from the Royal Capital.

I acknowledge Vanga-san and Martha-san as my children’s grandparents’, so my children have many grandparents.

I held Flora as I walked up the snow hill with Marnie and Maria.

Wappa and the others were already in the snow hill, and excited that it was far bigger than they imagined.

「Hey! Your mittens!」

As Maria distributed the mittens, I brought the sled out.

「I’m riding first!」  

「Not fair, oniichan!」

Wappa took the sled and climbed the snow hill with Sara chasing after him.

「Alrighty, our Flora also wants to play on the sled, don’t you~」  

「Please wait, Takumi-sama.」

When I tried climbing the snow hill with Flora, I was stopped.

「Eh? What?」  

「Takumi-sama, you aren’t wearing your coat and boots.」  

「Ah, I-it’s fine.」  

「Even though it has been endowed with temperature control, that’s not enough.」  

「Guh, I’ll come back soon!」

Leaving Flora with Marnie, I dashed back into the mansion.

# 630 - Take Me Skiing

When I teleported to the mansion, I changed to boots and wore gloves then teleported back to the snow hill.

It would have been nice if Maria had also brought it together with the ones she did for Wappa and the kids.

「Kyahahahaha!」

When I came back to the snow mountain, Flora was sliding down the hill in Marnie’s arms.

「Ahhh, I wanted to be the first one to sled with her.」

When I saw Flora looking so happy on the sled, I felt both happy and jealous.

And so, I looked around and saw that Wappa and the others looked like they were having fun.

Wappa carried the sled up the hill, but the smaller kids were playing and making snowmen with Maria at the foot of it, which was practically flat.

While I was checking if everyone was having fun, Marnie came over to me with Flora in one arm and pulled the sled with the other.

「Takumi-sama, please play with Flora.」  

「Thanks, Marnie! Come with me, Flora.」

I took Flora from Marnie and pulled the sled up the hill.

We played until Flora was satisfied.

Wappa, Sara, and the kids must have gotten hungry from playing all through the morning, so they went to their respective homes. Once they’ve eaten lunch, they’ll probably play again.

The children went home, so Marnie, Maria, and I returned to the mansion.

Even though she was growing up fast, Flora was still a baby, so being outside for a long time was very taxing on her.

At home, Sophia, Laeva, Akane, and the rest were gathered for lunch, Undine and Sylph who were having lunch with us requested some equipment.

「Takumi, please make more skis, snowboards, and skates.」  

「Yes. Today is fine, but the Sanctuary residents are going to come by starting tomorrow.」  

「Sigh, okay.」

Apparently, the Sanctuary residents did not come to the snow hill today out of respect for me.

「Takumi, could you make a snowboard for me too?」  

「Akane-sama, what’s a snowboard nya?」  

「I will teach Lulu.」  

「Woah, Akane, you know how to snowboard?」  

「I’ve gone out enough. I can shred.」

Snowboarding and skiing wasn’t that popular in Akane’s generation, her parents must have been snowboarders.

「Skiing and snowboarding?」  

「Yeah, it’s when you use specialized equipment to slide down the snow.」

Since Sophia helped watch over Etoile and Haruka today, she didn’t know what skis and snowboards were, so I gave a simple explanation.

「Is skating something similar?」  

「No, skating is when you glide over ice.」

Skiing and skating had similar names, so I explained what skates were, but Sophia couldn’t imagine what it was like.

「Ah, oh right, it might be easier to understand if I show you the prototype I designed.」

I showed her the skates that I made yesterday.

「Takumi, why don’t you show the skis, ski boots, snowboard, and snowboard boots too?」  

「Oh, you have a point.」

Like Sylph said, I took out all the prototypes from my Item Box.

「Nice, you recreated the boots and bindings well too.」  

「More or less. I haven’t attached the edges yet, and I still have to improve the bottom surface to improve it so it slides better.」

I haven’t decided whether I would make wax yet, but the edge can’t just be a plain sheet for a gliding surface.

「Should I measure everyone’s foot sizes?」  

「Can’t you just enchant it with Automatic Size Adjustment?」  

「It will need raw materials too. I’m planning on using materials that can handle two enchantments, but it would still be better to adjust the sizes to some degree.  

「Hmmm.」

Akane didn’t really understand, but she didn’t refute it when I said it was necessary.

I had everyone, not just my family, but the maids and my aides too, help me with gathering various sizes and shapes of feet.

「Alrighty, shall I make it right away?」  

「Please.」  

「Ah, Laeva will assist you.」

We had to make a lot, but since it’s a prototype of something that already existed, it would be alright if I make it in an assembly-line system.

Dividing the work with Laeva, we started making skis, ski boots, poles, snowboards, snowboard boots, and ice skates with various sizes.

I had considered making the edge and ice skate blades using a stainless steel compounded with chrome, but figured it would be better to just use regular steel if I enchant it.

To treat the sliding surface of the ski and snowboard, I had to reexamine their structures.

I remember the boards need to be flexible and durable

I’ll be using some excellent Treant Wood as the core material, so it shouldn’t break or get damaged easily, so it would be fine if I reinforce it on top of that.

We weren’t making that many, so Laeva and I divided the work and we finished before dinner.

Now all that’s left was to wait for tomorrow. It would be inconvenient if the hill was left as is.

# 631 - Takumi is Experienced

The day after we finished making the skis, snowboards, and ice skates, I climbed up the snow hill.

I made new snow fall from the top.  

Because of everyone playing yesterday, the snow was packed in and the surface hardened.

I then built a single tower at the top of the hill.

The metal tower pierced through the snow and into the ground, so it would still stand strong even with the snow hill gone.  

It was 30cm in diameter, but it was incredibly solid.

I then prepared a long rope.

I installed a long rail or a guard bar from the tower to the foot of the hill.

Yes, instead of a lift, this contraption can pull people to the top when they grab the rope.

「No, wait. Maybe this is too hard for the kids.」

With skis and snowboards, it would be easy to ride these, but it might be difficult for children who play on sleds.

「As I thought, it’s more work but maybe I should go with the lift?」

Since it’d be removed by springtime anyway, I was going to make something simple, but it wouldn’t be good to compromise for the children’s sake.

I immediately changed the rope to a wire.

I set up a support tower that would act as the fulcrum at the foot of the hill.

All that’s left to do is add benches to the wire, install a magic device to power it, and as a precautionary measure to stop all activity if danger is detected, a golem with a simple AI to control the power component.

With this, even if a child failed to ride the lift, it would stop immediately.

The moment I finished the lift, I heard a voice behind me.

「I was wondering what you’ve been doing since the morning, that’s quite the construction project you have going on. This is only for winter, isn’t it?」  

「Ah, Sylph? That’s right, it’s only for winter, but it’s very taxing climbing every time, right? I could teleport to the top myself, but that’s hardly any fun.」

The only ones whose presence I could not sense until they spoke up was the Great Spirits, and the one who did was Sylph.

And there was one other person there, Undine.

「Hey, should I handle the maintenance of the ice?」  

「Ah, can I ask you to? I think it’s fine since it was just from yesterday, but if you could, for now.」  

「Very well. In exchange, hand over my ice skates.」  

「Yeah, I can do that much.」  

「Ah, in that case, me too.」  

「Yes, yes.」

When I handed Undine her ice skates, Sylph, expectedly, wanted a pair for herself too.

「Well then, let’s try ice skating.」  

「Indeed, we will be the first ones.」

Carrying their ice skates, Undine and Sylph headed towards the skating rink.

「Alright, time to test it out too.」

I took out the skis, stocks, and ski boots out of my Item Box.

「Ohh, wearing ski boots that fits perfectly feels weird.」

I’m not wearing skiwear, so my clothes will get wet if I fell, but I’m just testing it out for a bit, so it should be alright.

I suppose I should at least wear gloves.

I stepped into the ski bindings with my boot and heard a click as it locked onto the ski. I did the same with my other foot.

I tried pressing my foot down to get a feel for the skis.

「Hm, its flex is just right.」

The ski was a type of carving skis(Also known as Parabolic Skis), which I had never used before.

Carving skis were wider on the tip and tail, with a narrow middle section.

I remember they were developed to make it possible for even regular skiers to carve turns.

Back when I used to ski, carving skis weren’t even invented yet. But since I’m making one anyway, I may as well try carving skis.

I skated towards the lift.

「Move the lift for me.」

When I called out to the lift-controlling golem, the lift began to move. The course wasn’t very long, so I reached the top in no time.

「Now then, let’s see if my body still remembers.」

Well, strictly speaking, it wasn’t this body though.

I vigorously pushed off with the stokes to slide down.

I tried carving turns, digging in the edges.

「Ooh, it’s easy making sharp turns. Maybe this is a benefit of my Body Control skill?」

This snowy hill was made for sledding with the children, so it’s gentle and has no bumps. It has a moderate slope, so it might be easy to someone experienced, but it’s still fun.

Before I knew it, I was already at the base of the hill.

「As expected, it’s over just like that.」

After all, the course was only 500 meters in a straight line. On skis, it was inevitable that it would be over in the blink of an eye.

「One more run?」

It’s just been so long that it’s so fun.  

The snow had been topped off just this morning, so it was powdered snow.

It couldn’t be helped that I was scolded by Maribelle for going skiing without having breakfast.

+++

# 632 - Coaching isn’t needed

「Whatever could you have been doing that you missed out on breakfast, Master?」  

「Sorry.」

What awaited me when I came home for a moment was a scolding from Maribelle.

Sophia and the others probably just assumed that I was going nuts over making another thing, and thought nothing of it since I was safe in the Sanctuary, but that didn’t pass with Maribelle.

And so, after having breakfast alone, I once again returned to the snow hill.

Unlike yesterday, there were residents who had come by during their breaks to sightsee.

Wappa and the other kids seem to not be done helping out at work so they weren’t here yet.

I built a simple shed in a convenient spot at the foot of the hill.

Here, I placed the skis and other snow equipment for everyone to use.

As ever, this was the Sanctuary so there was no worry of theft. Since it’s for everyone’s use, there was no need for lock and key either.

I also built a shed near the skating rink, and placed the ice skates there.

Once noon came around, Wappa and the kids ran over with their sleds after their lunch.

「Hey, hey! Takumi-oniichan, what is that?」  

「Ahh, I made a lift to make it easier to climb to the top.」  

「Not that! The small shed!」  

「Ahh, that one, huh? It’s a place to store the ski and snowboarding equipment.」

What Wappa was curious about was not the lift, but rather the shed. Please, take notice of the lift.

「Can we use it too?」  

「Of course, there are some meant for children, so use it as much as you like.」

When I showed the kids into the small shed, I showed them the ski and snowboarding equipment and explained how they work.

「I like the snowboard!」  

「Oniichan, Sara too, Sara too!」  

「Miri wants the snowboard nya!」  

「Lala also wants snowboard nya!」

It wasn’t only Wappa’s little sister Sara, but even Miri and Lala wanted to use the snowboards. And so, the Human sisters Colette and Shirona also chose the snowboards.

「I guess I could also use this one.」  

「Shirona wants what Oneechan has!」

Skiing’s popularity is…… I even made the carving skis for it.

And so, I noticed that among the early members, the Elf sisters Melanie and Malorie weren’t around.

「Where are Melanie and Malorie?」  

「They went to the ice!」  

「Ahh, so they went to the skating rink.」

Sylph and Undine were taking a break and skating at the skating rink. Melanie and Malorie had apparently gone skating as well.

「Anyway, I’m a beginner snowboarder, but I can give you a bit of advice, so do you want to play together?」  

「Yup! Please do, Takumi-oniichan!」

Everyone rode the lift separately and headed up the hill.

It was a short trip because the lift wasn’t that high, but the children seemed to enjoy it and had fun.

When I gave a brief explanation of how to turn, Wappa and the kids listened once and started practicing on their own.

「Ah, if you turn all of a sudden like that, it would be dange-…… or not.」

With that simple explanation, then Wappa and the kids began sliding down normally. Even if the course was simple, they were far too good.

Colette and Shirona were doing the same, so it wasn’t because they were Catkins.

Well, this only applied to me but my body which was made especially by Goddess Norn was excellent, and it can do majority of things easily. And I can acquire skills fast because of it.

After climbing the lift and snowboarding down with the kids a few times, I stopped snowboarding and rubbed my eyes.

「How are they getting airtime……」

The kids started doing jumps using the small gaps. And it wasn’t just the older ones, even Sara, Lala, and Shirona were doing it.

Pulling myself together, I slid down to the kids who were waiting at the foot of the hill where they then asked me for ramps to jump off of.

「Please make some higher bumps we can jump off from.」  

「Make it nya.」  

「Ah, yeah, just don’t do anything too dangerous.」

Just in case, I built several ramps on one side of the course.

After going through the course several times, they started striking poses in the air.

「……no way, I didn’t think this was possible.」

Now that I think about it, Wappa and the kids went through some power leveling. Not only do they have higher physical abilities with their levels, they also possessed body control type skills.

If this is the standard of people in this world…… it’s not, right?

+++

# 633 - The Great Spirits have no limits

As I was snowboarding with the kids, the sanctuary residents began trickling in and playing with the snowboard and skis.

Even with skiing, I only gave a brief demonstration, but it seems like they’ve gotten the hang of it.  

It’s a relief how not everyone was like Wappa and the others though.

Not everyone in the Sanctuary power leveled, after all. Even so, they naturally have better physicality.

Perhaps it’s because they lived in harsh environments.

I went to see the skating rink beside the snow hill.

Sylph, Undine, Melanie, and Malorie should be skating there.

「…………eh!?」

I was surprised by the two Great Spirits skating over the rink.

It might have been because they were used to flying in the sky, but they glided elegantly on the ice rink, sometimes turning, spinning, and jumping…… at least a double rotation.

Melanie and Malorie were not skating like beginners either. They were gliding smoothly, and even skating backwards.

As I stood dumbfounded at the side of the rink, Malorie must have noticed as she did a full stop right next to me.

「Takumi-oniichan, what do you think? Malorie is good, right?」  

「Ah, yeah, you’ve gotten really good at this.」  

「Heheh.」

Malorie stood proud when I praised her.

It was then that her sister, Melanie, came.

「Takumi-oniichan, thank you very much. Ice skating is so fun.」  

「Y, yeah, it was all worth it if you’re having fun. But be careful not to get hurt, okay?」  

「「Yes!」」

You also had to be careful to not get injured skiing or snowboarding, but skating on hard ice is even more risky. Aside from hitting the ice, the blades of the ice skates were as sharp as knives, so caution was absolutely necessary.

「Don’t worry. I am here too, healing injuries would be a piece of cake.」  

「Oh? Selene, you came here to skate too?」  

「It’s not just me. Look, Nyx and Dryas are over there as well.」

When I looked in the direction Selene pointed towards, Nyx and Dryas waved their hands.

「The Great Spirits seem to like skating.」  

「Mhmm, it’s fun gliding over the ice.」  

「Gnome and Salamander don’t seem to be here though.」

The Great Spirits aside from Gnome and Salamander were having fun skating together.

「Gnome didn’t feel good jumping and spinning. Salamander, I have no clue.」  

「Wait wait, most skaters don’t do spins or jumps. That’s already at a competitive level.」  

「Oh, is that so? But that’s just based on your common sense. See, take a look at the rink.」

When I did as Selene said and looked around the rink, aside from Melanie and Malorie, there were plenty of elves who were enjoying skating.

「……a-amazing.」  

「Right?」

They weren’t quite at the level of the Great Spirits, but the Elves showed smooth skating movements that made it difficult to believe that it was their first time.

「Huh? Almost everyone skating here are elves. Could it be because Great Spirits are skating?」  

「That’s right. Elves show their reverence towards us especially, so they like to do the same thing we do.」

As Selene and I were talking, Sylph approached us at great speed.

Sha!

The sharp edge of her skates scraped the ice as she braked.

「Listen, listen, Takumi. Figure skating is performed to music, isn’t it? Please make a magic device that stores and plays music.」  

「You sure know a lot about figure skating. Did I ever talk about it?」  

「Isn’t it only natural? I am a Great Spirit… is what I would like to say. Actually, I had asked Goddess Norn to show me images of the world you came from.」  

「Eh!? She can do that?」  

「Of course, we are talking of the divine realm.」  

「I-is that so?」

I was surprised that the Great Spirits were able to come and go between this world and the divine realm, but I didn’t know they could see images of various things from my previous life.

「This divine realm, I can’t see it, right?」  

「Oh, is there something you want to see?」  

「Well~ I’ve been wanting to watch some anime I haven’t seen in a while.」  

「Well, perhaps Goddess Norn would let you see it when you die?」  

「Stop it, that’s so ominous.」  

「More importantly, could you hurry and make a magic device that stores and plays music?」  

「Fine. Even I want a music player. Just wait a bit.」

The Great Spirits’ skating should be magnificent. They’ve been able to see it, after all.

In order to create what Sylph requested, I returned to the mansion.  

I instructed everyone to return the equipment to their original places once they were done using them.

A music player, huh. The thought never occurred to me.

+++

# 634 - Music Player

I’ve decided to build a music player at Sylph’s request.

I returned to the mansion and went right to my workshop.

「Now, how should I record the sound?」

I could make a magic device that records the wavelength of sounds as is, then pair it with another magic device that plays back that recorded sound by vibrating the diaphragm of the speaker.

No, rather than a diaphragm, maybe I should etch a magic formation inlaid with a magic crystal? But maybe it’s better to keep the original form of the speakers.

First, I’ll need a mic to capture the sound, an amp to amplify the sound waves, and a speaker to play those sound waves.  

Since I don’t need to convert electric signals, the structure was simple.

「Time to make a prototype.」

I took out magic crystals, wood, and mithril ingots from my item box, and invoked my alchemy skill.

「『Transmute』!」

The shape of the prototype was simple.

It’s a box that holds an audio recording magic crystal which is connected to an amp by a mithril alloy cord, and two simple speakers.

「Alright, now to test it.」

I placed my hand on the magic crystal, channeled magic power into the recording magic formation and began recording.

「Test! Test! Test! Doing a test record right now! …………okay, I guess that should do it?」

I once again placed my hand on the magic crystal, and channeled magic power into the playback magic formation.

《Test! Test! Test! Doing a test record right now! …………okay, I guess that should do it?》

I heard my speakers on both the left and right speakers.

「Ohh, it’s a success.」

It functions. All that’s left is to check the recording time.

The record playback magic crystal could be overwritten and saved as many times as one likes, and it can be swapped out like cassette tapes.

「Still, they have to record something. I wonder what Sylph plans to do with this.」

I adjusted the design of the prototypes of the microphone, amplifier, and speaker, but I couldn’t help but wonder what kind of music they would be recording with it.

It’s not like they could buy CDs or download it from the internet, after all.

They would actually need to make the recording to make a CD.

「For now, I suppose I should make another mic.」

Sylph would probably end up saying that she needs a recording studio, but maybe I should prepare.

As I was thinking that, Sylph, who should have been skating, appeared.

「Uwaa, I’ve told you to stop appearing in my workshop so suddenly, haven’t I?」  

「You’ve said it a lot, but we Wind Spirits do as we wish. Anyway, that’s the magic device that saves music, right?」

Dismissing my criticism, Sylph just pointed towards the newly completed magic device.

「Sigh, whatever. Yeah, that’s it. I’ve just completed it, so it doesn’t have any music in it yet.」  

「Hmmm, you did say it records sounds. So, is it usable already?」  

「Of course, but what music are you going to record?」  

「Isn’t that obvious? That’s what the bands in the Sanctuary are for. Once they find out that they can save their own performances, they will happily oblige.」

Sylph had already reached out to the musicians.

The band members of the Sanctuary orchestra had a high percentage of elves. There were humans, dwarves, and mermaids as well, but the majority were the elves. On that note, the second highest were the mermaids.

What I meant by all this was that, if Sylph approached the elven musicians, they would definitely not refuse. This was a reflection of their deeply rooted faith in the Spirits.

「We’re going to record the performance in the music hall, yes?」  

「Actually, I’d like to record each individual instrument, then mix them for balance, but there is no time for that. This will just be for the background music for skating, after all.」

The moment Sylph said that each part would be recorded separately, I had to suppress my shock. I don’t want to get dragged into such a tedious task.  

Fortunately, Sylph was impatient.

「Okay, there’s no time to dillydally, Takumi. Bring the record magic device to the orchestra immediately.」  

「Right now……?」

Apparently, the band members had already assembled in the music hall.  

They were currently rehearsing, and Sylph told me to set up the recorder while they practiced.

Recording in the music hall turned out to be incredibly exhausting.

Sylph’s fussing was tolerable.  

The real problem was on the band members’ side.  

During the rehearsal, I recorded and played back their performance. When they realized that there would be a remnant of their performance, the band gave it their absolute all.

Well, their attention to every minute detail, they were relentless……

In the end, I had a late dinner by my lonesome.

+++

# 635 - Sylph’s Performance

With the long recording session over, I set the speakers up at the skating rink at Sylph’s request.

「Now, try playing the music for me.」  

「Okay.」

When I operated the magic device and played the song that was recorded yesterday, the music spread across the skating rink.

Confirming this, Sylph began sliding on the ice freely in sync to the music.

Perhaps having imagined it since the recording, no one would have thought the performance she displayed was her first.

The elves in particular were watching her fervently.

「Okay, I will skate for the entire song, music please.」  

「Understood!」

Sylph who had been rehearsing her skating choreography to sections of the music had asked me to play the song from the top.

When I fiddled with the magic music player, the orchestral music began playing through the speaker again.

As Sylph’s performance began in sync with the music, the onlookersー the Elves, the residents who were watching the skiers and snowboarders, and myselfー all watched, mesmerized.

I tend to forget because they always interact with us so casually all the time, but Sylph and the Great Spirits had unworldly beauty.  

Perhaps because of their existence, they inspired awe and the emotional impact of seeing a beautiful scenery, but they had no awareness of the opposite gender.

Such a being was tracing elegant lines on the ice.

Ahh, the elven women’s eyes were dangerous, they were sparkling. This was definitely going to become popular.  

Surely they wouldn’t turn the skating rink into a year-round facility.

After Sylph did a spin and step sequence, she displayed a series of jumps with I’m not sure how many rotations.

She was a Wind Spirit, flying in the sky was normal to her, so she performed jumps so naturally.

To the mesmerized elves, I think even you guys might find this difficult.

Was the length of the music also in her calculation? Sylph’s performance matched the song perfectly.

Once the musical performance was over, there was brief silence, then applause and cheers from the elves poured onto Sylph.

Looking very proud, Sylph waved at everyone as she skated over to me.

「Well? Don’t you think it was perfect?」  

「Well, there were so many amazing things, I just don’t know how to put it into words, but…… did you hear about it from Akane?」

No matter how I look at it, that was figure skating, so I tried asking if someone suggested it to her.

「That’s not it. I told you that Goddess Norn showed me images in the Divine Realm. I saw all sorts of performance competitions.」  

「S-so it was that.」

Anything is possible with Goddess Norn, huh.

As Sylph and I were chatting, the Elves began practicing spins and jumps.

「Uwaa, I hope you know that this is a winter-only facility.」  

「If Undine and I are here, it wouldn’t be difficult to maintain this year-round.」  

「……so it’s going to be a year-round thing.」

So it seems they were going to maintain it all year long by sheer brute force. May as well leave it to those two since they volunteered.

「Takumi, please play the music on loop until the magic crystal runs out. It would be better for everyone to have some background music.」  

「Gotcha, when the magic power runs out, you’ll have to replace it yourselves.」  

「Fine. Do it please.」

At Sylph’s request, I set it so the recorded music continues to play on loop, then left the skating rink.

The skating in the Sanctuary had evolved to a level far different from the fun skating I knew, they were showing some pro level figure skating.

Sylph and the Great Spirits would probably get bored and move on to other things eventually, but the Elves had a bit of monomania, so the skating boom will continue for a while.

By the time the winter chill waned and spring took its first steps, the snow hill was already gone, and the lift was removed.

Wappa and the kids understood that skiing and snowboarding were winter sports, so there were no unreasonable requests to maintain the snow hill once it started getting warmer.

Incidentally, the elves who had fallen in love with figure skating had gotten various other songs recorded since then, and a considerable number still continue to skate.

Soon, the long-awaited spring would finally arrive in the Sanctuary.

+++

# 636 - The Arrival of Spring

The bloom of various flowers on the expanse of grasslands in the east signaled the arrival of spring.

The cherry blossom tree that was planted in my Sanctuary mansion garden seemed like it was about to bloom.

「We can finally have tea in the garden now that it has gotten warmer.」  

「Truly, look, the cherry blossoms are about to bloom.」  

「This cherry blossom tree is splendid. It will look so lovely in full bloom.」

Madam Rosary, Madam Elizabeth, and Madam Lumia were having tea in the garden while my children were on their lap.

Why were they in my house?

A few days later, the cherry blossoms began blooming all at once in the Sanctuary.

These trees were a bit special.

The speed of the bloom from bud to flower was quick, and the length of that full bloom was long.

Dryas said “Wouldn’t it be nice to see them bloom for a long time~”.

「Still, we should be grateful to Dryas.」  

「Yeah, seeing these cherry blossoms, it reminds me of Japan.」  

「Lulu loves cherry blossoms too nya.」

In the mansion’s garden, the flowers dotting the branches of the cherry blossom tree were fully open.

As a former Japanese man, seeing cherry blossoms always touched my heart. It seems Akane felt the same way, she was unusually quiet as she admired the flowers.

「There are cherry blossoms in the Royal Capital, Volton, and Rockford, but the one here is the best.」  

「Truly, cherry blossoms in full bloom are magnificent.」  

「I would love to have some in Yggurle Kingdom as well.」

And, as if it was the most natural event, Madam Rosary, Madam Elizabeth, and Madam Lumia were elegantly drinking tea and viewing the flowers on the table set in my garden.

The madams did their administrative work better than others, leaving no room for complaints.

As nobility and royalty, they were masterful in managing the civil officials in the new government office.

In the lawn, Haruka and Etoile were crawling.

Haruka and Etoile recently learned to crawl, and they seemed like they were having fun.

However, Sophia and Maria who were following Etoile and Haruka were having a hard time keeping up.

Meanwhile, Flora had been running around since her legs are stronger, though she still falls down often because her balance wasn’t that good yet, which was why Marnie always kept a watchful eye on her.

I was also interacting with the kids while eating the snacks that Maria and Maribelle prepared and drinking alcohol.

Though I’m not very good with alcohol, with the best location and the perfect situation, I felt like having a drink.

「Takumi-sama, the wine is running low.」  

「Wait a bit, I’ll bring more out right away.」

Laeva said she felt good and wanted to drink today, so she was eating food and guzzled down the wine.

「Takumi-sama, your glass is empty. Have some more.」  

「Ah, thanks Fluna-san.」  

「Ah! That’s not fair, Fluna-san! Please let me pour some for you!」  

「W-wait, Berkut, calm down!」

Today, it wasn’t only Fluna-san who came by, even Berkut did.

Fluna-san lived by the sea in the Sanctuary, so she would occasionally give gifts of seafood and have exchanges with us sometimes. But it was rare for Berkut to visit the Sanctuary.
