Normally, we would meet when I go to the Demon Continent base, or in the Sky Island, but she dropped by the Sanctuary this time.

Since there were more things to enjoy in the Sanctuary now, Berkut probably wanted to come by.

◇

A slight distance away from Takumi, the three mothers who were taking care of the children were whispering to each other.

「Takumi-sama hasn’t noticed Berkut and Fluna-san’s feelings, hasn’t he?」  

「Maria, that’s just how Takumi-sama is.」  

「Still, Sophia-san, that just makes Fluna-san and Berkut even more pitiful.」

Fluna and Berkut’s feelings towards Takumi were obvious to everyone around them, but Takumi himself hadn’t noticed.

「Takumi-sama is oblivious, after all. Well, that’s another thing that makes him adorable, though.」  

「Indeed. He isn’t like that with other people, but he becomes dense the moment it’s about him.」  

「With Takumi-sama, you’d have to be direct with your approach and close the distance, after all.」  

「Ahh, so that’s how it was for you.」

As they were already wives and mothers to his children, the three were at ease as they watched over Berkut and Fluna-san.

Since their own encounters with Takumi were under unique circumstances, they didn’t have the normal progression to romance. And that was why they looked upon Berkut and Fluna with warm, gentle eyes.

+++

# 637 - Fruit of the Flesh Tree

At the same time when the cherry blossom flowers began blooming in the Sanctuary and Valkyra Kingdom, in a ghost town in what was once the border territory of Sydnia which was in the middle of the continent, there was a tree with a bizarre flower.

Chomp, chomp

There was the sound of something chewing fruit in the abandoned church.

「Oh my, Lord Baal, you were in the middle of your meal?」

A sultry voice could be heard. If it wasn’t for her skin color, one would think a normal bewitching lady entered the abandoned church.

「Oh Gremory, were you scavenging for men again?」

The grey-skinned child named Baal looked exasperated.

Yes, that child…… the child of the Evil Spirit born from the Flesh Tree, Baal, had already grown to be around 8-10 years of age.

「Don’t cause too much of a scene. We still can’t afford to stand out right now.」  

「I understand, Lord Baal. I do it properly and change towns. I make sure to keep it to ten people at every town.」

Hearing this, Baal shook his head.

「It depends on the size of the town. If consecutive suspicious deaths happen in a single town, people would be on full alert.」  

「Oh my, I am not that foolish, Lord Baal. I make sure to spread out the days and transfer between places.」  

「That’s not something to be say so confidently, you fool.」

Gremory puffed her well endowed chest announcing that she thought about it thoroughly, resounding throughout the hall.

「Ah, you’re back, Agares?」  

「Yes, Lord Baal. Agares has just returned.」

The one who entered the abandoned church was Agares who appeared to be a typical old man with exception to his skin color.

「Gremory, until we have fully regained our strength, do not travel between towns and villages unnecessarily.」  

「Now, now Agares, Gremory’s hunt for men is rooted in by her instincts. It wouldn’t be ideal if we are too conspicuous, but we can overlook it ever so slightly.」  

「Hmm, if Lord Baal says so.」

Gremory nodded reluctantly when Baal said so.

「Oh what’s this, you finally thought to come back, seed sucker?」  

「Who’s a seed sucker!?」

It was then that Buer, who appeared to be an intellectual civil official, had come back to the abandoned church.  

Then as soon he saw Gremory, who hadn’t come back in a while, he mocked her.

「Our matters should not be reported to the surrounding nations. If we were to be reported, our surrounding countries would come for us simultaneously. Considering this, your actions are far too reckless.」  

「Lord Baal and Agares scolded me for the same thing just now, I don’t want to hear it from you too.」  

「Oh, Lord Baal. Please forgive me for my impertinent behavior.」

Buer made an exaggerated apology and bowed towards Baal.

「Kukuku, leave her be. Gremory will exercise restraint from now on.」

Baal said so to Buer, and chewed on the fruit he was holding.

「The growth of the fruits are well.」  

「Yes, by the time the Great Tree withers, I should have grown to my complete form.」

Seeing the fruit Baal was chewing, Buer then glanced at the Flesh Tree.

The gigantic Flesh Tree continued to grow until Baal was born, but once he was, the Flesh Tree was steadily getting smaller.

According to Baal, by the time this Flesh Tree shrinks and withers, it would have fulfilled its role.

「The truth is, we can only eat five- maybe six at most.」  

「It can’t be helped. Each time one of these fruits is produced, the Mother Tree grows smaller.」

The fruit produced by the Flesh Tree that Baal was eating was a bundle of solidified malice, miasma, and magic power.

If given to normal monsters, their bodies would likely explode.

Even for executives such as Agares and Buer, eating five or six was the limit, as eating more would cause them to burst, dying with not a single trace.

「By the way, how is the concealment barrier covering this town?」  

「Agares and I strengthened the barrier, it shouldn’t be affected from the outside. Assuming they do approach the barrier, they would likely not perceive it.」  

「Fumu, as expected of you, Buer.」  

「Agares and I specialize in intellectual work, not physical labor.」  

「He’s right, Milord. We are unlike that immoral woman and meathead.」  

「You wrinkly old man, Agares! Who are you calling an immoral woman!?」  

「I thought there was only one woman among the executives, am I wrong?」  

「Agares!!」  

「Enough! Agares, Gremory, cease your quarreling in front of me. Agares, watch your mouth.」  

「「My apologies.」」

After scolding Agares and Gremory who began quarreling, Baal sighed.

「I prohibit any fighting amongst comrades.」  

「「「Yes.」」」

Agares, Buer, and Gremory fell to their knees and groveled in apology.

A tiny portion of the continent had hidden itself from society, as though detached from the rest of the world.

When it appears again, disaster will strike the continent.

+++

# 638 - Fluna’s Request

When the cherry blossoms bloomed in our garden, all the cherry blossoms in the central district of the Sanctuary were also in full bloom.

The citizens of the Sanctuary enjoyed the flower viewing.

My daughters had become more energetic, and Sophia, Maria, and Marnie were busy parenting.

They continued to raise the children and participate in combat training.

They were reconditioning their bodies after it weakened from pregnancy and childbirth, and even though they had already regained their combat senses, they continued to train with me.

One peaceful spring day, Fluna came to the mansion, asking to receive some combat training.

「U-um, is that not possible?」  

「What’s the matter? Sea monsters can’t come through the barrier, right?」  

「Isn’t it fine? There’s no downside to Fluna getting strong too.」  

「Eh?」

For some reason, Akane suddenly told me to train Fluna-san.

「Fluna has been the leader of the Mermaids since a young age, so if she is able to strengthen her leadership, they can fish beyond the barrier of the Sanctuary. In such times, I’d say strength is a necessity.」  

「……well, what you say makes sense.」

The merfolk generally fish within the protective barrier and produce salt. However, it was also a possibility to fish beyond the border, huh?

「I suppose fishing in the ocean would let us catch plenty of big fish.」  

「Y-yes, that’s right! Right now, we basically only run away when we encounter monster, but if I were to become stronger, we would be able to fish safely!」

The moment I said there were larger fish in the deep sea, Fluna-san eagerly insisted that she needed to become stronger.

「Takumi-sama, wouldn’t it be better if you were to train with Berkut?」  

「That’s right, Takumi-sama. If you are together with Berkut, the burden on you would lessen.」  

「Indeed. It might be better to raise their levels to a certain extent in one go. If Berkut is there, she could fill in for when we’re not around.」  

「…………」

For some reason, Sophia, Maria, and Marnie were pushing for me to train Fluna-san together with Berkut.

There was no fault in what they were saying either.  

Berkut hunts monsters around our base in the Demon Continent, and she’s undergone some power leveling before this, so she should have been more than enough to train Fluna-san, but the three said it wouldn’t hurt to accompany them either.

With Kaede, Berkut, and myself, we could venture into high a slightly higher difficulty dungeon from the start.

「Okay, understood.」  

「Thank you very much!」  

「That’s great, Fluna-san.」  

「Do your best.」  

「You have nothing to worry about, Takumi-sama will protect you.」  

「Thank you very much. Sophia-san, Marnie-san, Maria-san!」

Fluna-san, Sophia, Maria, and Marnie were all holding hands in delight. Since when have they been this close?

「Takumi, could you make equipment for Fluna so she doesn’t get injured?」  

「Ah, yeah, of course, I can’t take someone without armor or equipment to a dungeon.」

Akane asked me to prepare equipment for Fluna-san.

Mermaid gear, huh…… sounds fun.

「Fluna-san, why don’t we head into the workshop so you can try our weapons and decide which one you like?」  

「Yes! Please!」  

「Well then, we’re stopping by the workshop for a bit.」

I had a stockpile of unused weapons and armor that I made for everyone in m workshop. There, she can choose her preferred equipment.

I teleported to the workshop with Fluna-san.

◇

Seeing Fluna and Takumi disappear to the workshop, Akane, Sophia, Marnie, and Maria sighed.

「Seriously, what a blockhead.」  

「Well, that’s one of Takumi-sama’s good qualities.」  

「That’s right. It’s a hundred times better than being a womanizer.」  

「Our relationship is a bit different from normal romances.」  

「You guys are far too generous with Takumi.」

The four knew about Fluna and Berkut’s feelings for Takumi.  

Akane had secretly confirmed Fluna’s feelings, and Berkut didn’t even try to hide her affection.

Even so, it wasn’t that Takumi disliked them, it was just that he didn’t have romantic feelings for them.

The three wives thought that, for someone of Takumi’s status, having one or two concubines was only natural. And if those partners were Fluna and Berkut, they would very likely get along, so they fully supported it.

At present, Sophia, Maria, and Marnie had recovered from their weakened bodies and dulled battle senses. They were also raising their levels, but even then, the children took precedence, so they wanted companions aside from Kaede to be by Takumi’s side.

Takumi was the type of person to give 120% of his strength when he has people to protect. That said, they did not want to male companions near them.

To Sophia and the others, Fluna and Berkut not only fit their requirements, they welcomed the two as companions considering their natures.

The problem, if there had to be a problem, was that only Takumi didn’t understand this……

+++

# 639 - Fluna’s Equipment

When they arrived at the workshop, I took out weapons such as one-handed swords, two-handed swords, spears, maces, axes, and others from where I stored the stock in.

「Considering surface combat and underwater combat, it would be difficult to wield one-handed and two-handed swords.」  

「Yes. The same with axes and maces.」

It was impossible to swing swords and maces with the drag from water resistance.

「So that leaves a spear, huh. You wouldn’t be able to swing it either, but I think you should be able to focus on thrusts.」  

「Also, knives and daggers seem like they could work underwater.」  

「Yes, it should be usable with the short blade of a dagger or knife.」

The reason I imagined a spear as Fluna-san’s weapon was because I was inspired by the Poseidon’s trident.

Then I made Fluna-san try out the spear, dagger, and knife.

Upon observation of her movements, I noticed something that could be considered a weakness unique to Mermaids.

「Oh I see, is it because Fluna-san is a Mermaid? Her footwork is clumsy.」  

「Urk, my apologies.……」  

「Sorry, I’m not critizing you.」

While trying to console the discouraged Fluna, I thought she needed combat training on land.

The Mermaids have demonstrated excellent mobility underwater, but on ground, they were only mobile enough to not impede on their daily lives.

「Even so, your race has high physical capabilities.」  

「Yes. We are capable of swim at high speeds underwater.」

That makes sense. Swimming is a very intense exercise, and the mermaids were capable of swimming fast for extended periods of time.

I gave her a brief lesson on how to handle spears, then asked her to practice the forms.  

If she had the aptitude for the spear, then by repeatedly practicing with proper form, it shouldn’t take long for her to acquire the skill.

Underwater, thrusts would likely be the main attack pattern, but I had her practice sweeping attacks and pommel strikes too.

After all, even though Fluna-san’s battlefield would mainly be underwater, the dungeons we’ll be leveling up in were all above ground.

「Ah! I learned the Spear Technique skill!」

After watching Fluna-san practice for a while, she suddenly yelled.

「Fluna-san, you might actually have the knack for the spear. Okay, shall we try getting the dagger or knife skill?」  

「Yes!」

Ecstatic from having obtained the spear skill, Fluna-san eagerly switched to a dagger.

While she trained with the dagger, I thought about the specifications for her possible weapons.

A spearhead that’s specialized for thrusts might be good.

Maybe it would be better if it could also slash when used on land? Thinking so, the trident seemed unfeasible.

For a Japanese-style spear, it would have to be the omi-yari, a long-blade spear. There was also the kama-yari for Japanese-style weapons.

A kama-yari had a cross-shaped spear tip, with a sickle-shaped blade protruding like a branch.  

I would need to arrange one for Fluna-san’s use, but I wonder if a single or double branching kamayari would be better.

To me, this was mostly a matter of personal preference.

If she wanted minimal water resistance underwater, it would probably be better to not have the sickle blade part.

Even so, I’ll have to experiment on the length of the sickle blade’s length and curvature to find the optimal shape that could be used with very little difficulty underwater.

The materials for the spearhead and shaft had to water resistant too. Of course, I could would waterproof it with an enchantment, but we should use highly water resistant materials nonetheless.

「Ah! I’ve obtained the Dagger Technique skill!」  

「Woah, Fluna-san, you really are a natural.」

I had only taught her a bit of footwork and body movements, and she had just practiced swings and forms, but given how she had already acquired the skill for a short time, she may actually have some decent battle sense.

Eventually, Fluna-san had chosen the kama-yari and a large knife for her weapons.

However, the problem was with her armor.

「Even light armor would be a hindrance underwater, wouldn’t it?」  

「That’s right. Generally, when we go into the sea, we only use swimsuits.」

Oh yeah. Before they moved into the Sanctuary, there were some that didn’t even wear bikini top swimwear. Nowadays, whenever they went on walks around the Sanctuary, they were using normal clothing, but……

Laeva came in while I was agonizing in the workshop.

「Are you troubled by something?」  

「Ahh, it’s you, Laeva. I was thinking about Fluna-san’s armor, but……」  

「I see, a functional armor that’s easy to move in even underwater, it seems interesting. Laeva wants to assist.」  

「Thank you, Laeva. I’ve done all I could by myself, you’re really doing me a solid.」

After that, Fluna-san herself joined us to brainstorm for armor ideas, and we somehow eventually managed to decide on a direction.

We would make gauntlets and a chestplate with a generally water resistant design. The chestplate was made into a bustier shape by Laeva and Fluna-san. In addition to that, we were providing shoulder guards, though minimal in size. She would be too defenseless if there wasn’t anything on her shoulders.

The problem was regarding the unique lower half of the Mermaids’ bodies, so we decided on special miniskirt-type armor.

This skirt-type armor had a form transformation gimmick.

The miniskirt-type armor splits side-to-side and front-to-back, so it can be deployed and attached to a special fabric inside the armor to instantly transform into spats the instant it is on land.

As for the color and finer details, it seems like Laeva and Fluna-san decide after some consultation.

I was hands off on that part of the design. I’m not confident in my fashion sense.

+++

# 640 - Fluna and Berkut

Fluna’s armor was something that Laeva and I created quite satisfactorily.

The shape changing armor in particular was a necessity to Fluna-san, so it was absolutely essential that we finished it no matter what.

After all, Fluna-san was a mermaid.

Underwater, her lower body transforms into a fish tail.

There would have been no problem if that condition was constant, but once she gets out of the water and comes up to land, her lower fish half turns into human lower parts, and areas that shouldn’t be seen would be fully exposed.

That would definitely be unfavorable for women of age.

Moreover, she needed boots when on land, but they were a nuisance underwater.

We eventually devised it so that the boots turn into accessories the moment her lower half becomes that of a fish.

As a result, we were able to incorporate Laeva and Fluna-san’s preferred design, and I think we created a satisfactory product.  

However, even though they were made with the finest materials,

we installed magic crystals onto her weaponsー the knife and the sickle spearー to strengthen the Water attribute which was the Mermaids’ racial attribute.

Then Kaede and I went into dungeon with Fluna-san and Berkut.

We were entering a highly difficult dungeon.

「Takumi-sama, Fluna-san’s armor is really pretty, could you please make me a pretty one too~」  

「No, it would be really bad if you were in a miniskirt. Your underwear would show if you fly into the sky.」  

「In that case, I can just wear spats like Fluna-san does, can’t I?!」

Berkut saw Fluna-san’s armor and said she wanted a cute design for herself too.  

I didn’t think that armor needed to be cute though.

It was then that Berkut said that it should be fine as long as she wore spats, but to me, even if she wore spats underneath her miniskirt, it was still too much if she were to fly around with her skirt exposed.

「U-umm, Takumi-sama.」  

「Hm? What’s the matter, Fluna-san?」  

「U-umm, you address Berkut-san without honorifics, but you add -san to me? Would it be possible for you to call me simply by Fluna as well?」  

「Eh? Umm, is that fine?」  

「Yes!」

I treated Berkut like a disciple ever since I first met her, so I dropped honorifics with her before I realized it, but when I first met Fluna-san, she was someone I had to shelter. Maybe that’s why I felt like I had to keep her at a distance.

「Umm, is it fine if I address you as Fluna?」  

「Yes!」  

「Good for you, Fluna-san.」  

「Thank you! Berkut-san, please drop honorifics with me too please.」  

「Okay Fluna, call me Berkut too.」  

「Very well, Berkut.」

Fluna and Berkut held hands and smiled warmly, but…… we’re inside a dungeon……

Unlike the two who had no feeling of tension, Kaede, who had been in charge of searching for enemies, began talking to me.

「Master, Kaede will lure the monsters, okay~」  

「Please do.」

Kaede said that then ran towards a passageway in the dungeon without making a sound.

Since there were no monsters within my detection range, I asked Kaede to handle it.

This dungeon was one of the many high level dungeons in the Demon Continent, and it had very few large monsters like Dragon-types, but it did have a lot of monsters that would serve training for Fluna’s combat skills.  

It was the type of dungeon that descends and had a fairly typical structure with large rooms, small rooms, and tunnel pathways.

There’s a few grassland-type levels interposed between the floors but there wasn’t much pattern to it.

I sensed the presence of Kaede and the lured monsters coming from the front.

「Fluna, Berkut, prepare for battle!」  

「「Yes!」」

We saw Kaede coming.

「Master, three Orc Generals!」  

「Thanks Kaede! Take out of them!」  

「Okay!」

When Kaede reached us, she turned around.

I could hear the rough, uneven snorting of the approaching Orc Generals who was one size larger than normal orcs.

「Then after Kaede deals with one of them, the rest will be up to you, okay~!」

The moment after Kaede said so, the Orc General at the very back suddenly turned into a pile of meat.

「They’re coming! Ready your spears! Now!」

Given her experience, Berkut smoothly stabbed the throat of the Orc General using her spear. Meanwhile, Fluna was nervous enough that her movements were stiff, but she stabbed the Orc General’s throat.

Berkut didn’t have any help, but Fluna was supported by Kaede’s threads.

Obviously, it would be impossible challenge if Fluna, who wasn’t used to fighting, had no support.

The Orc Generals whose throats were pierced died from it.

The spears were powerful, the Orc General that Berkut had defeated was one, but even the Orc General that Fluna fought had its neck nearly severed.

「Good work. Let’s continue hunting more.」  

「「Yes!」」

Now then, I think I would like to reach the middle floors.

++++

# Cave King – 276 – It Was Perfect!

---

The day after the fall of the fortress.

We were visiting the Arubal Company store in Lushika.

A merchant and well-dressed young man were standing in front of a shelf filled with precious stones.

“…What about this ring, which has a great, beautiful pearl? I am sure that the lady will like it.”  

“Oh, quite wonderful!! However, it is rather expensive…”  

“I am terribly sorry… But, if I may tell you a little secret, our craftsmen make jewelry for the royal family. And these items are only available once a year.”  

“Is that so! Well, I suppose she will like it then…”  

“There is no doubt about it. On top of that, this is your lucky day. I am sure you will get the answer you are hoping for.”  

“In-indeed… I will buy it then!”  

“Thank you!”

Alva was dealing with customers.

It was the same as always. Nothing strange. Both employees and customers would think that.

However, this was not the real Alva. It was actually Number 15.

“It looks like he is doing it well.”  

“Yes. No one would even suspect it.”

Rienna said with a nod. Fule chuckled.

“It is almost scary how good it is… I’m glad that Number 15 is on our side.”

It wasn’t just appearance. The way he talked, mannerisms and posture. All of his habits. Number 15 had replicated them perfectly.

“Yes. Now, as long as everything goes according to plan, we will be able to uncover the real villain.”  

“Alva talked about the company, didn’t he?”

I nodded at Fule.

“He even told us how to open the hidden vault at their headquarters. Apparently, it holds assets equivalent to an entire year of the kingdom’s national budget.”

Alva was very cooperative. During the interrogation, he told us about the company structure, their funds and contacts, rivalries within the company as well as secrets of the various officials.

Perhaps he thought that it would put himself in a better position.

However…

Rienna tilted her head to the side and answered.

“Still, he did not say the name of the person who hired them to do it… Besides, the company has so much money already.”  

“Normally, they would not accept such a job. Perhaps the president had a weakness that they knew about?”

I answered Fule’s question.

“That is possible… According to Alva, this president is a very cautious man. There are no negative rumors about him. And so if there was something bad behind the scenes, he would want to hide it.

“So this president is known for being a virtuous person?”

Rienna asked. I nodded.

“Aye. He sends donations to temples and poor towns and villages every year. He has even helped orphans and gave them jobs in the company.”  

“People like that who are actually villains behind the scenes… It’s not that uncommon.”

Claimed Fule.

“Perhaps… But the president has funds that match the national budget. It would be difficult to manipulate someone like that.”

“In other words, this person must be very powerful.”

“Yes. Also…”  

“Also?”

“While a normal merchant would turn it down, what if he is not a normal merchant? He may be different from what we, or even Alva are thinking. Perhaps he readily agreed to this plan. In fact, he could be the true person who is behind it.”

“So, it wasn’t something he was forced to do.”

Said Rienna.

“In any case, we will have to look into this matter. Apparently, Alva had received orders about what to do if the plan ran into any problems. He was to go to the royal capital directly and make a report to the president.”

“Then…Number 15…Alva, will have to go.”  

“Yes. We will send a carriage tomorrow. However, we should leave today, in order to take the lead…”

I looked out of the window.

There were a lot of people, and the streets were lively.

“They are celebrating the defeat of the bandits… Apparently, not just here, but in the other Leodor lands as well.”

“And as the hero, you cannot leave yet, Lord Heal.”

Rienna and Fule said with a smile.

“Hero. That’s an exaggeration…”

In fact, it seemed like there were people who called me that in the town.

The bandits of the Nostor mountain had been the biggest problem in the Leodor territory. So it was no wonder that the residents were happy.

However, I was not happy. The true enemy was undiscovered. And we were hiding the truth from everyone.

Of course, once this was all over, Alva’s crimes would become known. But I still did not know what to do about the device.

That’s why I could not celebrate.

In Langs, I had also lied about my identity. I was no good at lying. And so I had a lot of respect for Number 15, who could do it so perfectly.

However, this was all for Rish and the Leodor lands. If I wanted to get attention from the villains, then perhaps it was best to look like a dumb prince who was drunk on his victory.

“In any case…let’s go and meet Rish. She should be in the plaza.”  

“Yes!”

I nodded towards Number 15 and then left the building.

We walked through the festive streets.

The buildings and trees were decorated in bright cloth and flowers. There were barrels and wooden tables laid with food and drink. The people of Lushika raised their cups and celebrated.

Eventually, their faces turned towards me.

“Ah, if it isn’t Lord Heal!”

“All hail, Lord Heal!”

I waved my hand at them.

“Lord Heal. You look tense! You should smile more, like this! Yes! Is everyone having a good time?!”

Fule waved both arms in the air and smiled. The men of the town cheered in response.

…It seemed like she would fit in better here than me.

We continued on our way until we arrived at the plaza where many of the people were gathered. The smell of delicious food and drink was in the air, and people were dancing in the center.

I saw Rish holding a cup.

She was talking to someone, but excused herself when she saw us.

“Heal…! Your Highness. I am glad that you are here!”

“People seem to be enjoying themselves.”  

“Yes! This all because of you, Lord Heal. On behalf of my father and the people, I thank you!”

Rish said with a bow. As she was in front of people, she spoke more clearly and confidently than usual.

We had told her about our plan to use a fake Alva. And that we would be heading to the royal capital soon. 

Speaking of Alva, he had been sent to the Leodor frontiers. He would live in a small remote village in the mountains, where he would be monitored.

“I just did my duty as the prince… People of Lushika!”

I said loudly while raising a cup that was on a nearby wooden crate.

“I, Lord Heal, have removed the threat of the bandits!! From now on, you can return to your days of peace!!”

The people cheered and raised their cups as well. After that, they chanted ‘Heal! Heal!’ over and over again.

Fireworks explode in the sky above, decorating the air with various flowers.

“Oh, how beautiful!”

“I’Ve never seen fireworks so big before.”  

“Who made them?”

As the townspeople raised their voices in awe, Mappa looked a little embarrassed.

Apparently, he was the one who made them. I had a feeling that for the people here, the fireworks would be more memorable than me.

In any case, the festival was a great success.

Surely word would spread throughout the country now. The useless prince had defeated the impregnable Nostor fortress. All eyes would turn towards ms.

As I thought of such things, a sad voice echoed next to me.

“How beautiful…”

Rish was looking up at the sky.

At first, her eyes were bright, but she looked lonely now.

“Rish…”  

“…Huh? What? Um, what is it, Your Highness?”

“They won’t hear you with the fireworks. You can talk normally.”  

“Uh, yes. So, what is it?”  

“Well, about us going to the capital. I think you should wait here. I think we can deal with it by ourselves now.”  

“Heal… You are still worried about me.”

Rish looked a little happy, but shook her head.

“I’m fine. For Leodor as well, I need to end this.”  

“I see…”

After a short pause, Rish opened her mouth.

“More importantly, your friends really are amazing, Heal.”  

“I don’t mean to brag, but they really are. I couldn’t do anything alone. I am blessed to have them.”

This plan would not have worked without their help. It was always like that.

“Did you meet all of them in Sheorl?”

“Aye, that’s right. They took a liking to Sheorl. It’s a good place. With a beautiful sea…”

There was a lot that I was hiding from Rish. And so I was happy when there were questions that I could answer honestly.

“It must be a nice place… Will you take me there one day?”

“Of course. There are so many places that I want to show you.”

Rish said happily.

“Yes! Alright, next time, I’ll guide you to secret spots in Leodor too.”

“I’m looking forward to it.”

Once things settled down, I hoped that we could talk about the past together.

At the same time, when I saw her talking about Leodor, it reminded me about how much I missed Sheorl. I hoped that everyone was well.

As the fireworks died down, I heard screams erupt in the plaza.

When I turned my head, I saw the male customer that Alva had been talking to earlier. He was now kneeling in front of a woman and offering the pearl ring.

“I love you! Please marry me!!”

The woman’s eyes welled up with tears and she nodded.

So it was a success.

People cheered and clapped. 

Only God knew whether the ring actually helped him. Still, it was a nice thing to see.

“What a relief…”

I muttered, and then shocking words reached my ears.

“Prince Heal! You should marry Lady Rish too!!”

“Lady Rish is such a wonderful person! You will make a great couple!!”

Both Rish and I were stunned.  

Other people agreed and whistled.

Rish turned bright red and fired back.

“Ho-how insolent of you! The very idea of someone like me marrying the prince!! As-as kind, gentle and handsome as he is…”

Our eyes met, and then she covered her face with her hands.

Why was she reacting like that? It was making me feel embarrassed too.

This was bad. And so I turned to Mappa.

“Ma-Mappa!! More fireworks!”

Mappan grinned and stared back at me quietly. Apparently, he was enjoying seeing me flustered.

“Hey! Mappa! I need your help!”

I said more loudly.

And so Mappa shrugged and waved his hand towards the outside of the plaza. And then the giant fireworks exploded again.

“I see… Well, that settles it, Fule.”  

“Indeed. And she is very welcome.”

“We can talk about it when everything is finished!”

Rienna and Fule smiled.

I had no idea what they were talking about.

Regardless, the festivities continued after that.

And then the next day…

We set out ahead of Number 15,  and made our way to the royal capital by carriage.

+++

277 – The Royal Capital!!

---

After departing Lushika, we headed for the royal capital.

The carriage was currently rushing down the road to the south.

Number 15, who had taken the appearance of Alva, would follow us later. This would give me time to look into the Arubal Company and the president before they met.

Besides, it was possible that the president and culprit’s people were still in Lushika. And it was important to fool them by going at different times.

Furthermore, Rish would also go to Lushika after a short delay.

She had only reported to Count Leodor that the bandits had been defeated, and that she was going to the city in order to meet Elserd. She did not tell him about the device or the Arubal Company. And that showed that she trusted me.

The journey was peace itself. The road to the royal capital was protected by the royal Knights Order, and so there was little chance of seeing monsters or bandits during the day.

Not only that, but there were plenty of places to stop, and it was not difficult to find an inn. As the carriage was so comfortable, they did not really need a room. However, since it offered opportunities to enjoy food and shopping, they decided to stay at an inn for the night.

In the meantime, they contacted Sheorl through the golems. Things were well on the other side. Of course, we had also told them what we were doing now.

And like that, after a week of traveling, we were able to see the giant city from the window.

“It’s so big…”  

“I’ve seen many cities before, but this one is different.”  

Rienna and Fule were in awe.

Even Mappa looked impressed. He began to draw the scene onto a canvas.

I understood the feeling of wanting to capture it.

A city with white towers that pierced the sky. The gray walls around loomed like mountains that extended into the horizon. Outside of the city, there were endless fields and other large towns.

This was the city where the ruler of all of Sanfaris lived. And it was my homeland.

I turned to the others.

“Is it really your first time here?”

“I saw it a few times from far away. It’s hard to miss.”  

“You can really feel the size when you are closer…”  

“Yes. It has the highest population of any city on this continent…no, the entire world.”

It was also one of the oldest cities. In fact, no one knew who first came and settled here.

“It’s been a long time since I was here. But it really is big…”  

“We should make Sheorl into a city that can match it.”  

“While there is nothing wrong with big cities, Sheorl has its own special charm.”

I nodded to Rienna.

“A place that is lively with a lot of people is great. But it can also lead to problems.”  

“Indeed, now that you mention it. Just feeding everyone would be hard… Oh, where are we going to stay tonight?”

“I doubt there is a room for me at the palace these days. And so we should search for an inn or a cheap house.”

Rienna said,

“Inns are nice, but the freedom of a house is also appealing.”  

“Indeed. Especially if the investigation takes longer than expected. A house might end up being cheaper. And considering the possibility of using it as a base for Sheorl, a large building would be best.”

I thought for a moment and then continued.

“Our first priority is investigating the Arubal Company. And so we should finish the search for a house today. If we cannot find one, then we will just get a room at an inn.”  

“Yes. The president may be acting already.”

“Well, he should be more cautious than Alava and Berido were…”

I doubted we would find any evidence. Still, it was worth a look.

Fule said,

“But…we should get the layout of the company if we want to witness the conversation between the president and Number 15.”

“And I would like to see what kind of person he is. Perhaps we could meet your father after that?”

I nodded at Rienna.

“Yes. Regardless, I cannot meet my father immediately. Even royals have to request an audience first. Besides, he never meets people he does not have business with. Though, I doubt he would refuse to meet me… But he also leaves the city quite often.”

Fule chuckled.

“…He even hid in the cargo and came all of the way to Sheorl.”

“That really was a surprise. I thought kings were supposed to stay in their palace… Perhaps they have a double who takes their place.”  

“I never thought about it, but it is possible… Well, anyway. We will deal with my father later. Right now, we must focus on the Arubal Company.”

As we talked like this, the city gates came into view. The stone gates seemed much too large for humans. They were big enough for the giant Mappa statue in Sheorl to go through.

Around the gates, there were great lines of carriages and people who were coming or going.

Some of them were looking curiously at the carriage.

“What a great carriage…”  

“I wonder who is inside…”  

“It must be someone from the royal family.”

“The two women are very pretty.”  

“But the man is so plain.”

Rienna scowled.

“Why, I… But there is no one as impressive as Lord Heal. I think the people here must be blind.”  

“Now, now, Princess. We all know that it is what’s inside Lord Heal that really matters.”  

Fule didn’t bother to deny the accusation of looking plain…

Mappa continued to look happy and draw the scenes around him. He must be happy to hear the praise for the carriage that he made. 

Regardless, we soon made our way into the city.

Inside, there was a place where you could pay a fee to leave your carriage.

However, ours was so fancy. Considering the risks, we decided to pay extra so that it would be kept in a proper building and not outside with the others. Also, we had the golem driver stay with it.

After that, we headed out into the main street.

Rienna and Fule paused and looked at the street that extended into the horizon.

“…There are so many people.”  

“And carriages.”

The streets were overflowing with people. We were still close to the gate, but it was already difficult to walk without bumping into others.

However…

“This is nothing. Further on, there are places that are too crowded to even enter.”  

“Ohh. It makes me miss the quietness of Sheorl… Yes, I think it would be better that it remains small.”

“You changed your mind already… Well, Mr. Mappa seems to be enjoying himself.”

Mappa was moving around and looking at the streets and buildings. Perhaps he enjoyed seeing tall buildings.

Rienna looked at him with a smile.

“And there are so many clothes that I’ve never seen before. I would like to take a look around when things settle… But first, we have to find a house or room, yes? Lord Heal, which way should we go?”  

“Indeed… Considering convenience, a place that faces this street would be best. This is the biggest street in the city. It leads all of the way to the palace, and connects to all of the important places in the city.”

I said.

“And that includes the Arubal Company. Not only that, but there is a noble district near the palace.”

Rienna nodded.

“So we should be near this street for the sake of the investigation as well.”

“Aye. The other companies are all gathered here. And so we should look around and see if there is any good property. And if not, we can look for an inn.”  

“Understood… Though, it seems like it will be tiring having to walk.”

Fule said a little dishearteningly.

And like that, we started to make our way down the street.

However, an angry voice rang shortly after.

“Hey! You people! Stop!! Aren’t you monsters!?”

Rienna and Fule stopped.

For a moment, I was worried that we had been found out.

However, when I turned my head, the person who was shouting was facing in the opposite direction.

He wore tattered clothes and had a chipped sword on his belt. And there were other similar men surrounding him.

Thugs. And they had found someone to pick on.

It was not an unusual sight within the city. If anything, Leodor had been too peaceful. This was what you saw often all over the country.

But what was this about monsters?

Up ahead, I saw that there was an old wagon. And in the bag, there was a pile of supplies, as well as some hooded figures.

“Goblins…”

Fule muttered. Rienna nodded.

“I think so. Though, they must be a different tribe from us.”

Rienna had been a goblin too. So she could likely tell, even without seeing their faces.

Before meeting me, they had traveled all around the country. And sometimes, they had to visit human towns in order to buy supplies. That was likely why these goblins were here as well.

By law, monsters were forbidden from entering the city. However, the reality was that humans and monsters had been trading goods for many years. And it was seen happening all over the country.

There had been a time during the Barleon Empire, when humans and all monster races lived together in peace. It was a remnant of that time. Just as monsters wanted what humans had, humans were interested in goods made by monsters.

So in general, guards would be bribed to look away…

Still, there were always people who liked to torment the weak.

And so the thugs laughed as they surrounded the wagon.

“Hehe. If you want to get through, you better hand over all your money.”  

“Bu-but, we don’t…”  

“Then give us your goods. Eh?”

I could not allow this to happen.

And so I stepped forward.

But just then, a dark hooded figure appeared.

“Stop.”

The voice was familiar to me.

+++

278 – An Old Enemy!?

---

Near the front gate of the royal capital. As the monsters were being threatened by thugs, a man in a black cowl appeared.

As he was wearing a black robe, I didn’t notice it immediately, but both of his legs were prosthetics.

“Stop.”

The thugs then turned around and faced the man.

“Eh? And who are you?”

The man approached them.

Under the hood, his eyes flashed sharply as he looked at the monsters behind the thugs. He was telling them to go.

“Th-thank you!”

The monsters bowed their heads, and then they continued on with their wagon towards the outside of the city.

“Ah, wait!!”

The thugs tried to stop them, but the wagon was now on the other side of the crowd.

“Shit! Bastard! What do you think you’re doing?”

“Don’t you know who we are?”

They moved towards the man.

Fule muttered.

“He isn’t moved at all…”

“Well, he is able to challenge them alone.”

Rienna nodded.

Indeed, there was something different about his aura. You could tell that this was no ordinary man.

But more importantly, that voice…sounded familiar.

As I thought of such things, one of the thugs grabbed the man by the collar.

“Hey!! Why don’t you say something!?”

I thought that the man would fight back… However…

The thug’s fist slammed into the man’s stomach. And then the others began to punch and kick him.

“Say something!”  

“Not going to fight back? What a creep!!”

Contrary to my expectations, the man was being beaten up.

I frantically ran towards him.

“Hey! Stop!”

“What? Who are you!? Are you… Wah!?”

Rienna and Fule used wind magic to knock the thugs off of their feet.

“Wh-what!? Wind!?”

As the crowd began to murmur, another voice rang.

“What’s going on here!!”

And then someone began to make their way through the crowd.

“Is that…”  

Rienna said in surprise.

It was a man in a red coat and shaggy hair. He also had a beard on his familiar face.

“Balpas!? We-we have no quarrel with you!”  

“Le-let’s get out of here!! There will be trouble if we fight with Balpas!”

And so the thugs scattered at once.

The new arrival was Balpas. The eleventh prince and my older brother.

Balpas did not look at the fallen man, but turned to me instead.

“You…”

Perhaps he was not too surprised, as he might have heard the news about how I had defeated the bandits on the Nostor mountains. Otherwise, he would have surely been taken aback by my appearance.

There was no point in hiding now. And there was no necessity either.

“Brother. I can explain. But right now…”  

I turned to the man in the hood. Rienna was already casting healing magic onto him.

However, the man raised his hand and quickly stood up.

“I am fine.”

He said, and then quickly walked away. However, his steps were slow, as if he was still in pain. Also, the kicking seemed to have damaged his prosthetic legs.

After hearing the voice, I finally knew who it was.

I turned towards Balpas.

“Brother. That was…”

Oren. The eighteenth prince and my younger brother. A man who had visited Sheorl and then lost everything. I had not even thought of the possibility that he would still be alive.

He had murdered nobles and had been judged by the laws of the kingdom. There was only one punishment for that… However, perhaps being of the royal family had spared him.

“…As you have guessed, it is him. Well, there were reasons for it. In any case, we should find somewhere more quiet where we can talk.”

Balpas said, and then beckoned for us to follow him.

Indeed, two princes could not stand out here and talk about Oren and Sheorl.

Balpas knew about our strength. Besides, matters had been mostly settled between me and my father. Sheorl and Sanfaris had a peace treaty. And so he would not try to trick us.

“Very well, brother.”

And so we followed Balpas and entered a back alley.

Balpas seemed to be a little curious about Mappa as he asked hesitantly.

“Hey, Heal… What happened to that one who looks like that small old man?”

Balpas was clearly talking about Macha. A ryukin golem that looked a lot like Mappa.

Before our father left, Macha had taken a liking to Balpas. 

“She didn’t come this time… Did you want to meet her?”  

“No! The exact opposite! Who would want to see that! Well, nevermind… I am relieved.”

Balpas said with a sigh. Perhaps he really was troubled by the attention.

It was then that Balpas stopped in front of a large building made of stone. There was a sign in the front with a tankard painted on it. 

“A tavern I frequent. Let’s talk inside.”

It was quite boisterous inside. Even though it was still midday, the people were all drinking. Music was playing, and people danced.

Balpas passed some money to the owner behind the counter.

“Old man. Four seats. The special ones.”

“It’s open now. Want me to call the ladies? Ah…and perhaps some men?”

“…We aren’t here for that. Just prepare some drinks and light food.”

Balpas said, and then they were led to the back of the tavern. It was separated from the other tables, on a mezzanine floor.

When I looked down at the first floor, I saw that Mappa had taken a seat at the counter. Was he going to order a drink…? No, the bartender gave him some milk.

Balpas sat down and said,

“We will be fine here. The people drinking and shouting are mostly my own subordinates or allies. In fact, this is basically like my base.”

And so we all sat down at the table.

+++

279 – Brothers!

---

We took our seats on the opposite side of the table, and then Balpas began to speak.

“There are a mountain of questions I want to ask you… But first, I will answer your question.”

Balpas glanced to the side. There was a man sitting on a chair in the corner of the first floor. A hood was pulled deep over his face, and he was crossing his arms. It was Oren.

“Oren was supposed to be executed as the monster who killed the real Oren and took his place. Oren himself accepted this punishment… But father prevented it.”

“Was he showing mercy to his son?”

Rienna had a conflicted expression, but Balpas shook his head.

“He is not the kind of man who would do that. He only saw value in using him for something else. Recently, we’ve had a need for people we can use.”

Breaking laws and agreements for your own personal gain… It wasn’t just our father, but past kings of Sanfaris had worked like this in order to expand the country. So this was not the least bit strange.

Oren was no longer able to use magic. But he was still part of the royal family. That meant above average knowledge and skill with the sword. Well, he probably could not use a sword in that body now…

“Well, regardless, he does not have much longer to live. He is constantly bleeding and in pain. Could you see this as atonement, and be lenient?”

Things had been settled between me and Oren. It did not concern me what my father wanted to do with him now. And so I did not feel any anger.

“I have no objections. But…”

“You’re not going to say you feel sorry for him, are you? He is not the kind of person you should pity. Even his saving of the monsters earlier. It was not from a sense of justice.”

Rienna turned to Balpas.

“Then…why?”

“Because he doesn’t know anyone would help the weak. He was taught to always be strong. And that the weak are nothing but tools. That is, until he went to that island and became weak himself.”

Balpas turned to me.

“And yet you offered your hand. Welcomed him to the island. He had never experienced such kindness before.”

Kindnes… Oren had always been surrounded by his followers. But now that I thought about it, I had never seen him being helped by anyone. And even if someone did something, it would be considered normal for Oren.

Balpas answered as he exhaled a puff of cigar smoke.

“It’s ironic that he should realize his own foolishness after losing everything. But he still does not understand why you helped him.”

It wasn’t something that I could explain either. It seemed natural to me, and was how I had treated others up until now, when I could.

“And so he was copying what Lord Heal was doing. As a way of trying to understand…”

“I don’t know if he will ever learn… Still, we share the same blood, so I will watch him until his final moments.”

Balpas said as he lit another cigar.

“Well, I have no right to talk, as my hands are much less clean than his.”

Balpas had the Twilight crest, which allowed him to be silent and invisible. And he had assassinated many people according to our father’s orders. Both good and bad people were killed, merely for the gain of this country.

Though, I wondered what Balpas meant when he said they lacked people to use.

“The kingdom seems very peaceful now, brother… Is there something happening that requires help?”

“If there was, I wouldn’t be telling you. It’s a state secret.”

As Balpas said, he had no duty to tell me about Sanfaris. Every country had its own problems, and it wasn’t as if there was anything that I could do.

“Now it’s my turn to ask a question. What are you trying to do? Suddenly leaving your southern island and coming to Leodor, defeating the Nostor bandits… And now you are here in the capital.”

“There is no deep meaning behind it. We were just traveling through Leodor, when they needed help. And so we took down the bandits.”  

“Well, you never were able to leave people alone… And I’m sure it was an easy task for you.”

Balpas has seen our power on the island, and so he knew that bandits wouldn’t stand a chance against us.

“And did you stop by the capital before going to Leodor?”  

“No, we did not. While it may seem like we were taking the longer route, we went around the east coast of the continent directly to Leodor.”

“Hmmm. But why to Leodor of all places… Ah, I think I know why.”

Balpas looked like he remembered something.

“You used to be close with that Rish! I saw her not long ago, and she has become quite beautiful…. Though, I did hear that she is to be engaged. Elserd…of house Bessel.”

Balpas seemed to know everything. Perhaps he knew about the Arubal Company as well?

I wondered, but then Balpas looked at me with a grin.

“Too bad for you. But you won’t be able to win against Elserd when it comes to the ladies.”

“I am not trying to do anything in regards to Rish…”  

“Really? Well, even if he is handsome, his personality is another thing. I am sure you are much better. Maybe you have a small chance?”

Balpas said teasingly. While it was annoying, it did seem like he had no connection with Elserd. And it seemed unlikely that he knew about the teleportation device or the Arubal Company.

As the Leodor matter was not important, Balpas quickly moved onto the next question.

“Leaving such jokes aside… Why are you here in the capital? For fun? I can see that you do not lack the company of pretty women, but I can still recommend some establishments.”

Rienna blushed a little.

“I just want to speak to our father.”  

“…Don’t tell me that you miss him?”  

“Never… It is something important. Though, not necessarily urgent.”

“I see. Unfortunately, father is not in the city right now.”  

“Is he out on an inspection?”

“No. Officially, he is still somewhere inside of the palace. He went out in secret. And so even I do not know where he is. As you know, he is the kind of person to secretly sail away to a southern island.”

I had wanted to tell him about the black miasma.

After seeing the situation in Arancia, I had felt that the danger of the prophecy was getting close. We had to work together in order to face it. Even if he didn’t agree, he at least had to know about the threat.

“I suppose you don’t know when he will return either?”

“Indeed. Sometimes he returns the next day, sometimes he is gone for months before suddenly appearing behind my back.”

“If only I knew where he was going… But I doubt he would tell anyone.”

Balpas nodded.

“Aye. And so you have no choice but to wait here. Of course, if I see him, I’ll let him know that you wish to speak to him. Ah…you don’t have to tell me why. I don’t want to get involved in any more trouble.”

Balpas said with a tired sigh. He said that they were in need of help, so he was likely dealing with a lot of trouble. Perhaps that was why my father had acted.

“You must be very busy. And father is also busy. Would he really agree to meet me now?”

“Don’t worry about that. He will definitely want to meet you if I mention your name. After all, he knows about how much power Sheorl has.”

“Very well… I will stay here and wait then.”  

“Aye. You should do that. Should I recommend you an inn?”

It wasn’t that I didn’t trust him, but Balpas worked behind the scenes. It was likely that he had great influence over any inn he would recommend. And that someone would be spying on us.

“Thank you. But I think we’ll look for one on our own. Besides, I want to show my friends the city.”

“I see. Well, do as you wish. I am often in this tavern, so you can come here if you want to find me. And if I’m not, just leave a message with the owner.”

“Thank you, brother.”

I wondered if I should ask him about the Arubal Company and Elserd, but I decided not to.

And so we stood up and bowed.

But just as we were about to leave the tavern, Balpas called out to us.

“Wait. I just remembered. I would avoid going to the palace if I were you.”

“I don’t intend on going unless I can meet father…but is there a reason?”

“Our other brothers and sisters know about the island. They will be sure to try to draw you into something.”

The various competing factions of royals. Before Sheorl, I had been considered to be too useless, and so I was mostly left alone.

But things would be different now.

“Thank you for the warning, brother.”

“Aye. If something happens, you should come to me. While I don’t want to get involved either, I can listen. And don’t worry, I won’t pull you into anything as well. Now, goodbye.”

Balpas waved his hand. I didn’t know what his true intentions were. Still, he knew about Sheorl, and so he was easy to talk to.

Just then, I heard a strange ringing sound coming from the first floor of the tavern.

“Hmm? Is that a bell? Hey, you’re all drinking too much!!”

Balpas said as he looked down.

However, everyone on the first floor was looking at a single man.

“Ah, it’s Mappa.”

As Fule said, Mappa was banging a hammer. With metal and wood, he crafted something that looked like a thick leg.

And when it was finished, he carried it towards…Oren.

Oren looked up at him.

“…What do you want?”

Mappa looked at Oren’s prosthetic leg. Due to the thugs earlier, it was broken.

“I don’t need that… This is enough.”

Oren said as he looked away.

However, Mappa removed the false leg and attached the new one.

With his arms still folded, Oren raised the new leg.

“It is lighter…and looks durable… Are you sure?”

Mappa nodded with a satisfied expression.

“I see… You have my thanks.”

Said Oren, and then Mappa patted the leg with a somewhat sad expression.

“What’s with that old man…”  

“How dashing…”

As the others murmured around him, Mappa put some money on the bar counter and headed to the exit.

“That kid is showing off…”

Balpas said as he turned to me.

“…Well, at least I won’t have to carry him to a workshop now. From now on, any meals or drinks here are on me, alright?”  

“Thank you. But…Mappa does eat a lot.”  

“If it’s not drink, then it’s cheap. Besides, he looks like someone you shouldn’t get angry…”

Balpas said with a chuckle. Though, he was probably thinking more about Macha than Mappa.

After that, we reunited with Mappa and left the tavern.

++++

# Pupil of the Wiseman Chapter 305 -  Breakfast in Valhalla

「Thinking back to those times, our meals became rather bizarre. We’d have sweets for breakfast, lunch, and dinner.」

Alfina looked baffled as she recalled that. In short, Frodina was always making sweets from the day she obtained the cookbook, and she explained that she merely wanted to try out every single recipe at least once.

They would have a hefty dessert with each meal, and then she would even bring more sweets to practice as snacks. Once she was done trying out every recipe, she continued to master the ones she had liked the best.

「At the time, I could only think of preparing and eating them, so by the time we noticed…」

Frodina said that, the light fading from her eyes. As they spent those days, indulging in all those sweets, they realized that they had gained weight and became fatter.

「But…but there were so many delicious things to eat every day!」  

「It was too difficult…to resist.」

Elivina and Celestina spoke, their heads low in self-derision as they recalled those times. The sisters had gained weight at different rates, with those two and Christina being the most impacted. Especially Christina, who was the one eating the most at the time.

「It’s all Frodina’s faulttt!!!」

Christina yelled in distraught, realizing that Mira would learn of that dark blemish in their history, and pinned all the blame on Frodina for making those delicious desserts, and claiming she was merely a victim.

It did not seem like a very rational excuse, but more than half of the sisters seemed to share that sentiment, showing just how big of a temptation sweets could be.

「I see, so that’s what happened… And you said you gained weight, but exactly how much was it?」

The sisters were all in perfect shape, making it difficult to imagine them looking more plump in the past, so Mira asked just how bad things had gotten. Gaining fat could mean a different thing to different people, and Mira wanted a more specific answer.

Asking a girl something like that was usually taboo, and Mira would have been branded a tactless person with no manners if she had not been a girl herself, and the master of the sisters.

「Well…」

But as those conditions were met, Alfina replied without reservation.

Eletina, Frodina, and Shalwina had all gained around five kilos. Elivina and Celestina seven. Each time Alfina mentioned their names and that information, the valkyries looked down in shame. And eventually the last name came.

「And Christina… She gained fifteen kilos.」

Alfina sighed after saying that, still baffled that it had happened in the first place. That was also followed by a deafening cry, which obviously enough came from Christina.

In other words, the ban on sweets had been a form of dieting for them.

Frodina was not allowed to make sweets anymore, completely stripping their menu of desserts. Alfina was the only one who had not gained any weight, even though she had been eating the same desserts as the rest. That was because she always subjected herself to a far more strenuous training regiment than the rest, and knowing that, she also made her sisters train harder to make their new diet more effective.

「Hmm…now I’m getting the full picture.」

Having heard the whole story, Mira actually agreed with Alfina’s decision to ban desserts.

「Awww… Masterrrr…」

Christina let out a begging plea, and the other sisters soon joined her. They had just seen Mira, their only hope, switch sides to stand with Alfina. But luck was still on their side.

「I think it’s fair to say that there was a more than valid reason to remove desserts, but isn’t it about time that the ban is lifted?」

The sisters had spent more than a decade like that, and yet they were still burdened by that lack of sweets and strenuous training. So Mira tried to reason with Alfina. The diet had been successful and everyone had lost the weight they had gained, so there should be no problem with serving a dessert every two or three days.

「I agree that serving sweets three times a day every day like back then was excessive, and gaining weight is a logical result. If you’re a bit more mindful of how much sugar you’re consuming, you shouldn’t gain much weight so quickly.」

Mira could not help but feel pity for the situation the sisters were in, so she listened to their pleas and attempted to convince Alfina, as Mira herself believed sweets were medicine for the soul.

「That’s a really good point… Maybe it’s time for some change.」

Knowing Alfina, it was no surprise that she took Mira’s words to heart, and eventually decided she would take some time later with Frodina to discuss how often they could have sweets.

The sisters, spearheaded by Christina, began cheering loudly the moment they heard that. Alfina looked a bit baffled by that, but also had what seemed like a gentle smile. And Mira was also glad to be part of that.

「Things sound really lively so early in the morning, did something good happen?」

Bruce peeked into the dining hall with a curious look, hearing the cheers of the valkyries as their sweets situation had improved.

「Oh it’s nothing. We were just talking about food for a bit.」

A lot happened and now they would have sweets again. Mira summed up everything like that and went to sit down at the table, figuring it was about time they ate. The sisters all followed their master, making it seem like an actual breakfast scene, instead of what looked like a celebration after a successful battle.

Bruce repeated 「Sweets?」 as he walked over to sit with them, still trying to understand. Then he saw the french toast and grinned, 「I love french toast.」

「And the soup for today is my special salad stew.」

Frodina announced that while bringing a pot from the kitchen, a delicious scent of vegetables and meat wafted from it. At the table, she poured the stew from it into bowls that were already filled with salad. But her hands seemed to be slightly unsteady, almost nervous as she served.

(This really is the first time I’m seeing a dish like this.)

That was one of Frodina’s original creations, salad stew. It consisted of fresh vegetables cut to bite sizes put on a bowl, over which a beef stew would be poured instead of dressing. It was both an intricate and daring idea for a dish.

Mira had been shocked when she first heard about it, but the other sisters seemed to really value it as a special and delicious breakfast. They were all in the best mood having that on top of the sweet french toast they had already seen.

Frodina went around the table, serving the stew on everyone’s bowls. When she passed by Christina, she requested, 「Lots of meat please!」 and then stared in terror when she got a large pile of tomatoes instead.

Tomatoes indeed. The whole conversation earlier had centered around the french toast, but the salad stew with tomatoes was the actual star of the show, meant to play a key role in the main quest Mira and Frodina were on, to heal Alfina’s distaste for tomatoes.

This was the first time the stew was brimming with tomatoes like that, cooked to perfection and almost falling apart to the touch. But as they were cut in big chunks, they were clearly visible and stood out on the bowls.

Eventually, it was Alfina’s turn, and when her bowl was filled with stew, there was a clear change on her usually calm and collected face.

(I already knew, but she really does loathe tomatoes…)

Mira had been watching and mentally evaluated the reaction, as she wanted to see what would happen. There was no mistaking it now, Alfina did not want to have anything to do with tomatoes, and was staring daggers at Frodina for it.

(You deserve a medal after this, Frodina…)

While Alfina’s eyes seemed to be murdering Frodina, she somehow managed to keep a smile as she put down the pot while saying, 「There’s still a bit left if anyone wants seconds.」

But that only lasted until she sat down, her smile vanishing and her shoulders trembling in terror.

Mira looked at Frodina, her gaze conveying praise for having endured so far, and gave a gentle nod signaling that she would handle the rest.

Seeing Mira’s reassuring response, Frodina offered a weak smile and leaned back, clearly drained of energy.

「Sweet…so sweet..!」  

「Yes, there’s nothing like a sweet breakfast…」

Elivina and Eletina took a bite of french toast as soon as they began eating. The other sisters also did the same, savoring the sweetness with delight. Even Alfina looked happy as she ate, likely also having a bit of a sweet tooth after all.

Just calling it delicious did not do it justice. That french toast had been made with an exceedingly rare type of egg, freshly baked bread, and Frodina’s special way of preparing it all. It was miles ahead of anything Mira had tried before.

「Ohh, this is heavenly!」

Just one bite was enough for Mira to know how different this was. Some time had passed since the slices had been fried, so the interior felt even more pudding-like. It really felt like an actual dessert rather than breakfast.

That also made it the perfect dish for the sisters to celebrate the end of their ban on sweets.

Eletina ate slowly, savoring every bite as long as possible. Frodina nodded to herself, satisfied with how it came out. Shalwina was not just entranced by the taste, but also enjoyed the jelly-like texture. Elivina struggled to conceal a grin, feeling like they were overreacting over french toast. Celestina wanted to save the best for last, so she only took one bite of french toast before quickly going through everything else.

And then there was Christina, who had already devoured all her french toast and was now eyeing Celestina’s plate like a hawk. Sadly, there would be no opportunity to attempt stealing some, as her opponent was Celestina the weapon master, whose hands could turn a humble butter knife into a lethal weapon. Christina knew how badly things would end if she tried that.

However, she also noticed that Celestina’s guard was weaker against things happening the other way around, so Christina had been quietly offloading her vegetables onto Celestina’s plate instead.

There were a lot of long-held emotions swirling quietly around the dining hall, but Bruce was oblivious to it all, making lighthearted comments about how good the food was.

After some time, they reached what could be considered the middle point of their breakfast. Everyone had eaten in different ways, but they had at least tried a bit of everything, except for Alfina. Mira had been watching the entire time, and noticed that the eldest sister had not touched the salad stew at all.

(Maybe it’s even worse than I imagined…)

Alfina had been constantly turning to glare at Frodina, in what felt like a silent interrogation. Each time that happened, Frodina would turn to look at Mira, seeking salvation.

Frodina had let Mira decide when to enact their plan, as they had anticipated, something like this would happen and Frodina would be out of the picture after serving. And also, because the effect would be the strongest if Mira brought it up.

(At least now I see why she was so confident about this salad stew dish. It’s definitely worth all the praise.)

Still mulling over the best moment to enact their plan, Mira ate a bit more of the salad stew.

The stew made with a beef soup base, with various spices and vegetables, then thickened with potatoes grown in Valhalla, complimented the fresh vegetables cut into bite sized chunks perfectly, greatly elevating the dish. The spices also gave clear accents of flavor, which were refined by the sweetness of the tomatoes.

(No matter how much someone hates tomatoes, they should be able to eat this.)

Mira had also seen the potential of the salad stew, and fully believed Frodina’s claim that having just one bite would be enough for anyone to crave more.

But that first bite was the crucial part. Alfina was nowhere near trying it, she even refused to look at her bowl, instead turning to Frodina, her eyes demanding to know why Frodina was harassing her like that.

Those constant stares also made it harder for Frodina to feel at ease, and she had hardly eaten anything from her own plate.

With time, Frodina’s face began to turn pale, hardly enduring the wait until Mira would save her. Soon, she would reach her limit.

(I promise I’ll make all your kindness and efforts pay off.)

Frodina knew that Alfina would react that way, but she had still wanted to help Alfina be able to enjoy tomatoes. Mira would not allow those feelings to go to waste, so she gave Frodina a reassuring nod, ready to enact their plan.

But before Mira could say anything, Christina held her empty salad bowl and stood up, unaware of the plan. Then she headed to the stew bowl, her gait airy and carefree.

「Meat has a higher density, so it likes to sink to the bottom~」

She had switched targets from Celestina’s french toast to the pieces of beef remaining in the stew pot. After taking off the lid, she held the ladle and began digging around the bottom of the pot, and just as she wanted, found a trove of beef.

「See? Just like I predicted.」

Now that her bowl was full of beef, she beamed a radiant smile. There was nothing that made her happier than following her cravings. Mira also started grinning, but in a more devilish way, seeing this as the perfect chance to spring into action.

「Now, now, Christina. Beef might be good, but you shouldn’t neglect your vegetables. Don’t think I didn’t see you shoving all of them away to Celestina’s bowl.」

Mira stood up while calling her out, and Christina let out an audible 「Wawahh!」 while her shoulders twitched. At the same time, everyone’s eyes focused on her.

「So that’s what happened. And I was wondering why there were so many…」

The main victim, Celestina, stared at Christina with disapproval while holding her bowl of salad stew. In a way, it was more surprising that she had not noticed, but that was simply because the french toast she saved for later was all she could think of.

At least Celestina did not seem to hold much of a grudge past that. The other sisters mostly shook their heads, already familiar with Christina’s antics

And then Mira made her move.

「Alright, give me that.」

Knowing this was her best chance, Mira walked up to Christina, took her bowl, and then poured a large amount of tomatoes from the pot on top.

「You need to eat vegetables too. And especially these tomatoes since I picked them and cut them myself. They’re delicious, aren’t they?」

Mira said that while holding out Christina’s bowl, buried in a pile of tomatoes. She just stared vacantly at it, her hopes dashed. But then someone else spoke loudly in shock.

「What? You did that, Master?!」

It was Elivina. She had noticed that the tomatoes were cut more roughly than usual, when Frodina usually made very regular pieces. That was why she reacted so quickly.

「Well, it’d be a shame if we didn’t finish them then.」

Elivina said that, trying to act like she was doing it out of concern, and went up to the pot with her bowl.

「Ah, a serving of tomatoes for Elivina too then.」

Mira snatched Elivina’s bowl and filled it with tomatoes just like before, and Elivina was actually shocked now.

「Ah, Master, you served me…yourself…」

Elivina was mortified that she had accidentally pushed Mira into a serving role, but Mira laughed it off, telling her it was alright. Mira also added a few chunks of meat to the bowl, and returned it.

「Th-Thank you so much.」

Elivina happily took the bowl back. The other sisters had seen all of that, and they began standing up one after another.

「Oh, we might actually get through the whole pot at this rate.」

This was a very rare occasion for the sisters, so they all lined up with their bowls, wanting to have more of the tomatoes hand picked by their master. They were not as obsessed as Alfina, but they still held Mira in very high regard.

And Bruce also snuck in amongst them. He was in a similar situation, being able to receive something from Danbulf the Army, the Wiseman he admired and looked up to so much.

+++

# 306: Alfina’s Determination

While Mira continued serving the stew, Alfina was finally starting to show some movement, slowly turning to finally look at the salad stew she had refused to even glance at so far.

Her furious and resentful glare towards Frodina was gone, replaced by a warrior-like determined look as she firmly grasped her spoon.

Then, with the same impetus as an executioner swinging an axe, she scooped up a piece of tomato, bringing it up and staring at it with eyes wide open, ready to take the plunge without looking back, and then she put it in her mouth.

Slowly, she began to chew, while Frodina watched with bated breath. Frodina had a great amount of confidence in her cooking’s ability to change one’s opinion on tomatoes, but she could not quite shake off her uneasiness this time, as she was essentially up against the final boss of tomato haters. That was why she was silently praying, waiting for Alfina’s reaction.

Luckily, all of her worries were dispelled in the best way possible.

After swallowing, Alfina took another bite, and another, speeding up until soon she had finished her whole bowl of salad stew.

「Yes, it worked!」

Frodina celebrated in a low voice, glad that their plan had been successful.

The plan she came up with Mira did not involve a direct order to eat the tomatoes, but creating a situation in which Alfina would be compelled to do it of her own volition.

That was how Mira ended up helping with making the dish. Alfina’s fervent devotion to Mira would never allow her to ignore a meal while knowing that Mira had helped cook it, and Alfina was aware that no one enjoyed watching others seem disgusted by food they had made. When put in such a situation, Alfina’s only possible action would be to eat the tomatoes herself to not disappoint her master.

At least, that was what Frodina had hoped, pushing Alfina to take her first bite, after which the food would do the rest, showing Alfina that tomatoes could be really tasty.

The two had planned to act out a whole skit about it, but Mira chose to improvise when Christina stood up, making the interaction much more natural and allowing Frodina to stand back at ease, as she was terrified of the fate that would befall her if Alfina figured out her plan. Now, Frodina did not have to worry about acting out their whole skit, or having to use their trump card of saying Mira had wanted to eat that.

After quickly cleaning her bowl of salad stew, Alfina jumped on her feet and rushed over to Mira, who was still next to the pot of stew.

(This isn’t quite the reaction I was expecting…)

All Mira had wanted was for Alfina to hear about the tomatoes so she would try them, but before she knew it, she had turned into something like a school’s lunch lady. All of the sisters requested a second serving, and even Bruce lined up with them. In the end, the contents of the pot decreased greatly by the time she was done.

There was roughly enough for one more serving, still with plenty of tomatoes, and many pieces of meat.

(Well, at least my plan worked out!)

There was another reason why Mira was so happy serving everyone. She wanted to control the contents of the pot herself, so that when she refilled her own bowl in the end, she would get the most meat.

But the other ploy she was carrying out ended up throwing a wrench into that.

「Master… May I also have a bit more?」

Alfina held out her bowl, looking slightly hesitant, but her eyes twinkled with hope.

Mira looked up, startled, seeing Alfina standing in front of her and Frodina a short distance away. That was when she realized their plan had been successful, especially considering the victory gesture Frodina made.

「Of course, hand me that. I’ll make sure you’re satisfied.」

In the end, Mira was happy she had been able to help Alfina get over her pickiness. So she took Alfina’s bowl, divided the remnants in the pot into two, and poured one half into the bowl.

「Thank you very much!」

Alfina was deeply emotional as she received the bowl, and then nearly fainted from bliss when she heard what Mira said next.

「But there isn’t much left, so we’ll have to share half and half.」

Mira said that as she poured the remaining meat on her bowl, which seemed to leave a deep impression on Alfina.

「Ahh, sharing half and half with Master…」

Alfina seemed to prefer sharing a portion with Mira rather than having a full bowl all to herself. When she returned to her seat, she ate eagerly, almost in a trance, her distaste for tomatoes gone like it had never existed to begin with.

(That’s one more thing taken care of.)

Mira surveyed the table, everyone enjoying their meal now, and began happily eating her meat too. Things continued peacefully that way, and breakfast came to an end.

「Thank you very much, Master!」  

「I barely did anything. It’s your cooking that made it possible.」

Mira and Frodina gathered in secret after breakfast to celebrate their victory. Frodina would continue to incorporate small pieces of tomato to her dishes moving on, making sure that Alfina did not have any further issues with it.

When they were done cleaning up after breakfast, their regular routine resumed. Contrary to Christina’s wishes, Mira told the sisters to not mind her and train as usual, so they were all busy with that. They would start by going over the foundations of combat, before conducting practice fights in alternating pairings.

「Alright, we should get to work too.」

Just like the previous day, Mira went to the second training area together with Bruce, as he also had to practice his partial summoning.

「Thank you for teaching me!」

Bruce gave an energetic reply and he began to focus, a long staff in his hand. They began training right away, with Mira wanting to make sure he could use partial summoning in actual combat as soon as possible. They took no breaks either, relying on potions and various pieces of equipment to increase their mana regeneration speed to continue.

Mira was always observing how Bruce activated the various spells, pointing out his shortcomings and how to amend them constantly. She was only able to do that thanks to her own wealth of knowledge about summoning, and her precise instructions also meant that he was improving at a staggering rate.

(Good good, I knew I could count on a spellcaster from the tower. He’s quick to take in information, and he excels at everything!)

At that rate, Mira was convinced that Bruce would do really well in the tournament. She even began to dream of him winning the whole tournament. But then, she recalled that Meilin was likely going to be there, so that would be more difficult. Still, she was hoping he would get to the finals, and show the power of summoners to the world.
