But the place was so dark that she could not see anything past the Life Sensing readings, and she was too far away to hear what they were talking about.

(I guess it’s time to use that.)

There were multiple ways one could explain it, but Mira had already decided from the circumstances that they were up to no good, and acted upon it. She could not allow herself to overlook ruffians scurrying in the shadows of the empire led by her good friends.

Driven by that, she carefully hid behind the hut and activated a summon without them noticing.

The magic circle resembled a cat’s eye, and Cait Sith, the First Lieutenant, emerged from it, wearing a black ninja outfit.

“Hattori Nyanzo, here to serve you. Nin-nin.”

There was still no telling where he was learning all of those things, as the First Lieutenant, or rather Hattori Nyanzo now, seemed to have turned into a ninja and made his appearance while trying to recreate the classic ninja pose with his hands held together. Except that he did not have fingers long enough to fully recreate the hand sign, so at first glance, it just looked like he was praying or pleading for something.

“Well then, Hattori Nyanzo. If you look over there…”

Usually, Cait Sith was a summon that eased tension, but Mira tried to stay focused and briefly explained the situation to him, telling him that she had discovered three suspicious subjects, and that they were likely some sort of thieves.

+++

# 312: Those sneaking at night

“…That’s why I’m certain they’re up to no good.”

Mira explained how she had found those three sneaking around in a deserted part of the park. In response, Hattori Nyanzo announced, “Yes, that reeks of evil meow. Something must be afoot,” agreeing with Mira’s assessment.

“That’s where you come in. I want you to get as close as you can without them noticing.”

Mira then outlined her plan, which was nothing complicated. She just wanted Hattori Nyanzo to get close enough to the three to be able to listen in. That was all.

Her side of the plan involved testing out the next step in Sense Sync she had researched in the Tower, being able to receive both visual and aural information. Hattori Nyanzo was specialized in being silent, so he could get much closer to the target than she could, and with him in position, she would use his eyes and ears to gather information.

This made things way more straightforward as she would hear everything herself, instead of having to rely on a report after the fact. And Hattori Nyanzo would be able to ignore their conversation and focus on keeping watch for approaching guards, while Mira did the listening, keeping them even more hidden.

“Go now, Hattori Nyanzo. I’m counting on you.”  

“Your wish is my command, meow.”

Mira gave the signal to go, and Hattori Nyanzo vanished into the darkness. He really knew how to sneak around, but after Mira looked around for a bit, she noticed something white swaying amongst the trees.

It was his sign, which currently read “Actively Stealthing”, even though the white rectangle of the sign was almost glowing in the darkness.

Mira informed him of that, and Hattori Nyanzo hurried to bring down the sign, only for it to reappear on his back a few seconds later. This time the sign itself was black, and the letters were white. There did not seem to be an option for the sign to be completely gone.

While that nonsense continued, Hattori Nyanzo had made his way to the three, and was close enough to hear them.

Mira leaned against the hut to remain hidden and focused, activating Sense Sync with Hattori Nyanzo. Thanks to all her training, she was already used to doing that, and it only took her three seconds to activate it. Soon enough, she also heard the three voices.

“…same for you then? At this point, do you think that Oracle is even real?”  

“I think we’re in this situation precisely because it’s real.”  

“Then why is no one coming after us yet? I don’t get it.”

All three of them had male voices, wary of their surroundings as they spoke in whispers. But Hattori Nyanzo’s ears were sharp and could clearly pick up everything they said, transmitting it to Mira.

Mira had only started listening halfway through, but so far she could guess that the three were searching for someone they referred to as the Oracle.

As they continued to talk, Mira discovered that even those three did not know much about the Oracle, not the name, age, or even whether it was a male or a female, only that the Oracle lived in Nirvana. That meant they had an incredibly broad area to search, making them rather grumpy about it.

“At the very least, they could’ve sent more men with us. This is supposed to be an important mission, right? Then why just us?”  

“There was no way around it. The more of us come, the easier it’ll be to notice us. And they’ve increased vigilance because of the whole tournament too.”  

“Yeah, and don’t forget that we’re in Nirvana. If they spot us, they’ll sic those Twelve Apostles on us, and they might even track us back to our organization.”

They were making very little progress and just continued complaining. But at least they left a few breadcrumbs relating to who they were.

“Is there really no other way to get rid of that Oracle?”  

“They already tried and failed, that’s why they sent us. The Oracle’s powers really are the worst.”  

“Something about seeing the future, was it? And that ruined a bunch of business deals for our boss already. I don’t think we’ll be left very alive if we fail either…”

They also lamented the fact that such an annoying mission had been pushed onto their arms.

(I don’t think they’re thieves anymore…)

At first, Mira thought those suspicious men had gathered deep in the forest to discuss a hit on one of the nearby rich mansions, but things went in a different direction. They were assassins sent by some organization.

They had also mentioned some Oracle in Nirvana, who had the ability of seeing the future and had ruined business for their organization, which was why the assassins had been sent out.

But Nirvana was well prepared, and the assassins had no luck tracking down the Oracle, as was evident by their incessant complaining.

(Hmm… That’s interesting. I wonder what that Oracle thing is all about…)

Mira understood why the three men had gathered there now, but she still wondered about that Oracle. She did not remember anyone like that in Nirvana thirty years in the past, making her curious.

But that did not stop her from making up her mind. There were assassins targeting the Oracle, and she would not allow that to happen.

She was getting ready to apprehend the three when one of them finished his grumbling and said something else.

“Anyway, we should probably return and report to the boss at this point. We’ve searched everywhere and haven’t found a trace of the Oracle, so a different approach might be needed.”

Mira could infer from that that they had a hideout somewhere, as well as the existence of a boss. The other two were not so sure, and instead wanted to keep searching for another day. It was clear that they were afraid of upsetting their boss.

(Maybe it’s better if I let them show me the way to their hideout then.)

Rather than capturing the three there, it was better to let them go to find their hideout, and then capture them together with their boss.

Deciding on that, she released Sense Sync and proceeded to deploy a Rosario Summoning Circle to bring out the spirit of stillness Worthramble, to have the best chances of tailing them all the way to their hideout.

“Alright, please activate optical and aural camouflage.”

Mira told him what to do as soon as he was there, quickly reaping yet another fruit of her training and research. Now she could use those two abilities at the same time, enhancing her ability to sneak around, while avoiding the much harsher time limit of Complete Suppression.

“Umm, okay.”

Worthramble quickly did as told, and once they were concealed he asked, “So what exactly is the situation here?” while looking around at the dark park.

“Oh, right, I almost forgot…”

Back when Mira was testing out Sense Sync in the Tower, she discovered that the information gathered with it would not be passed on to the Spirit King and Martel. That also meant that Worthramble had no way of knowing anything that Mira had just learned.

She briefly filled him in while they headed to regroup with Hattori Nyanzo.

“Things will only get worse if we waste more time without getting any results. If we go back now we’ll just get off with just a small punishment. And you know how a̲n̲a̲l̲ the boss is about giving constant updates. We’ll just be delaying the inevitable.”

Somehow, they were still discussing whether they wanted to go back or not. Two of them seemed especially hesitant to see the boss.

(Who cares about all that. Just take me there already.)

Mira did not care if the three were punished by their boss or not, she was just fed up that they still refused to move.

“Okay, okay, let’s do it this way then.”

After some more discussion, the one who first mentioned going back to their hideout came up with a compromise. He would report to the boss alone, and the two could stay out if they wanted.

He seemed to be something like a mentor for the other two, and wanted to watch out for them. That kindness had no effect on Mira’s opinion, they were all wicked assassins in her mind and deserved no pity.

At least, the three finally came to an agreement that way, so Mira and Worthramble went on the move, tailing the assassin from a constant distance. Mira also sent Popotwise flying overhead to keep an eye on him, their formation making it impossible to lose sight of the target.

A small shadow also ran off in a separate direction. Hattori Nyanzo had been given a new mission, to head to the imperial palace in the center of the city to warn their friends of Nirvana about the assassins.

The Oracle that could see the future, an organization that disliked that and sent assassins, all of it were matters best handled by the government of Nirvana. So it was best to report directly to those higher up.

To make that happen, Mira had sent Hattori Nyanzo with a certain medal on top of the message. That medal had been given to Mira by Solomon, and symbolized that the carrier was working directly under Solomon.

It did not matter if it was late at night and that it was a strange cat carrying it, the medal would surely allow Hattori Nyanzo to get into the imperial palace, and Mira’s friends there would listen to everything he had to say.

With their assistance pretty much guaranteed, Mira felt comfortable storming the hideout of the assassins, and any mess she left would be taken care of by them. Mira was mostly excited about the prospect of a fight, as she had many new abilities she wanted to try out, so she grinned widely as she continued tailing the assassins.

Worthramble’s powers also once again proved their worth, as none of the three noticed them.

After around twenty minutes of following them, they reached the alleyways of a new district. There, the assassins began to act strange, looking around much more, until they lowered their stance and ran across a lawn of a nearby mansion.

(It looks like we’re finally here.)

The way they acted made it clear that the mansion was their hideout. Mira checked it out with Life Sensing and saw at least twenty people inside too, so it was quite a big group hiding there.

Mira and Worthramble were around ten meters behind the three, so they had to hurry up their pace to follow them into the mansion. Popotwise remained outside, keeping watch over the mansion from high above.

(This mansion is quite nicely built.)

The premises were quite large, with a twenty meter gap existing between the outer fence and the actual building. There was nothing offering cover when crossing that garden, so anyone trying to sneak in would be spotted immediately.

But that was no barrier against Worthramble’s power, and together with Mira, they followed the three assassins all the way to the front door, which was left unlocked, so after switching to Complete Suppression for just a moment they entered without being noticed.

“Ah, you’re back. How did it go?”  

“Still nothing, nothing at all. The boss isn’t going to like it.”  

“Aw man… I’ll be praying for you then.”  

“Thanks, I appreciate it.”

The three seemed to have a rather high position amongst those inside the mansion, as everyone they passed bowed to greet them…and remained oblivious to Mira’s presence.

The power of stillness kept her hidden even while deep in enemy territory. This was partly because so few knew about Spirits of Stillness and their powers, let alone how to detect or counter them.

Eventually, they reached what looked like a storage room deep within the mansion, with miscellaneous things strewn about randomly.

“I’ll be going then.”  

“Okay.”  

“Break a leg, or two…”

After exchanging a few words, one of the assassins snuck his hand into the mouth of a lion statue in a corner of the room. A mechanical click followed, and the floor opened up.

(A hidden switch, huh. I guess that’s par for the norm in mansions like this.)

Mira had seen such gimmicks a lot in the past, and thinking about that, she attempted to continue following them, only to be stopped by Worthramble.

“Mira, we’re almost out of time.”  

“Oh, let’s find a place to hide around here then.”

Hearing that warning, Mira decided to interrupt her chase and instead went to hide in a corner of the room before Worthramble’s powers wore off.

All of Worthramble’s abilities could only be active for a limited time, which was an understandable restriction considering how convenient his power was. That also meant that his powers had at least one weakness too. Currently, there was a half an hour time limit when using two abilities at the same time, with a ten minute cooldown.

She checked what was past the hidden corridor with Life Sensing and saw around ten people, including the three she had followed. The boss they had mentioned was probably also there. Mira wasn’t sure how skilled those people were, and she feared that visual camouflage alone wouldn’t be enough to conceal her.

If there was a skilled sage down there, they would also notice her presence much faster, putting her in danger. It would be even worse if they could use Life Sensing, so she needed to employ both visual and presence camouflage simultaneously to avoid detection.

“Let’s wait and see for a bit.”

Mira decided to survey the movements beneath them with Life Sensing until the cooldown period was over. She saw the three assassins making a straight line to another reading, presumably the boss. It was hard to tell with Life Sensing alone, but judging from the size of the readings, the boss seemed to be quite larger compared to the three.

Just around that time, she received information from Hattori Nyanzo, who had gone to the imperial palace.

+++

# 313: Encirclement

‘Meow Master, I’ve completed the meowssion you entrusted to meow.’

Eventually, Hattori Nyanzo reported back, relating everything he went through.

He had arrived at the palace’s front gates without incident, and upon seeing the majestic building, the ancient blood coursing through his veins was set ablaze, showing him that it was a palace worth conquering. But upon acting on those instincts, he was soon surrounded by guards and forced into questioning, and only released after he showed the medal Mira entrusted to him.

Not long after that, he succeeded in making contact with Esmeralda, one of the Twelve Apostles, who he told about the assassins and their hideout. After all that, he reported back to Mira.

‘I feel like there was a lot of irrelevant information halfway through, but good job. You did well.’

Everything would have gone much more smoothly if he simply showed the medal to the gatekeepers instead of the roundabout way he went, but that aside, things were looking promising. Mira decided not to bring that up, and instead asked what action the palace would take.

‘Oh right. They said they’ll send out an assault platoon to deal with them.’  

‘Hmm, an assault platoon, huh.’

According to Hattori Nyanzo, they were currently hastily putting together an assault team, and once ready, they would follow him all the way to the hideout.

That did not please Mira very much, as she wanted to be given the green light to take them down herself. Not being able to jump into action made her disappointed, but this was a foreign country, so she had to follow their rules.

‘Meow meow, and there was one more thing. They also said that if they show any signs of escaping before the platoon arrives, to take them down yourself.’

Hattori Nyanzo added that, almost like an afterthought. In a way, that also confirmed that they knew Mira’s true identity, as no regular Rank A adventurer would be expected to accomplish that on their own.

But someone like Danbulf the Army, one of the Nine Wisemen, would have little trouble seizing a whole hideout of assassins. At the same time, those were the exact words Mira had wanted to hear.

‘Hmm, alright. Tell them I’ll do that if things come to it.’

Mira replied with a grin, already thinking on how to do it in the most impactful way possible.

Maybe she could deploy her Dark Knights to wreak havoc, or have Alfina and her sisters perform a flashy entrance to take down everyone. Or maybe she could continue using the power of Stillness to pick off the assassins one after another, like a scene straight out of a horror movie. And so on, she really wanted to consider every possibility.

‘Someone just arrived at the mansion! Someone who was in a hurry!’

But those thoughts would be interrupted by a report from Popotwise, who was keeping watch outside. There had to be a reason why that person was running like that, especially compared to the three she had followed who were much more cautious.

A few seconds later, she heard hasty footsteps approaching before a man bursted into the room where Mira was hiding. He was likely the person Popotwise had mentioned.

(Oh, this must be him. It seems he ran all the way here.)

He was breathing heavily from all the running, but he did not wait a second to operate the hidden stairs and continued rushing down there.

(So he’s going straight to the boss.)

Mira followed the man’s movements with Life Sensing, and saw his reading move rapidly to the same room as the first three assassins she had followed. She could only wonder what kind of information required so much haste.

Driven by that curiosity, she began debating sneaking down there as well, but was stopped when she noticed more movement.

The man who rushed in turned around and ran out from the hidden stairs, while raising his voice to repeatedly yell, “Pack everything! Quickly! An assault platoon is on the way!”

(Now that’s something… Does this mean they have a mole in the palace? They found out way faster than I expected.)

According to Hattori Nyanzo’s regular updates, the assault platoon had just been gathered, but they had not left the palace yet. But somehow that man had already known about them and came to warn the rest.

(Well, that’s a problem for them to handle later.)

That was an internal issue of Nirvana’s government, so the higher-ups of Nirvana should deal with that. But she would gladly do what she was asked to do and stop the assassins from escaping.

Now that she had a valid reason to act, she quickly began her plan.

First, she used Sense Sync to gain the viewpoint of Popotwise, before unleashing yet another ability she had acquired in her research at the Tower.

Summoning sites had to be designated before a summon would appear. So far, Mira had been limited to deploying summoning sites within a fifty-meter radius, and only if she had a clear line of sight. But now, she had enhanced that capability by integrating Sense Sync, allowing her to deploy summoning sites in more places.

Now, even with Mira deep within the mansion, she could borrow Popotwise’s line of sight to deploy summons outside of the mansion, and soon, there were forty five Holy Knights and five Ashen Knights encircling the mansion.

(Ohoh, this came in handy much faster than I thought.)

One of the men in the mansion decided to travel light, picking up only a few items before rushing out of the front door, only to receive a Holy Knight’s shield bash straight on the face and flying back into the mansion. Soon after, there was a big argument between those inside.

Popotwise’s point of view showed how the man flew back and hit a wall before falling limp, as the hit knocked him unconscious.

The loud noise lured more people there, where first they saw their fallen comrade, and then the Holy Knight standing at the door. Once they processed what had happened, they ran around in a daze like headless chickens.

“What the hell! They’re already here!”  

“I thought he said we still had time to escape before they got here?!”  

“What do we even do now? We’re surrounded!”

They thought the Holy Knights were the assault platoon, and now they did not know where to run off to, while also starting to blame the man who had warned them.

“No, that’s impossible… I ran here as soon as I heard they would come! They shouldn’t be here so soon!”  

“Then who the hell is standing outside! We can’t slip out anywhere!”

As they continued to argue, the man who warned them insisted that the assault platoon was still getting ready, until he saw the Holy Knight and his face contorted with fear.

“Who in the world is that… That’s not the assault platoon…I’ve never seen anyone like that in the whole army…”

Some tried to find an opening through the encirclement, others tried to break through by force, but no matter what they tried, they were always mercilessly forced back by the Holy Knights.

And that was not all, as the five Ashen Knights also made their way into the mansion.

With them inside, it did not matter whether the men ran, tried to stand their ground, or fought back, they all fell at the hands of the Ashen Knights.

The man who came to warn the rest, who could not recognize the Holy and Ashen Knights, also stood no chance and soon joined the rest of his comrades, lying unconscious on the floor.

(That’s one side taken care of.)

The first floor of the mansion had been taken care of, leaving only those past the hidden stairs. With that in mind, Mira cut off Sense Sync and walked up to the lion statue in a corner of the room, sticking her hand into its mouth. Inside, she felt a small ring, which opened the hidden stairs after being pulled.

“Let’s go get them.”  

“Yes, I’ll cover you.”

After that quick exchange, Worthramble activated visual and presence camouflage simultaneously, after which Mira headed down the stairs.

The underground hideout of the mansion looked like a long hallway, with various doors on each side, leading into at least ten other rooms.

But what caught Mira’s eyes the most was how luxurious everything looked. The furnishings there were just as shiny and gaudy as those of a noble, so that hidden area likely belonged to someone important.

(They’re really living things out down here.)

All of those items belonged to the assassins, so Mira already knew what would happen once the assassins were apprehended. The mansion would be cordoned off, and all items within would be declared abandoned and confiscated into the imperial coffers.

That realization soon tempted her to take one or two items herself, as they could be useful when bartering for items with spirits in them later on. But she soon stopped herself, as it did not matter how much she rationalized it, it would still be stealing at the end of the day.

(Having to work honestly and earn enough to obtain them is what allows us to accept each other.)

Any of those items would sell for upwards of ten million Rils, making them really enticing, but Mira forced those thoughts out of her mind, telling herself that they would at least give her some reward money for her work there, and moved through the hall.

“Really? You want to carry that all the way out?”  

“Why not? I really like it.”

One of the doors was slightly opened, and she heard those voices coming from within. Peeking inside, she saw a man holding onto a rather unsightly vase, and another one looking at the first in disbelief. Both of them were also wearing eerie masks, making them rather unsightly as well.

The ground floor was currently filled with cries of dismay as they all fell at the hands of Mira’s summons, but those below were unaware of all that.

She checked other rooms as well, and heard people casually talking about how they struggled to sleep with different pillows, or how their plants were about to sprout, what was worth taking, and so on. They did not seem to have any rush in leaving.

For a moment she wondered if they had no idea what was happening above them, but that was not quite it.

“They got here far earlier than anticipated, huh. At least we shouldn’t have any issues.”  

“Yeah. It’ll take them a while to find this place.”

There was a large room at the end of the hallway, where the men in higher positions began to gather one after another. There were around twenty of them in total, and they seemed unbothered by what was happening upstairs. They were confident that no matter what happened, they would be able to get away.

And they had more than enough reason for that, as simply finding the existence of a secret room in a mansion took time, and prying open the way there took even longer, giving them plenty of time to get ready to escape.

The way they spoke also made it clear they had more authority in their group than the rest. All of them wore masks, and referred to each other by whatever their masks represented.

(Hmmm… It makes sense for the higher-ups to be in the secret area. And they have a secret route out too…and it’s somewhere in this room)

It was almost expected for a secret area in a mansion to also have an escape route. So that was the first thing Mira searched for in there, and deduced that it was located somewhere in the big room everyone was gathering in.

Mira silently snuck into the room as well, staying in a corner to observe what would happen. She did not want to let a single one get away, and it was better to just get them all in one go, so she waited until everyone was there.

She also noticed some movement in the farthest end of the room. A large Gardia Tribe man, the boss of everyone there, had just ordered the three assassins Mira had initially tracked to tear off the wallpaper.

“Ah, there it is, that should be the lever.”  

“Let’s get away already!”

After a brief moment of confusion, Mira understood why they did that. There was a cavity in the wall beneath the wallpaper, housing a hidden lever, which was likely the way to open the secret exit. Seeing it, the three assassins gathered around it in unrest.

“Stop, don’t even think of pulling it yet.”

And then the boss stopped them. That lever would open the way out, but it would also activate a mechanism that would destroy the exit after three minutes. So they could only leave once everyone gathered.

(Hmm, only three minutes… That complicates a potential pursuit.)

At least that meant that no one would leave ahead of the rest, something Mira appreciated as she grinned devilishly while sitting in wait for the remaining members.

“I wish I had an Operator’s Bracelet too.”  

“You were expelled once already, right? Then just give up.”

The men arriving were all carrying large and heavy loads, and they seemed to really regret not being able to take more of those valuable items with them, as they constantly complained about it. Still, they knew that facing the assault platoon was a losing battle and had no choice but to escape.

“I just secured the entrance, but things are really ugly upstairs. That assault platoon is far stronger than we heard, especially those in gray armor. Just who’s the moron that failed to report on that?”

One of the men who entered, who gave off a rather knowledgeable appearance, began complaining about that. Somehow, he gave the appearance of being the boss’ right hand.

“They got here faster than we thought, and they’re also stronger. It seems they were feeding us fake information.”

The boss replied with a clearly irritated voice, but without raising it too much. “We’ll make sure to pay them back for this,” he added, grinning menacingly, to which his right hand man replied while smiling similarly, “They’ll regret making us go all out.”

(Sorry about this, but I’m not the assault platoon you were expecting.)

The higher ups down there still were under the impression that Mira’s summons were the assault platoon, so they kept repeating things like, “Next time we’ll slaughter them all,” “Just wait and see what happens next time when I go with the search team,” and so on, already making plans for the future.

(Sorry again, but none of you will have a next time.)

Finally someone arrived, apologizing for the wait. He was the final member, so with him there the boss said, “Time to leave then,” and gave the order to pull the lever.

Just in case, Mira used Life Sense to check the surroundings and verified that everyone had gathered in the room. That meant it was also time for her to act, so after looking around the room, she went to the door.

“Hm? Is it me or the door just opened on its own…”

Everyone was looking at the three with the lever, when one noticed a soft noise and turned around, noticing that the door was slightly ajar. And Mira aimed for that moment.

(Catch! A small present from me.)

Mira and Worthramble had gotten out of the room, and Mira chuckled as she threw various Magic Bomb Sealing Stones into the room.

“What’s that?!”

The stones became visible once they flew outside of the optical camouflage range, making the man that turned around raise his voice in confusion. That prompted everyone else to also turn around to look at it, just as the stones were set off into a thunderous explosion that shook the whole building.

+++

# 314: Testing Grounds

“Let’s see how well that worked…”

After using her Magic Bomb Sealing Stones to recreate the way special forces use stun grenades before storming a building, Mira opened the door again to check the results.

The first thing she saw was the furniture, torn apart and spread around wildly, as well as the other luxurious items they were trying to take out. Then she saw the three assassins she had followed, collapsed in front of the lever.

The Magic Bomb Sealing Stones she had used were far harsher than mere stun grenades, packing quite an impact as she knew that she was dealing with experienced assassins, and she wanted to knock out as many of them as possible.

Still, they began to stand back up one after another, even those closest to the explosions. The boss and various others had only been grazed by it.

But the three assassins and the boss’ right hand man were knocked out cold, so it had been worth it to an extent.

(Oh…they managed to survive through that. They really aren’t ordinary men…)

That group had managed to sneak deep into a powerful country like Nirvana undetected, so its leaders had to be considerably powerful. Mira verified all of that by peeking through the door, carefully examining the situation.

“You there, by the door, did you do this?”

Some of them were powerful, but the boss was a step above the rest. He had taken a defensive stance, and after relaxing and standing up straight, he sharply turned around to stare directly where Mira was.

She had to undo her concealment to throw the Magic Bomb Sealing Stones, but recast it right away. The effect was also obviously active, as others were looking at the space in the opened door, but not making direct eye contact yet.

Only the boss seemed aware of Mira’s presence, as he followed her with his eyes as she entered the room.

(He seems rather adept at sensing others… I guess there’s no point in hiding anymore.)

There was no longer a reason to stay hidden, so Mira undid her camouflage, revealing herself to them.

“…Who’s that?!”  

“Where did she come from?!”

All of a sudden, a girl appeared in a spot they believed was empty. The men there were clearly confused by it all, and only their boss took a few steps toward Mira, a displeased look on his face.

“And to think it’s such a little girl. Just who are you?”

Considering his line of work, surprise attacks were something the boss encountered on a daily basis, but he had not expected to be confronted by such a girl, and more importantly, he felt almost insulted that they would send someone like that after him.

“Who could I be, I wonder?”

Mira just grinned teasingly, dodging the question.

For a moment, she thought of introducing herself as a summoner fighting for justice, imitating Lastrada. But she was dealing with lowlife assassins, so she did not think it would really have much of an effect and stopped herself.

“You don’t seem to be a bounty hunter either… I can only imagine that you’re part of the assault platoon that moved ahead of the rest, but I wasn’t told about anyone that looked like you. Then again, I don’t even know if the results of that investigation were reliable or not anymore. This country really knows how to mess with us…”

The boss continued to stare at Mira, examining her features while gradually growing more enraged, feeling like Nirvana had played him like a fiddle. In reality, their information had been extremely reliable, but Mira and her summons had completely disrupted their usual activity.

“Whichever the case, I commend you for getting this far. That stealth ability of yours is something else, I hadn’t noticed you until you attacked. But did it work in the end? No, you underestimated us. All you did was tell us you were here.”

He was still surprised that Mira had made it so far into their hideout, carefully watching her in case she tried something else, while also stressing that things would have gotten better if she just remained concealed.

Only a few of the men there had been knocked out, leaving Mira overwhelmingly outnumbered. Mira silently listened to the boss prattling out, but a different thought got lodged in her mind.

(Now then…how come none of these recognize who I am?)

Not too long ago she kept getting stopped in the streets by people wondering if she was the Spirit Queen, or at least whispering about it in the distance. And yet everyone there, from the boss to all his men, did not seem to even think about the S in Spirit Queen, instead pinning her as being part of the assault platoon.

At first, she assumed that they were not up to date on the things happening in the city since they spent their days holed up in their secret base, only to remember the actual reason why.

(Ah, I forgot. I’m wearing a disguise.)

She had dyed her hair black, put on a pair of glasses, and even changed outfits, so now she looked like a cute city girl and nothing more. There was nothing on her that would identify her as the popular Spirit Queen, so it made sense that no one thought of that. That also meant that none of them would know what type of spells she used.

“Hehehe, underestimating me will be your last mistake. I’m a member of the assault platoon’s covert ops unit, and the commander of the black hair shock troops! You’re all under arrest!”

It was better to exploit their misunderstanding, so she claimed to be part of the assault platoon, and raised her voice while looking around to rile them up.

“Hmph, covert ops and shock troops, you say? And you’re still calm while completely surrounded like this. I can’t tell if you’re overly confident or just trying to put on airs, either way it was a mistake for you to come here alone.”

While Mira stood up confidently, the boss faced her without hesitation or fear too. He had no doubt that the strength of his men, and especially his which was a step above the rest, would make easy work of Mira.

“Oh, that’s not quite right, is it? Over there…”

The boss suddenly glanced toward a different location, raised his palm in that direction, and after gathering mana, unleashed a shockwave straight at it.

“Woah, that was close…!”

At the other end of the shockwave, Worthramble had to jump to the side to dodge the attack. So far, only Mira had stepped outside of the camouflage effect, while he remained concealed. Still, the boss had noticed his presence.

“You aren’t alone, there’s two of you. I don’t know how you kept yourselves hidden, but your surprise attack won’t work anymore. I’m guessing that was your trump card? Too bad, it’s not enough to take me down.”

Many of the boss’ men surrounded Worthramble, who just raised his hands in resignation, something that brought a smile to the boss’ lips.

“Hmm… Not too bad for the leader of a group of assassins.”

The boss was strong. Even the average Rank A adventurer would be beaten in an instant. And that strength gave him the confidence he displayed earlier.

But that interaction revealed that the boss was a sage. He had used Life Sensing to detect Worthramble, and then used Shockwave to force him out of hiding. And he was skilled at both.

“You’ll have a better time if you stop trying to fight and just give up. You’ll regret it if you continue…”

The boss announced coldly while equipping a jamadhar, which was something like a fist weapon with a blade sticking out of it. It was clear he was used to such situations, and he had gotten this far by treating each time as mere business.

A tense atmosphere filled the room as everyone got ready for the brawl, but then one of the men there took a step forward.

“Boss, could I have a moment? I’d really like to take her out myself.”

The man who intervened looked rather different from the boss, smirking widely as he looked Mira up and down, licking his lips in excitement.

“She might be wearing a really plain outfit, but look at her more closely, she’s definitely a looker under those clothes.”

He wielded a short club, a sleazy grin on his face as he suggested they capture Mira alive.

“Oh, so you’ve actually noticed my cuteness? You have good eyes, but I take no pleasure in being seen by a pervert like you.”

As he approached, his gaze seemed to slither up Mira’s body, from her feet all the way up, and Mira was clearly displeased. The man was the opposite, as that reaction only accentuated the look on his face.

“Ugh, he’s going all weird again. He always goes out of control when that happens.”  

“And then he gives us all a bad reputation. I really wish he’d keep himself in check a bit more.”

The comments from the others there made it clear that the man had a really depraved nature, and even they were tired of him. There was only one reason why they would keep him around despite his fame, his strength.

“Oh? I know I can trust your eyes, so I’m sure there’s demand for girls like her out there too.”

The boss finally replied to the perverted man, adding, “Let’s capture her alive to sell her off somewhere then.”

Hearing that, the perverted man looked horrified and began to protest, as he would not be able to get his way with the girl without damaging their future merchandise.

“Why did it have to come to this… I saw her first…but I guess I’ve got no choice then. Boss, at least let me do the visual inspection later…”

He staggered a bit as he continued to walk toward Mira, almost drunk in his own lecherous delusions. He raised his club, licking in lips in delight, clearly becoming a walking representation of perversion.

(Unbelievable… This is the first time I’ve felt such strong vulgar emotions aimed at me.)

She had noticed men looking at her with such intentions plenty of times, but this was the first time she actually shuddered and felt disgusted by it.

“Just be a good girl and go to sleep now. Everything will be over when you wake up.”

He continued to grin as he slowly lowered his stance. His mind was overrun with disgusting thoughts, but that did not interfere with his fighting ability, as his form was impeccable without any openings.

It was impossible to read when he would move or what kind of attack he would use. He just kept that disgusting grin on his face as he slowly continued to step forward.

Mira quickly understood she could not afford to be careless around him and remained watchful, when something moved behind her, swift like an arrow. It was also positioned right in her blind spot, and flying straight at her.

That was all part of their plan. It did not matter if that was his true nature or just an act, as long as the perverted man could make his target uncomfortable and wary of him, the target would fixate on him while someone else attacked from behind.

Mira was disgusted like never before about that man’s attitude, which was obvious to the other men there, with one picking that perfect moment to attack.

The man that attacked held out his hand to grab Mira’s wrist, closing in the few meters separating them in an instant. And just when he was about to take hold of Mira’s wrist…his hand phased through it.

“What…?!”

That strategy had never failed them before, so the attacker raised his voice in shock and disbelief. He had been tricked, the wrist he tried to snatch belonged to an illusion, the afterimage left behind by Mirage Step. Mira had not lowered her guard for a second.

Mira’s real body was just a step behind the illusion, putting her in the ideal spot to counterattack, as the man who rushed at her was off balance from his failed attempt.

“Too bad for you.”

Calmly saying that, Mira took hold of the attacker’s arm, and no matter how much he tried to shake her off, it was too late for him.

A purple flash illuminated the whole room together with a deafening sound, as a bright and powerful bolt of lightning passed through the man. Mira had used Lightning Grasp to knock him out cold, and after he fell to the ground, the only remaining sound in the room was an echo of thunder.

Then there was silence, the men there shocked by everything that happened in such a short time. They had thought their plan was working, until Mira turned things around halfway through, in a far more dramatic way than any of them expected.

“Ohh she’s a feisty one. That only makes me want to savor her more.”

The first one to react was the pervert, showing that those propensities had not been an act, as his face became even more indecent. At least, he still had the presence of mind to take a few steps back, understanding that Mira was stronger than they anticipated.

“Then why don’t you come and try to get a taste already?”

Mira held out the hand she had just used to take down one of them, taunting him as she narrowed her eyes and looked around muttering, “So who’s going to try sneaking up on me next?”

She was fully confident she would be able to thwart any sneak attacks they would attempt, which made the men in front of her begin to appear nervous. At least, until one of them stepped forward.

“I see you’re a Sage as well… which explains why you were able to evade an attack coming from your blind spot.”

It was the boss, who grasped the pervert’s shoulder and pushed him aside. He continued taking a few steps forward, and merely glanced at the other man that had been knocked out.

“And you’re quite an adept one as well. I guess this should be a reminder to not get deceived by appearances.”

The boss sounded rather miffed as he spoke to Mira, who just replied, “I mean, I didn’t even think there was a need to deceive any of you since I got here.”

“Heh, do you really think I’ll fall for your cheap provocation? But now I’m curious.”

The way Mira acted like there was no need to come up with plans to deal with them was starting to have an effect on them, especially on the boss’ pride.

“I won’t just take that and not say anything back. We’re both Sages, so let’s settle this with a proper duel.”

The boss suggested that, and even ordered his men to put down their weapons and step back. They soon obeyed, also releasing Worthramble to prove their intent to remain honorable.

“Hmm… Very well then. I’ll take you up on that offer.”

She knew she was dealing with underhanded assassins, but a duel was something she would never refuse, not to mention that it would provide a much more convenient solution.

Mira and the boss stepped to the center of the room, while other men stepped back near the walls around the two. Worthramble also moved to stand next to the door.

The stage was set and the two combatants stood facing each other, ready for the fight. The boss seemed rather confident in his own ability, as he looked straight at Mira while discarding his jamadhar to fight barefisted.

A tense atmosphere soon filled the room.

“You, give us the sign to start.”

The boss spoke to the pervert, who came up to them with a silver coin and said, “Let’s do it the usual way then.”

That was something Mira had also seen plenty of times while she was searching through the street fights earlier. The pervert would flick the coin into the air, and the fight would start the moment it struck the floor.

The two stared at each other as the boss slowly lowered his stance, gathering strength to act swiftly when the time came. Mira kept her rather relaxed stance, focusing on the small movements from the boss.

That all happened while the silver coin was still rising in the air, eventually reaching the peak of its assent and began falling.

And as if that was the real signal, all of the men there began moving at once, brandishing weapons they had kept concealed to lunge at Mira.

They had attempted to deceive Mira twicefold. The coin toss had been a signal for the rest of the men there.

She knew she was completely surrounded thanks to Life Sensing, and could only assume that the boss and his men had decided to overwhelm her with numbers after their first attack had failed.

A grin also appeared on the boss’ lips, almost mocking Mira for being deceived so easily and putting herself in a disadvantageous position.

But she did not seem shocked or taken by surprise in the least. Instead, she also smirked at almost the same time as the boss.

They were all capable, which made sense considering their rank so close to the boss. It took them hardly any time to get their hidden weapons ready, making it impossible for most people to react in time.

That did not apply to Mira. Almost at the same time as they all began moving, they all noticed tall figures standing behind them.

“What..?!”  

“Who are these..?!”

All of them were knights with black armors of a terrifying appearance. They were Mira’s Dark Knights, which she had fully equipped for combat, giving them a far more imposing presence. The moment they appeared, they sprang into action, swiftly moving to restrain the men.

Soon, the tables turned as their surprise attack was completely reversed by the Dark Knights. The attackers had charged blindly toward Mira, leaving their backs fully exposed. No matter how skilled they were, there was nothing they could do, Mira’s Dark Knights swiftly overwhelmed them.

One was knocked out cold from a strike of a Dark Knight’s warhammer, then another had both his knees shattered. One of them tried to fight back, only to end up thrown at a wall, caving it in as his bones broke and he let out a painful groan.

Everything started and ended in an instant, with all the men soon lying motionless on the floor.

“That was flawless.”

Worthramble could not contain himself from saying that after witnessing how perfectly Mira had deflected their surprise attack.

“Heh, I wasn’t expecting it to go this well. Your power really is something impressive.”

Mira was still watchful of the boss’ movements as she glanced around to see the result herself.

That had also been accomplished thanks to a new type of summoning, only possible when Worthramble was already summoned. Concealed Summoning was an ability that would mask over the whole summoning process, making it invisible until the summon acted.

She had used that to deploy Dark Knights all around the room, which remained imperceptible until they moved together with the men.

“You little…!”

Only the boss had been spared, as he had been more attentive to his surroundings to make sure the surprise attack worked, and he was capable enough to fend off the incoming Dark Knights as well.

It was clear why he was the boss of the other assassins. He was at least as strong as a Rank A adventurer, or maybe even a step above, not even breaking a sweat when facing off against three Dark Knights.

Mira had also made her Dark Knights stronger recently, but that was still not enough to take down the boss.

The Dark Knights swung their heavy warhammers effortlessly, but that was not enough to catch the boss, who deftly evaded every single attack, even performing counterattacks with powerful Sage Arts.

Two more Dark Knights joined the fight, chaining their attacks one after another, but their speed could not match the boss, who endured through it and responded with a special attack of his own.

His first strike caved in their armor, and the second shattered them. The boss was not just a shrewd tactician, but had the Sage Arts to match.

It was only a moment after that, when he defeated a third Dark Knight, that he began to appear distressed. The shattered Dark Knights had faded away, revealing that they were not human opponents.

“Are you afraid of my Dark Knights now?”

Mira placed a hand on the boss’ shoulder and spoke with a boastful voice.

The Dark Knights were tall, wielded brutal weapons, had enormous strength, and had a terrifying presence to them. Meanwhile, Mira had the complete opposite appearance, creating a dissonance that distracted the boss.

Mira took advantage of that, successfully reaching that spot behind him.

That also signaled that the fight was over. There was a multitude of powerful Sage Arts one could use after taking hold of an enemy, something the boss knew better than most, making this situation no different from having a blade pressed against his neck.

“This is it then…you’ve managed to catch me off-guard. I surrender.”

He raised his hands as he said that, but as she was behind him, she could not see that his face was not one of resignation. He was merely pretending to give up, hoping to exploit the moment Mira moved to restrain him to turn things around one last time.

“Those are summons, aren’t they? I could tell earlier when I hit them. You really got us good, I thought you were only a sage. But that reminds me of some adventurer I’ve heard of recently, the Spirit Queen or something like that.”

His eyes were rapidly darting around the room as he tried to buy more time for himself, trying to find anything he could use.

Soon he found it, the lever to activate the hidden passage, which would collapse after three minutes of being opened. The explosives set up there were powerful enough to level the entire mansion, while also being simple enough that a strong impact would activate them without the need for the lever.

It was going to be a risky wager, but it was the only way out for the boss.

“Can you believe it? Out of everyone, it had to be a summoner who would take me down.”

He decided on his plan in hardly no time, so he continued talking about trivial things to conceal his intentions, while waiting for the moment when Mira would look away. But he had made a grave miscalculation. Mira was far more ruthless than her appearance would suggest.

**Sage Art – Earth: Lightning Grasp**

With her hand still firmly holding his shoulder, she unleashed that attack without mercy, once again illuminating the whole room with a flash of lightning. Mira also knew when the ideal timing to break free would be, as she herself had done that many times in the past, and she would not take any chances with the boss.

And she was dealing with a ruthless assassin that deserved no pity, so she had no issue with completely knocking him unconscious before restraining him. She even felt it would be faster that way.

“I didn’t appreciate how you talked about summoners right there.”

Actually, her use of excessive force was because of something far simpler.

A burnt smell permeated the room as the boss’ tall body toppled over, his hands still raised.

+++

# 315: Assault Platoon

“And this for a job well done.”

Mira downed some Matcha au Lait once she finished wrapping everyone in Arresting Cloth, celebrating her victory in the secret basement. That drink was also a staple of Nirvana, a place known for growing a wide variety of tea leaves.

With everyone fully restrained, she thanked Worthramble for his help before sending him away, leaving her as the only person moving around the mansion. Her next step was to check the various bags and sacks the men had tried to take out of the mansion.

“…Maybe I should’ve picked weaker ones…”

Since they had been trying to escape the mansion, the assassins had packed the most valuable items to take with them, from amongst the already luxurious items stored there. After the brawl, most of those items had been shattered to dust.

The Magic Bomb Sealing Stones she had thrown into the room at the beginning had done most of that.

Still, there was a decent number of items that had survived, which were mostly sturdy high quality weapons, and pieces of art the men had reflexively covered with their bodies.

To Mira’s eyes, each one of those would sell for at least a few million Rils.

At a glance, she calculated there were around a hundred million Rils worth of items that had survived, a sum that would grow many times over when factoring everything the assassins had decided to leave behind.

She visited the various rooms in the secret basement as she added it all up in her mind, a greedy smirk on her face.

Sure, most of that was likely stolen goods, but she could not stop herself from looking at it as spoils of war, or at the very least compensation for her work.

After some time loitering like that in the basement, she finally noticed something important.

“Hmm…I didn’t think about this before. How do I get out of here now?”

She recalled hearing one of the assassins mentioning blocking off the entrance, and when she went to check the stairs they were certainly blocked off. Mira was trapped in the basement.

There was still the exit the boss and his men had tried to use, but she did not know where it would lead her, and the path would be destroyed some time after she pulled the lever.

(It’s not the first time I’ve heard of an escape route that also traps in any pursuers.)

It was a common trope in spy movies and such for buildings to auto destruct and erase any evidence in them after the villain escaped, and that could very well be the case for the mansion as well. So as long as she did not know the extent of the destruction, she could not pull the lever so haphazardly.

(I just have to find a way up then.)

She could try to break the basement’s ceiling to make her way out. As far as she could tell it was built of stone, so it was worth a try.

But she soon noticed that it was rather sturdy stone, and no mere explosion would be enough to break a hole.

A more powerful blast would do the trick, if only she could think of the right means to produce it. Sadly, all that came to mind would be far too powerful and would destroy everything on the floors above as well, which was not something she wanted to deal with.

With no other options coming to mind, she began to seriously consider it…checking if there were still any unconscious men on the floors above.

‘Commander, the reinforcements are almeowst here!’

She had almost forgotten about the First Lieutenant when she heard his voice in her head, announcing that the real assault platoon was about to arrive.

‘Ohh, I see. Could you tell them something for me then?’

With her allies on top, she could no longer blast her way out of the basement, especially as they would witness her destroying all sorts of valuable evidence in the process. Instead, it was wiser to communicate her predicament to them through the First Lieutenant.

“And that’s the situation, meow.”

The assault platoon, riding as fast as they could, arrived at the mansion. The First Lieutenant was with them too, firmly held onto the shoulder of their leader.

“I can hardly believe they’ve been taken down already… I can see why the Spirit Queen is so admired.”

Their leader was called Cecilia. She was a highly talented knight, who had become the leader of the assault platoon at her young age, and answered directly to Nirvana’s Twelve Apostles.

(I was under the impression that she was just another adventurer, but I’ve never seen Lady Esmeralda get so flustered. Just who is she…)

Cecilia had been together with Esmeralda when the First Lieutenant arrived at the palace. Esmeralda was one of the Twelve Apostles, so Cecilia was really surprised to see how flustered and nervous Esmeralda got at the sight of the First Lieutenant.

And now the same person who did that had just single handedly taken down the whole mansion of assassins.

(Don’t be rude…don’t be rude…)

Now Cecilia was also starting to get nervous, recalling Esmeralda’s instructions to politely invite Mira to the palace. Fighting against bandits and assassins was one thing, but the intricacies of noble etiquette was something Cecilia constantly struggled with, as she had grown up in the countryside.

It was quite late at night, and only a few windows were lit up on the houses in Ratnatraya’s new residential district. Usually, those were tranquil streets with nothing special to see, but this time, there were many people peeking out the windows to see what was happening.

What was especially curious was that the center of attention was a mansion that had never stood out before.

There were plenty of rumors for other places, like a house said to be used for strange rituals late at night, another where eerie voices were occasionally heard, others frequently visited by menacing figures, and even one that appeared inhabited though no one had ever seen anyone enter or leave.

But this time, none of those were the center of attention. Instead, something was happening at a seemingly ordinary mansion, one that had never stood out before.

That fenced mansion was eerily silent this time, surrounded by strange white knights, which also had an unsettling appearance.

People began looking out of their windows, speculating with their neighbors about what was happening, but none of them dared approach the mansion. Then they all began cheering as they saw the assault platoon arriving in their galloping horses.

“Look, it’s Knight Cecilia!”

A certain gentleman with binoculars to admire beautiful women announced loudly.

“What a platoon…they’re all elite knights!”

Another man, who was enthusiastic about the army, also shouted in excitement after a glance with his binoculars. He could see the best members from across all units in Nirvana’s army gathered there, which was like a dream come true for a militia aficionado like himself.

Usually, nothing much happened on those streets, which only made that change in scenery all the more exciting for the people there.

‘Yes, that’s the place. Then just go a bit more…there, the entrance is right there!’

Meanwhile, beneath the mansion, Mira had stopped trying to break herself free, and instead had decided to rely on Cecilia to get her out.

All of the assassins in the mansion had already been taken down thanks to Mira, so all the assault platoon had to do was investigate the building for evidence, and take everyone into custody.

After Cecilia finished giving orders to her men, Mira spoke with the First Lieutenant to guide Cecilia to the room with the hidden staircase.

Once there, Cecilia said that maybe she would be able to break through.

Mira had been too afraid of causing too much damage by attempting that, but if the person in charge did it, then at least Mira would be able to wash her hands off the matter if things went south. Having taken a few steps back, she gave the signal to the First Lieutenant to begin.

There was a moment of silence as Mira looked attentively at the sealed entrance.

Then there was a short metallic sound, which repeated various times, and then silence again. That was interrupted by the sound of a small chunk falling from the basement ceiling, quickly followed by a crack that spread from that spot, and then it all fell down.

“Now that’s really impressive too…”

Once the noise of falling debris subsided, it was clear that the hole only appeared in the spot Mira had told them to, specifically right above the stairs. When Mira examined the hole, she also noticed that it did not look like it had been broken, but there was a clean cut all around.

Somehow, Cecilia had cut through the stone with her sword, showing just how excellent her abilities were.

Nirvana had really sent their best knights with the assault platoon, ready to deal with a dangerous organization like those assassins.

“There it is! Let’s jump meow!”

While Mira admired the cut rock, the First Lieutenant jumped down through the hole, followed by a lady in deep blue armor.

As soon as she landed, she ran up to Mira.

“Thank you so much for your assistance in this…umm…huh?”

After a quick bow, she finally got a good look at Mira, which made her stammer and look confused. Despite her magnificent knight armor, she was still a countryside villager at heart, so her evident confusion gave her a peculiar cuteness.

“What? Is there something on my face?”  

“Ah, please excuse my actions. It’s just that I was told you’re the Spirit Queen, but you don’t look quite like I was expecting…”

She quickly straightened her back and apologized for her reaction when Mira pointed that out. With all the rumors going around, she had expected Mira to have silver hair and wear a magical girl dress, which were the two things Mira had changed for her current disguise.

“Ohhh I get it now. I actually put on this disguise to sneak all the way here without letting them suspect who I was, so they were easy prey for my summons.”

Mira quickly came up with an excuse for it that would make her look better. Then again, the result would have been largely the same even if they knew she was the Spirit Queen.

“I see, that’s very impressive.”

The lady instantly believed Mira’s idiotic story, and then seemed to recall something else as she straightened her back and introduced herself. “I’m Cecilia, appointed as commander of the assault platoon. It’s my pleasure to make your acquaintance.”

“I’m Mira. As you already know, I’m also commonly called the Spirit Queen.”

Mira also introduced herself, while taking back the medal from the First Lieutenant and storing it in her Item Box. That act also served to prove her identity.

“Sorry to cut things short, but where are the boss and his men?!”

The First Lieutenant also tried to say “And I’m…” but Cecilia talked over him, her eyes full with determination. She was still a knight on a mission, so securing those men was her main priority. As soon as Mira said, “In that room over there,” Cecilia excused herself and ran there.

“What a hardworking girl.”

Mira nodded to herself as she said that, then followed after her. Behind them was the First Lieutenant who had been robbed of his spotlight and mumbled something to himself.

“I’m nothing but a shadow, sometimes as a servant, sometimes as a thief, but always living in the darkness and fated to die in obscurity…meow…”

There was no one looking at him, clad in his ninja master attire. The sign he carried also read ‘One with the shadows,’ as he trotted after Mira and Cecilia.

“Hyaaahhhhh!!”

Cecilia’s scream echoed through the basement. She had gone ahead to check on the restrained men, and seemingly had encountered something there.

“What happened?”

Mira looked into the room to see what had happened, and saw Cecilia standing with her sword unsheathed in front of a Dark Knight. Now they were standing still, with Cecilia looking around awkwardly.

That was enough for Mira to understand what had happened.

The boss and his men were all tied and piled up in the center of the room, surrounded by multiple Dark Knights in case something happened.

From a cursory glance, that made it look like some sort of wicked ritual with human sacrifices. Mira had also given the Dark Knights orders to face anyone who entered the room.

So it was understandable for Cecilia to be startled once she got there.

“Umm…I’m sorry…it’s nothing…”

The shock wore off quickly as she sheathed her sword and began examining the men on the floor, trying to act like nothing had happened.

“Hmm, if you say so.”

Mira also decided not to torture Cecilia any further and pretended she had not heard or seen anything. That would have been the end of it…if it was not for someone who could not read the room at all.

“A maiden’s cry is the call for a hero! The warrior of justice Cait Sith will always come to your rescue meow!”

The First Lieutenant, who somehow had found the time to change from his ninja attire into a superhero suit, leaped into the room, landing with an exaggerated pose and an overconfident grin.

A moment later, just as he was asking “Milady, what troubles you?” he was enveloped in light and vanished.

Cecilia looked back, unsure of how to react to all that, and Mira just shook her head awkwardly.

All of the men were still knocked out cold, so Cecilia swiftly checked their clothes for any concealed weapons and took off their masks to see who they were. The way she moved suggested that she was quite used to searching people like that.

“No way… Jorg?”

After going through the lower ranking assassins, she gasped in shock when she finally unmasked the boss, whose face still looked roughed up from Mira’s treatment.

“Do you know who this man is?”

Since Cecilia seemed to know the man’s name, Mira began to wonder if it could be someone famous. Cecilia took a moment to think of an appropriate response, eventually saying, “Yes, we already suspected he was part of a certain organization.”

“An organization? Does that mean this whole mansion was one of their bases then?”

It sounded like they were not just a group of assassins, but part of an even bigger organization. That piqued Mira’s interest, but Cecilia stopped her before she could ask more questions.

“This is something Lady Esmeralda wanted to tell you directly as soon as possible. And that happens to be another of my objectives here. I’m tasked with bringing you to meet Lady Esmeralda once we’re done cleaning up here.”

It was already clear that Cecilia would not take too long to finish her investigation there, so she had also been tasked with bringing Mira to the palace.

“I understand you’re a very busy person, but could you take some time to come with me? I’m sure there’s also a reward ready and they’ll also serve you a luxurious dinner.”

Cecilia had seemed like a seasoned investigator when checking the restrained men, but that appearance quickly vanished.

She seemed almost worried that Mira would not want to follow her, and she desperately wanted to fulfill Esmeralda’s special orders. She even insisted that she would help Mira with anything she wanted if it meant they would go to the palace together.

“Calm down, I just have to go to the palace, right? I can do that, don’t worry.”

Mira had already been planning on visiting the palace for her own reasons, as she wanted access to the tournament registration forms to find Meilin, so she happily agreed to go with Cecilia.

“Thank you, thank you so much!”

Cecilia’s face lit up with immense joy hearing that. Then she called her second in command, who would be in charge of wrapping up their investigation while Cecilia left on her other important mission. Hearing that, the second in command also seemed relieved and politely thanked Mira.

They all seemed to take Esmeralda’s special orders very seriously.

+++

# 316: Mirako and Emeko

After a quick ride on a carriage with Cecilia, Mira arrived at Nirvana’s imperial palace. And as they were on a top secret mission, they entered through the back gate. Then Mira was guided straight to the drawing room.

“Please sit back and relax while I go to announce your arrival.”

After telling Mira to wait a bit, Cecilia dashed out of the room. It was clear she did not want to keep Mira waiting, or maybe it was more accurate to say she did not want to keep Esmeralda waiting.

“That smile of hers was always terrifying…”

Mira had plenty of friends in Nirvana, including Esmeralda, and even after all those years, it did not seem like she had changed. Esmeralda was the type of woman who would never make her anger evident, but that only made her scarier, as sometimes things left unsaid could weigh a lot more.

Various memories from the past floated in Mira’s mind as she reclined on the sofa and reached out for the cookies left on the table in front of her, which she was told she was free to snack on while she waited.

Around five minutes later, there was a knock on the door and Esmeralda the Divine Herald made her entrance.

“I’m sorry for keeping you waiting.”

Esmeralda said that as she entered, and then smiled a bit when she saw Mira sprawled over the sofa.

“I was told to be ready for your disguise and that you wouldn’t look the way everyone describes you…but you’re Mira the Spirit Queen, right?”

She approached Mira with inquisitive eyes, who washed down the cookies she was eating with tea and then replied, “Yes, I’m Mira.”

“Alright then… I guess that means we don’t need to introduce ourselves since this isn’t the first time we’re meeting?”

Esmeralda asked that with a grin, essentially prodding to see if Mira would confirm that she really was Danbulf. This was the first time ‘Mira’ was there, but they had long been friends with ‘Danbulf’ after all.

“You could say that. For me it’s just been a few months since we saw each other, but for you it must’ve been years…decades even, right Emeko?”

Mira nodded affirmatively, and then also broke into a grin by the end of her response. In a way, that was also confirming that she was Danbulf.

That made Esmeralda break into a delighted smile, which quickly turned into a pout as she grumbled, “How many times have I told you to stop calling me that.”

Back in the day, Danbulf kept complaining that Esmeralda was a long and complicated name, and decided to just call her Emeko. Mentioning that nickname was Mira’s way of proving her identity.

“Hmm…it’s not fair. I can’t even call you Danjiro anymore.”

After staring at Mira for a considerable time, Esmeralda said that with a sulky voice. Back in the day, she used to refer to Danbulf as Danjiro in protest to her nickname. But now Mira looked completely different, and that nickname made very little sense, making Esmeralda increasingly upset as the frown on her forehead deepened.

“Heheh, too bad. Be a good girl and just call me Mira now.”

Mira had started getting more comfortable in her current appearance as well, so she gave a cutesy smile while saying that, as if trying to get on Esmeralda’s nerves.

Lately, Mira had been thinking up various ways of exploiting her appearance to get her way with things. All because one time when she visited a cafe, they gave her a bunch of free sweets simply because she was cute.

“Ughh…you little rascal…”

There was no denying Mira’s success at acting cute, motivating Esmeralda to figure out a way to fight back. Eventually, she began saying, “Mirako…yes, I’ll start calling you Mirako too then!”

That had only lengthened Mira’s name, but it was all Esmeralda was able to do.

“Anyway, Mirako, I’m sorry to cut this conversation short, but we should find a more private place to continue talking. Come with me.”

They had their fun celebrating their meeting after such a long time, so it was about time they moved to discuss more important things, like Jorg and those assassins, and the organizations they were part of.

Cecillia had mentioned that Esmeralda wanted to talk with Mira directly about those things, and it seemed to be a really important but secret topic.

“Alright then.”

Mira stood up right away and followed Esmeralda further into the palace.

Nirvana was the second largest country built by players, and the imperial palace governed over the entire empire, so it was a far bigger building than Arkite Castle.

All of the corridors were illuminated with magic wares, making them as bright as during the day, and highlighting the sheen of the white walls and exquisite carpet. The corridors were also ample, dotted about with furniture that seemed like pieces of art, and even the equipment of the guards was impressive.

“Ohh… This place is overflowing with elegance…”

But what impressed Mira the most were the maids serving there. They moved around and performed their duties with grace, dazzling anyone who looked at them. As Mira and Esmeralda passed by, the maids also turned around to politely bow at them.

There was an enormous rift between them and the maids in Arkite Castle, who would nearly kidnap Mira whenever they saw her and make a big fuss about new outfits.

It was like a heavy weight was lifted off Mira’s shoulders as she realized that she could finally move around a place like that without having to watch every corner.

In reality, the maids of Arkite Castle were all trained and educated to essentially the same level, except when they were around Mira, who would likely never see them in that way.

Mira continued thinking about maids and other things for around five minutes, when she realized they had made their way quite deep into the palace.

The environment felt quite different there compared to the drawing room, being more quiet and solemn.

Fewer people and furnishings were visible on the corridors, but the few ones that existed looked even more impressive than before.

(Security is way tighter here too…)

Mira assumed that meant they were in a place with restricted access, nearly at the deepest parts of the palace.

She began to wonder if that organization really warranted so much vigilance, and as she thought about that, she followed Esmeralda into a room. It was a room at the end of a long hallway, so narrow that it almost seemed like an extension of the hallway.

At the other end of the room was a door, with two knights standing guard, who gave off an imposing presence just by standing there, showing just how powerful they were.

Whoever they were protecting past that door was clearly someone very important.

“We’re at your service, Lady Esmeralda.”

When they saw Esmeralda, they knelt to greet her. Then they looked at Mira and asked, “Is she the guest we were anticipating?” Those two had also been informed about Mira’s arrival, but as she was in disguise, they wanted to make sure they really were in front of the Spirit Queen.

“Yes, she’s the same Mirako everyone’s been talking about. She’s just wearing a disguise at the moment.”

They looked at each other with excitement hearing that response, willfully ignoring that Esmeralda had referred to her as Mirako.

“I’m Mira, nice to meet you.”

Mira decided to greet them herself, and they introduced themselves as well. One of them was Griss, and the other Ligner.

Esmeralda and Mira went through the door those two were guarding, which led to a small room with a bunch of doors, where they entered one on the right and finally arrived at their destination.

“Oh, you got here fast! I’m still getting things ready here!”

They entered a rather minimalist room. The rug on the floor had no distinctive patterns, there was a table, a kitchen on one side of the room with what resembled a fridge, and on the other side of the room was a plain bed. It was essentially a ten tatami studio apartment, where a woman was setting up the table to welcome Mira and Esmeralda.

“Ohh, I was wondering who I was going to meet here.”

Mira was quite familiar with that woman wearing a sweatshirt and shorts, who was carefully setting up the table like a waitress. Or rather, there was no one in all of Nirvana who did not know her.

The woman in front of them was none other than the ruler of Nirvana, Empress Alma.

“Esmeralda brought you all the way here, so you must be the Grandpa! It’s just as I suspected! See? I told you my instincts as empress were right!”

Once she had finished setting up the table, Alma ran over to Mira, staring at her intently before turning to Esmeralda, clearly proud of herself. It seemed like Alma was the first one to figure out the Spirit Queen was Danbulf, while Esmeralda had been skeptical about it.

“Ughh…I mean, who would ever expect Danjiro out of everyone to do something like that…”

While Alma gloated about being proven right, Esmeralda continued to pout about it, glancing at Mira and muttering, “Was he always into this stuff?”

“No no, that’s not it at all. It’s just that—”

Dread filled Mira’s heart as she realized that the reputation she had worked so hard to build as Danbulf was about to crumble depending on how she replied. But before she could get more than a few words out, she was cut off by Alma who loudly announced, “I knew from the start that Grandpa liked girls like that!”

“Ack..!”

If she had to be truly honest, it was true. But she could not bring herself to admit it and desperately tried to find an excuse.

“Stop! This is actually something I had to do to complete a super secret mission.”

Saying that, she explained that she altered her appearance because she would need to travel all around the world without being recognized. Danbulf was particularly famous as one of the Nine Wisemen, and she could not let that fame get in her way.

“Hmmm I see…so that’s why you did that. So, what’s that super secret mission about then?”

A mission so important that Danbulf turned himself into a young girl to complete it. Esmeralda could not help but get curious about it, but Alma quickly interjected to say, “Let’s not stand around and talk, the tea is going to get cold,” and trotted back to the table.

“Right, sounds good.”

Being a ruler herself, Alma seemed to understand that Mira’s mission was a state secret, so she spared Mira the conversation and changed topics. Mira also agreed right away and went to the table.

Once all of them were sitting, Alma began pouring the tea and brought a platter with various snacks, completing preparations for their tea party.

“Now we’re ready. Grandpa, please go on!”

Alma’s eyes were sparkling with curiosity as she urged Mira to talk. She had not been worried about making Mira leak state secrets at all. All she had wanted was to get comfortable to really get in depth about it.

(I should’ve expected this, they aren’t the type to give up easily.)

As Alma led a more common life, she was also the most curious about everything that happened outside, something that had not changed after all that time.

Mira knew that Alma could be more persistent than an oil stain.

Thinking about it some more, her search for Meilin was something she would need to reveal when requesting to see the tournament application forms. But then again, it was a state secret. It would be better to ask Solomon for permission first.

“I’d like to tell you, but my mission is a state secret, so I can’t just talk about it out of my own will…” Mira decided to plainly state why she would not talk about it, and then Alma picked up the black box on her lap and placed it on the table.

“So we should just ring up Solomon to get permission, right?”

That box contained a communications device. Mira was always told how expensive those were, but Alma was an empress, so it made sense for one to exist in her room. Alma had been even more ready than anticipated too, as Solomon’s number was already dialed.
