Perhaps she thought it wouldn’t be a good idea to make such a decision on her own, so Lily decided to consult with us first.

“I’m fine either way.”  

“Ah~, do I want to go~? If we can go, it would be a good experience, and getting hired on as reservists could be a bonus~.”

Contrary to the usual, I was okay with either option and Arisa was positive to the idea. As for Kuro…

“Mui~.”

She was half asleep and didn’t seem to hear us. But, with Kuro’s personality, she would say it doesn’t matter either way. I suppose her opinion is the same as mine.

“Hmm… In that case, let’s go and listen to what he has to say.”

So that is how it happened. We went to speak with the Magistrate.

“Hmm, then I’ll hire them as reserve forces. It’s better to be prepared in case of an emergency.”

It turned out that we were easily hired.

That said, we were basically waiting in the back, just watching the battle. We’re only the reserves after all.

To defeat the magic beast this time, some troops from the territory’s Order of Knights will be coming, and it sounds like their strategy has already been drawn up, so us being poorly incorporated may disrupt their coordination. That being said, even if we don’t take part in the battle, we’ll still be compensated. Thanks for that.

Other than that, Lily was asked to use healing magic to treat the injured after the battle. Although they’ve prepared potions and other supplies, it would be better if use of military supplies was kept to a minimum. The Knights were expected to arrive the day after tomorrow, so the departure was scheduled for the next day.

And with the Magistrate strongly pushing, we ended up moving our accommodations to the Magistrate’s residence. He told us that he wanted to hear all kinds of adventurer stories.

This is only natural, according to the Village Chief, while the Magistrate is called a ‘Knight,’ it’s actually more accurate to call him a Vassal Knight. In other words, he’s a private soldier who serves his Lord and hasn’t been officially knighted, and apparently, he’s a former adventurer. So when he goes to the Royal Capital with his Lord, he’s treated as a Commoner Servant. However, while within the territory, he’s given the same treatment and authority as a real knight, or in some cases, greater treatment.

The Magistrate is a man in his 30’s, named Jan. When I used honorifics, he gave me a strange look, so I decided to talk casually. He was actually a very friendly person.

The Lord of this territory seems to be a very caring lord, and Jan said he wanted to help the Lord in the future, ever since he was a child. After growing up, he became an adventurer and worked hard. His efforts were eventually rewarded and he was successfully promoted.

By the way, the usual response when a village is attacked by monsters or magic beasts, they usually send people to nearby large cities to make subjugation requests to the Adventurer’s Guild. Basically, the reward for defeating them would be paid out by that village. However, responding to the damage caused by monsters is largely up to the Lord who governs that village, and most Lords would end up paying a portion, if not all, of the reward given after said subjugation.

There are, however, a few Lords who will send out extermination forces from their own territorial army or among their private soldiers, with the Lord of this territory being among that minority. It looks like each Lord has their own response and measures against damage caused by monster attacks, though it all depends on the individual Lord. Even Jan doesn’t seem to know the details about other territories.

As we were discussing this over dinner, an unexpected fact came to light.

“What?! Arisa is Gustav’s niece?! Is he well?”  

“Ah~, well~, I haven’t seen him recently, but I think he’s probably doing well~.”  

“I see, I see! A blood relative, and a daughter of the Hamilton school’s main family? We’ve got some truly reliable backup!”

Yeah, I don’t really get it, but it looks like Jan was acquainted with Arisa’s uncle. Rather, he taught him swordsmanship during his time as an adventurer, and they may have been in the same party together for a time?

By the way, this uncle of Arisa, Gustav, it sounds like he used to be an accomplished A-Rank adventurer. Moreover, his companions at the time were Lily’s aunt, along with someone who I was surprised to hear, Harula’s Guild Master! The name of the Guild Master is Warzel, and it looks like Lily and them were in Harula because of this connection. The world is small…

“Gabras will likely be upset when I tell him about this.”

For some reason, Jan said that with a smile on his face. Who’s Gabras? Haven’t I heard that name somewhere before…? But then, this mystery was solved immediately, thanks to Arisa. Actually, I heard about him too. He was the one who taught Rad swordsmanship.

This Gabras is apparently from a branch family of the Lord’s main household, and Jan taught him swordsmanship. According to Arisa, that teaching was later passed down to Rad, making him a distant relative within the same martial school. Yeah, it’s complicated! After hearing many stories from Jan, Gabras seems to have developed a deep admiration for Gustav. While he plans to serve the Lord in the future, he is currently working as an adventurer while also undergoing training.

Anyways, it wasn’t all just casual conversation, we also discussed details about the magic beast.

The beast in question was a large, snake monster, the type referred to as the ‘Black Viper’. Lily says that when it grows up, its head will be over five to six meters high when you look up at it, and girth so large that you can’t even reach around it with both hands. And as the name would suggest, it’s poisonous.

Luckily, our opponent wasn’t so big this time, with this one being about three to four meters tall and having a girth that’s small enough, an adult man could hug it with his arms. No no, that’s still pretty big!… Come to think of it, they were attacking a lot of goats… Swallowing them whole… Scary…

As for the strategy to subjugate the Black Viper, they intend to throw javelins tied to ropes, as well as ropes fitted with hooks in order to immobilize the target, then beat it down. An easy to follow plan.

When the Village Chief was around, Jan said we’d interfere with their strategy and coordination, but that was just a pretense. In reality, he intended for us to join the battle with full force if the extermination team looked like they were in danger.

After listening to the stories of our adventures, and of our victory against the Goblin Lord’s Legion, he was relieved to know that his expectations were correct, he smiled while saying he could now fight with all his might.

In Jan’s opinion, considering the training level of the extermination squad, there will probably be a few wounded, but nothing too serious, and likely no fatalities. So, I suppose it’ll end without us doing anything? Well, it would be best if we could get paid without doing anything, it’d be easy.

The next day, before breakfast, Jan and Arisa were engaged in a fierce mock battle.

…Yeah, they had mock battles after breakfast too, then took a short break for lunch, then more mock battles until the evening. They’ve been doing this for so long. Hmm, maybe these people are from the Land of Asura?[1](https://re-library.com/translations/not-sure-another-world-reincarnation/volume-3/chapter-157-the-world-is-much-smaller-than-i-thought/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-109596)　

No no, aren’t these people too energetic?!

By the way, Jan’s win rate was overwhelmingly high. Arisa won maybe three times, but after that, she was completely defeated. All the matches she did win, she did so barely by using Feather. Yeah, Jan is incredibly strong…

Kuro jumped in for a bit too, but it was a one-sided fight, so she dropped out halfway and went for a walk with Norn instead. The level difference for Kuro was too large and didn’t feel like training. Discussing it among ourselves, we thought it best that Arisa focused on getting the combat experience instead.

Thanks to that, Arisa’s Hawk’s Eye skill, which she picked up during her matches with Rad, shot up to level 3 in one go. Also, she acquired the skill Herculean Strength at level 1! A sudden power up! Amazing!

By the way, Arisa had already acquired a skill that was higher level than Hawk’s Eye, called Precognition, but she couldn’t use it properly since her eyes couldn’t keep up. But thanks to Hawk’s Eye leveling up so quickly, she ended up finding it much easier to avoid attacks in their final mock battles.

“Well~, that was tough, but I’m glad we did it~. Thank you Jan~.”  

“It’s been a while since I’ve fought such a worthy opponent, and it helped me regain my fighting instincts. You ended up helping me.”

Yeah, these battle junkies.

But, even though I wasted the entire day together with Jan and Arisa, it wasn’t really a problem. It looks like all their preparations were almost ready, most of the supplies have already arrived at the Magistrate’s residence, and the rest will be brought tomorrow by the extermination force.

Rather, he had too much time on his hands, but he was thrilled to kill that time by sharpening his combat instincts. As expected of the Magistrate, he’s very shrewd.

By the way, Norn and Bell are acting separately. She said staying here would just make her feel sluggish, so she took Bell out for some training. Apparently, they’re close enough to sense our presence, and plan to meet up with us once we leave here after the subjugation is over.

And so, we passed the time like that, until the extermination force arrived the next day.

The force that showed up consisted of ten Knights, ten Squires, and thirty additional soldiers, fifty people in total, quite a large group. Just a note: Jan isn’t included among the ten Knights. He’s considered the Supreme Commander, and since he’s their strongest combatant, he’ll be conserving his strength for now.

Ah, in addition to the fifty, one of Jan’s personal Squires and three of his direct subordinates came along. So the final headcount for the extermination force was fifty-five, plus the four of us, and two animals.

After wrapping up the remaining preparations, we decided to get some early rest and ready ourselves for tomorrow.

Then, the next day, we finally set out to subjugate the magic beast.

# 158 – It’s all about collecting flags

“Shoot more arrows! Javelin too! Hurry!”  

“Wooooh!”  

“Hit it!”  

“Good, grab that rope! Tie it to the tree over there!”

Soldiers are busily moving about, firing their bows at the black snake, throwing javelins, or throwing ropes with hooks.

Jan loudly shouted his commands, and at times, he was busy stabbing and slashing with a long spear. Two days have passed since we departed, and we are now in the middle of the hunt for the Black Viper.

After departing from the Magistrate’s residence, we camped for a night along the way. The next day, we made our way to the area where sightings of the beast had been reported, and found the Black Viper coiled up and asleep in a slightly open area. We were then quick to deploy and went straight into battle.

For the first two hours of the battle, the Black Viper was raging and thrashing about, but over time, as javelins and hooked ropes were thrown and fastened to trees, they had gradually restricted its movements.

No, really, it was really rampaging in the beginning and soldiers kept getting blown away by its tail, it was quite a challenge. If things had continued like that, the damage would have been greater than expected, so some changes were made to the original plan.

Arisa and a few soldiers would retrieve anybody seriously injured, while Kuro, Lily, and I treated them, and as soon as we were done, they would immediately return to the fight. It ended up being a very hard battle.

Our role went like this, if the injury was minor, Kuro or I would wash the wound, apply medicine, then bandage it. For those with more serious injuries, Lily would use healing magic, and for those with severe injuries, they would use potions from the supplies that they brought.

Fortunately, if I should call it that, no one was so seriously injured that their lives were at risk, and by the looks of it, the subjugation was going to be a success. I got a bit worried when I first saw a bunch of soldiers being sent flying through the air, I started to think, ‘wouldn’t it be better to bring out the magic armor?’

“Good! Knights, approach with your polearms, and finish it off!”

While I was thinking about such things, it sounded like the Black Viper had become tightly restrained. Several heavily armored knights, including Jan, approached with long spears, poleaxes, halberds, and other such weapons in hand. Without our involvement, the operation to exterminate the Black Viper seemed to be reaching its final stage.

“Somehow, it seems like it’s going to end without any incident.”  

“Ren, if you say something like that, it’ll just cause trouble.”  

“That’s right~, it’s called a flag~.”

A ‘Flag’… Could it really have been someone reincarnated from the past who left behind those words?

“Well, if that happens, Lily can use her magic…”  

“No, isn’t that something Ren will have to take care of? …Actually, on second thought, not Ren. If you were to release your magic armor, it’ll likely cause a lot of problems, and the damage would be quite severe. There’s also my ring that strengthens the effects of magic, if I use that, maybe I could manage it… somehow? …maybe…? Yeah…”

What I’m being told feels kinda rude.

But yes, the magic armor does stand out, so if such a situation did occur, maybe I’ll use the improved, but power reduced, Burst Dagger?

When I first used them against the Frost Giant, the explosion range was much larger than I expected, but since then, I’ve made several new varieties with suppressed explosive power. Of course, the original explosive power can still be used in an emergency.

Still I did hold back when I made that… or at least I thought I did. Considering the explosive power from the earliest type of Burst Dagger, I wonder how much damage it would cause if it were an All Attribute Magic Sword that would explode.

Well, that’s how it is, with the new model prioritizing ease of use and reduced destructive power, it would possibly take down an enemy by blowing off just the head, I think.

While I was talking with Lily and them, the Knights managed to cut off the Black Viper’s head. Fast, huh? … Arisa, who was watching the fight while chatting with us, said they were swinging their weapons down without any restraint, hitting the ground with loud BANG! BANG! sounds. Eh, scary…

Anyways, without collecting any flags, the Black Viper subjugation operation ended successfully, but we’ve still got some clean up to do after the battle.

Even though the fighting was over, soldiers were busy running around, collecting weapons that had been knocked away, or clearing ropes that had been tied here and there.

Some of the faster runners ran ahead to report to the Lord. Also, they usually would need to bring more manpower to help collect the Black Viper’s body, which would have been a lot of work, but since I have a large capacity magic bag (which is actually me using Storage), the efforts in collecting and transporting it had been greatly reduced.

When I listened to the talks of their operation, it all seemed rather difficult, so after checking with Lily, I decided to help with the retrieval.

By the way, when Jan heard about the magic bag, he started looking very covetous. Well, no one asked me to give it to them though. If it’s a large capacity magic bag, the selling price would be astronomical…

I mean, it is a useful item, so I can understand why people look at me like that… Apparently, it’s a lot of work to transport the collected taxes. Hmm, soldiers and high-ranking officials alike have it tough.

Well, we’re still busy treating the injured, so it’s pretty hard work…

After cleaning up to some extent, we set up our tents and camped here for the night. No surprise, after such a big catch, nobody has the strength left to travel long distances.

The soldiers were too exhausted to cook their own meals, but since we weren’t too tired, we decided to cook for everyone. Rather… It was Kuro who first made the suggestion. ‘We still have energy left, so let’s make some food for everyone!’ she said.

Eeeh, seriously?

No, we’ll have to make a lot because of how many people are here, isn’t this going to be a lot of work?

Well, what’s been decided can’t be helped. The soldiers brought with them plenty of supplies… So we decided to make a large amount of stew.

… After the meal was over, even Kuro, who first suggested it, was slumped over, exhausted, and looking as if she wished she’d never suggested such a thing.

Then at night, everyone slept in their own tents.

I also restrained myself and used a homemade tent. Carriage? As expected, I didn’t use it in order to match the marching speed. First off, the Black Viper’s habitat was predicted to be in the mountains. In addition, we were in charge of cooking, therefore we didn’t have to take part in the night watch. Thank you.

So I’m lounging around inside my tent, thinking about various things. I’m using a camping mattress that I had made so that my body doesn’t get cold. I made it well enough so that it had excellent insulation. Incidentally, I also lent the same thing to Lily, Arisa, and Kuro.

So, I’m thinking about some ideas for improving weapons.

It occurred to me while watching the Black Viper subjugation. Today, I was considering using a Burst Dagger if necessary. Actually, I had created it as a last resort.

Originally, I was training my blacksmithing with the goal of making projectile weapons for my [Sword Control Magic], and this is the resulting projectile sword, or at least the blade part. But due to the various powerful enchantments attached to it, it can no longer be so easily thrown away. After firing them out in great numbers, if someone were to pick one up… Thinking about that, I can only imagine all sorts of terrifying things.

You would think it would be fine if I just didn’t attach any effects, but that’s still not the case, as the quality of the swords used as materials are all of the highest grade, ‘Supreme Sword’. This is also something that I can’t just throw away.

Its penetration power is guaranteed. However, they’re supposed to be disposable bullet replacements, and if they’re scattered around carelessly, future repercussions are guaranteed to be quite frightening.

So my idea was reversed, and the Burst Dagger was created, making it disposable rather than retrievable. By releasing the magic that is attached to it, the dagger would explode and shatter into pieces, preventing someone from picking it up and reusing it later.

Even though I had lowered the effects of the initial Burst Dagger, there was still a problem in its explosive power being higher than expected, and I ended up improving it by reducing its explosive power in order to make it easier to use. But the improved version hasn’t been used in combat, so I don’t know what the results will be.

By the way, the visual collection range of [Storage] is approximately 50 meters, though if it’s something that I own, I can store it at a distance of up to 200 meters, if I try hard, but I have to be able to see it with my eyes, and for some reason, it makes me feel strangely tired.

Incidentally, seriously firing a sword using [Sword Control Magic], even using the shortest estimate, it would still fly a distance far beyond 200 meters, so at maximum range, it would be impossible to retrieve. The actual range has been proven to some extent when I was using the Burst Daggers against the Frost Giant.

I’ve talked about a lot of things, but the problem was that it was difficult to retrieve any sword bullets after firing them, so if I could just find a way to recover them, it would actually be usable in combat.

Then, I came up with the idea, ‘Why not just connect them with string?’

Well, you see, during today’s subjugation, the soldiers were swinging around javelins and hooks with rope attached, if they missed or didn’t catch, they’d pull the rope to retrieve it and throw it again. So in the same way, I’d use rope or string… Or maybe chains would do, so why not make something like that and connect them together? That’s what I thought.

The swords I prepared as ammunition for [Sword Control Magic] were still unfinished blades, so I thought it might be a good idea to attach a strong chain made of magic steel to the eyelet holes in the stalk.

I feel that for a dagger-sized blade for everyday use, steel thread might be sufficient. If I make the chains and steel wire themselves very rigid, they’ll be less likely to get cut by the enemy’s weapon after being dodged, and if they don’t miss, I can just reel them back in right away.

Also, it might be a good idea to make various tips without being limited to just a sword shape. For example, a weight? With that, you could trap your opponent and then use lightning magic to send out an electric shock. You can send out an electric shock when using a dagger though. Either way, it would increase the number of cards I could bring to battle.

Well, I won’t know until I actually try it. Still, there are a few issues… but I guess I’ll just have to make it and see how it goes. Now I just have to secure the time and place to make it… I’d like to sit down somewhere and make it calmly, but I could also just make it while travelling in the carriage. I might not be able to relax if Lily gets involved, but in that case, I can just throw her into the driver’s seat.

Mhm, the ideas have come together rather nicely. Good, good.

So is this the next thing I’ll make? I’ve got a few other ideas in mind to create, but I don’t have the materials for that yet, so I’ll deal with it later.

Also, I think I’ll try making something I had in mind for Mina, or rather, Anna? I’ll have to be up early in the morning to travel again, maybe I can make it tomorrow while we’re camping. Considering the materials being used, this one should be easy to make. I think it’ll be fine.

Now that that’s decided, it’s time to go to bed. Good Night~.

# 159 – Hehehe… We’ve got the best medicine, sir~

So there was nothing noteworthy on our way back and we returned to the Magistrate’s residence.

Eh? Too fast? Rolling along, rolling along. What? I was going to make something? Ah, I made it quickly without any trouble.

I don’t quite get it, but if I imagine what it is I want to make, and pick up the various ingredients needed, I kinda get an idea as to what materials I need. This, at first, I thought it was because my skill level had increased, but I feel like it’s probably something different, somehow. It’s probably just me, but I think it’s because [Creation Magic] and [Analyze] are interacting nicely. No, there wasn’t a particular reason, it was just a feeling. It’s sort of like a hunch, that’s what it felt like.

Anyways, although we made it back to the Magistrate’s residence, we decided to leave early. You see, everyone seemed busy with reports, cleaning and whatnot, and we have been here for about a week now.

Jan seemed like he wanted me to help him transport the materials for the Black Viper to the Lord’s residence, but there were reasons not to, such as leaving work for the laborers who came to do their job and ensuring that money was circulating for the people of the territory, so we weren’t asked to stay. It must be tough for the ruling class… Maybe it’s not so bad for serious people if they do the job properly… However, compared to transporting goods from deep in the mountains, the roads in the plains are fairly well maintained, so it’s still better.

But it seemed like Jan’s main reason was that he wanted to have more fun with Arisa, rather than transporting items. He really was a battle junkie…

Arisa seemed reluctant to accept another match with Jan, so we took her and returned to the village.

The village was lively, almost like during a festival, with people busy recruiting laborers for transportation and preparing for the celebration after the beast subjugation.

Hmm, we should probably leave immediately, else they’ll likely keep asking us to celebrate with them.

And when we returned to the Village Chief, he stopped us, as expected. Well, free food is appreciated, so we decided to take him up on his offer. However, they’ll be serving wild boar steaks, which they only serve on special occasions, so it made me a little excited.

The celebration was quite a success. Or rather, it was a big fuss. It seems that among the 30 soldiers who went on the subjugation, several were from this village, and it seems that some of them were allowed to go home temporarily due to labour recruitment and other matters. According to the Village Chief, this was the same for the other villages. As there was going to be a festival, Jan instructed them to spread the tale of the subjugation, as it would increase his popularity with the Lord, and appease the people in the territory. The reason they couldn’t send all the soldiers back is because they still have security work and other tasks… The Village Chief said he believed that those who’ve yet to return will likely be compensated for it later.

By the way, Arisa voluntarily participated in the subjugation story telling. Although she didn’t earn any personal military achievement this time, and it was a small-scale battle, it was her first time participating in a group battle, which she found fun. She had learned a lot from the experience, and apparently wanted to hear directly from the soldiers who had participated. During the subjugation, Arisa had been watching from the side-lines, and expressed her impressions of the soldier’s movements from her point of view; she ended up talking about various things with the other soldiers.

Me? I’m squishy, so I was eating my steak. It was really delicious. Next to me was Kuro, who was silently eating her meat.

Uh, looking closely at Arisa, is she drinking with the soldiers? …Well, both Lily and Arisa are 15 this year. 15 is the legal drinking age… I’m jealous. Ah, I wanna turn 15 soon too, I want to drink the large quantities of handmade alcoholic beverages I’ve put away in Storage…

I’ve heard that it’s usually not a big deal if someone under 15 years of age drinks a little, though some people will frown upon it, they usually don’t make too big of a fuss. I intend to stick to the rules for now though. Well, I do sometimes taste a little bit to check the quality of the alcohol I made, or to use it in cooking.

Anyways, it’ll be problematic if something went wrong, so I grabbed Arisa and returned to the detached building of the Village Chief’s house. It’s already getting late and we are leaving tomorrow.

“Arisa! Don’t drink alcohol! Come on!”  

“Lily, lets drink~, really it tasted bad and I didn’t wanna at first, but now it’s fluffy and fun~.”  

“Hey, stand up and walk properly! We have to get up early tomorrow too! And I’m not 15 yet! It’s still a month away!”  

“Ahahahaha~.”

Oh, this is no good.

I took the drunk Arisa back to the detached house, and Lily is somehow looking after her, or I should say she’s keeping her company.

“Aha~, Ahaha~.”  

“Wait, get changed properly and go to bed! Here!”

Hmm, maybe Arisa is a part of a subspecies of laughing drinkers? I suppose she’s a bit confrontational too? …Come to think of it, she said the alcohol tastes bad… Hmm, maybe she would enjoy a simple but sweeter alcoholic drink. Actually, I’m also curious about this bad tasting alcohol. From what I’ve seen so far, the alcohol consumed in this world is possibly beer, or ale? It doesn’t look like they’ve got beer, or rather, lager beer yet. Well, I got some in my Storage! I collected the hops from plants in the forest. I think I’ve also seen it in pharmacies as stomach medicine?

Wine seems to be sold normally, and I’ve seen some fruit liqueurs around too… I think there was mead as well? I don’t remember very well…

So what about sweet alcoholic beverages, like fruit liquor or mead? Well, if it doesn’t exist, I just need to make it, or maybe just dilute fruit juice with a flavourless alcohol? Alcoholic beverages such as vodka and gin, I already made using wheat and potatoes. High-concentration alcohol can also be used as a disinfectant, and has many other uses.

…Yeah, naturally, I’ve also prepared distilled liquor. Like whiskey or brandy. The aging rate is increased by using [Creation Magic], so 20 year old bottles actually exist already. But, I’ve never seen any distilled alcohol either, it may turn quite dangerous if I put these out into the public. It might just be a coincidence that I’ve never seen them though.

And as I was deep in thought while watching Lily struggling with Arisa, Anna brought us a bucket of water. Thank you.

I could have used water magic, but I don’t want to fight a drunk person. Meanwhile, Lily started filling a wooden cup with water from the bucket and started making Arisa drink it. Hmm, Lily is strong.

Ah, right. Now’s a good time to give that to Anna! My homemade medicine!

As for its use, it’s to help address what Mina was worried about, regarding Anna’s breastfeeding. To briefly explain, it uses magic to enhance medical properties, promotes the secretion of breast milk and magically relieves blockages in the mammary glands.

By the way, it’s quite effective and is intended to be diluted before use. If taken undiluted, you’ll end up producing an insane amount of breast milk for a few days, so be careful. If diluted, you should use a few tablespoons of it in the bucket? So in a cup, it would probably just be one or a few drops.

As I explained this, I handed Anna three potion bottles. Three bottles should last her about six months to a year, I think. Well, it depends on how often you use them… You’re not going to share them with the wives in the neighbourhood, right? …Just be careful.

“Eh, such a valuable item… is it really okay?”  

“Yeah, please do. I don’t use it. However, please be careful not to use it incorrectly. Also, if you share it with your neighbours, please be sure to teach them how to use it properly… If used incorrectly, it will cause a big problem.”  

“Yes, I’ll be careful…”  

“You’d better keep it out of reach of small children.”  

“I understand, certainly… I will.”

Yeah, seriously, be careful.

This medicine, because it works on people of all ages and genders. It’ll also work on animals. It would even be helpful for dairy cows to drink it… Yeah, when I appraised it, it said ‘It works for both men and women, and even animals’. In other words, if you give it to an old man or a young girl to drink, it could cause disastrous problems!

Well done Ren! You can now try a new style of play! No way! Who would do such a maniac play?!

…No, seriously, I won’t… I don’t have that kind of fetish, really.

While talking like that, it looks like Arisa fell asleep. Lily, thank you so much for your hard work. Kuro? Kuro returned back to the detached house with an unconcerned attitude and fell asleep early.

“…You’ve created some amazing medicine. When did you make something like that?”  

“Ehm, while camping?”  

“While camping.”  

“Yes. Like this, just a bit.”  

“Just a bit.”  

“Yes.”  

“……”

… She looked like she wanted to say something. But I responded like I knew nothing.

“…How should I put this… No, should we just go to bed?”  

“Right, let’s go to bed.”

It looked like she had a lot she wanted to say, but she kept it to herself and kept quiet. You’ve grown up, Lily…

“Goodnight.”

Yeah, goodnight~.

---

### Translator’s Remarks:

The idea of Ren getting drunk sounds terrifying. She’ll end up getting black out drunk and waking up in the royal capital in her magic armor with her house crashed sideways through the wall. Half the city will be frozen over with ice magic, and Neil will be passed out next to her with no pants on and a bottle shoved up his a̲s̲s̲. I kinda can’t wait until she turns 15.

Also some trivia, at least as far as I’ve been running this through the translation machine, that last moment when Ren remarks that Lily grew up seems to be the first time she’s stuck no honorific on the end of her name. Why would I note that? In case it’s the start of improved friendship. The first instance was right here.

# 160 – Equipment Restrictions Lifted

Good morning.

We’ve been preparing to leave since early this morning. That being said, there isn’t much to do. I’ve retrieved the mattresses and put everything back to the way it was, I guess I just have to pack my luggage? Basically, almost all of my luggage is put away in [Storage], so really, it’s just the rest of the party’s luggage. Two of them just had to put their clothes away in the magic bags that they borrowed, so once they threw it all in, our task was over in no time.

Once we’ve finished packing, we went over to the Village Chief’s house to say our goodbyes before leaving. The Chief was already awake and was busy recording things in what looked like a ledger, while his wife and Anna were preparing breakfast. Mina was still asleep.

“Oh, good morning. Anna tells me that you’ll be leaving soon… Though I don’t mind if you take your departure a bit slower…”  

“No no, we would feel uncomfortable to rely on you for too long, and besides, adventurers are meant to travel.”  

“I see, that is certainly true… Then, please be careful, and I wish you all a safe journey.”  

“Thank you very much, well then, we’ll be on our way…”

And with that, Lily wrapped up the conversation quickly after giving a brief goodbye.

By the way, we declined breakfast. That’s because we were given a huge lunch box! It had black bread, leafy vegetables, and diced leftover steak from the night before. There was enough food in there for all four of us to have three meals for the day. No, hey, this was too much. But hey, we were grateful for the free food, so we accepted it without hesitation.

We went to the stables, retrieved the horse golems, and tied them to the carriage parked next to the detached building, then we were ready to go. Ah, by the way, I’ve improved the horse golems so that they can pretend to eat. Since we travel by carriage a lot, it would be very suspicious if the horses and carriage suddenly disappeared while staying at an inn in town, so I included this function to camouflage them better.

Then everyone got on board the carriage and we started to move. We made our way through the village and headed out.

The festivities were still in full swing in the village square. However, there were drunk people passed out all over the place, making for a rather strange sight.

Seeing the villagers like that, Arisa had a strange look on her face. Please drink alcohol in moderation…

As we were leaving, Mina chased after us and said goodbye. After that, we left the village and headed for the highway. After driving for a while, I suddenly opened the window and stuck my head out, turning to look back at the village.

In the end, we ended up staying in that village for almost ten days… Am I getting sentimental, or maybe not?

“We stayed in that village for quite a while.”  

“Yea…”  

“I never thought I’d end up participating in the Knight’s subjugation operation.”  

“Mhm.”  

“Well, I wasn’t a combat soldier, I was just providing support in the back while treating the injured… But it was the first time I’ve ever used so much healing magic.”  

“That’s right.”

“But thanks to this ring that Ren gave me, my magic consumption was reduced, so I managed to pull through.”  

“Is that so?”  

“Yes.”  

“I see.”  

“Ren? Are you listening to me properly?”  

“I didn’t hear.”  

“Reeeen?!”

No, wait, what is it? I’m catching about half of it, but I’m still listening properly! Actually, I’m concentrating on calling Norn and Bell, so could you please be a bit quieter?!

Well, you see, Norn and Bell were supposed to meet up with us when we left the village, but they haven’t come back yet. I’m currently using [Familiar Synchronization] to try and find out where they were.

So I’ve been sending out thoughts for a while, and it turns out that Bell would be training for a few more days before they would join up again. It looks like they know our location. I see?

Well, they aren’t children, once they’ve finished what they’re doing, they’ll come back soon.

When I told the rest of the party about Norn and Bell, they had the same opinion as me. Arisa said that they’re probably doing teamwork training just for the two of them.

That being said, if Norn and Bell aren’t around, we’ll have to take turns with the night watch, but there’s no problems for now. Rather, Lily and Arisa sometimes stay up throughout the night even when Norn and Bell are around, so that they have proper training and experience in that sort of thing. I have homemade potions to keep me awake so I don’t accidentally fall asleep. Though, this does seem like it would be really bad for my health… If there is a problem, it would probably be from Kuro, so she’ll stay awake together with me until she gets used to it.

After setting up the night rotation like that, we started travelling again to the hot springs. And as I had planned, I started improving my weapons.

By the way, I told Lily, “I want to concentrate on my work,” so she moved to the driver’s seat in disappointment. Now, Kuro is in the passenger cabin, but she’s just been sleeping the entire time. She seems like she’s catching up for the night… Well, whatever, as long as she’s quiet, it’s fine.

The first thing to make is steel threads. Rather than making the main item straight away, I’ll start by making things that I can use on a daily basis, and gain some experience.

Hmm, if it’s too thin, I’m afraid I might slice my finger off… Let’s make it a little thicker. And to increase durability, something like that, and this, and that… and attach…

Okay, that feels good. I’ve tried pulling and bending it, but it’s not like a wire, but more like a soft string. How strange. By the way, I have thinner ones prepared as well. Cutting things up with steel threads, or stretching them around to create a restricted area, it’s romantic to do something like that.

Next, once it’s finished, it’s connected into a dagger-sized sword. When I say ‘connected’, I don’t mean simply tying it directly to the sword, rather like passing a metal ring through the eyelet and connecting the steel thread to that metal ring… Good, good, that feels nice.

Then, I stored the completed item in [Storage], then activated [Sword Control Magic], taking out the sword from Storage and keeping it in the air. Then, about half of the blade suddenly appeared from the empty air and remained motionless.

…This, it looks exactly like Gate of Baby…ahem.[1](https://re-library.com/translations/not-sure-another-world-reincarnation/volume-3/chapter-160-equipment-restrictions-lifted/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-117762)　

Yeah, this is fine! No Problems!

After working that far, it was time for a lunch break. Lily is on cooking duty again today, so I stepped away from the carriage for a bit, and found a random tree beside the road to aim and shoot at, using the dagger I had modified earlier. I fired it at the speed of a pistol bullet, **CLANG!** It hit the tree with a high-pitched noise.

…Hmm, I thought the wire would cause the bullet speed to slow down, but that doesn’t seem to be the case… Actually, it feels like I can still increase the speed even further.

By the way, the wire extended out from the hollow space where it was emitted from, so it really does look just like the Gilded King.[2](https://re-library.com/translations/not-sure-another-world-reincarnation/volume-3/chapter-160-equipment-restrictions-lifted/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-117762)　

Anyways, in this state, use [Storage] and put it away… Ah, it disappeared in an instant. This is convenient. This solves the problem I’ve been having up until now… Seems to have been an easy solution.

Hmm, if that happens, then… Ah, let’s see if we can tow with it. I pulled out a suitable piece of wood from [Storage], then aimed a dagger at it and, hit. Then, from this state, “Store the steel wire by winding it up inside [Storage].”

…Oh, it’s working. The wood is being pulled towards me… Yeah, this is nice! With this, I can pull things that I see in the distance closer, won’t that have many uses? Okay, later I’ll make a large warhead with an arrowhead like a barb too.

Hmm, is there anything else I can try…? Let’s try to see if I can hit it in a curved shot, I’m able to interfere with the trajectory to a certain extent and hit the target, so this should work. Let’s get started.

**Swish! CLANG!**

Yeah. Hitting a target in an arc is easy to do.

Next up… If I can bend it at a sharp angle, I could add some variety to my attacks, wouldn’t I? After it gets dodged, the dagger turns around and hits my target from behind, and… that’s it!

**Swish! Clink! CLANG!**

Oh, I did it, I did it. This will have a variety of useful applications. For example, I could fire off multiple swords in different directions, attacking the target from multiple directions simultaneously and at different times… This would make defending and evasion very difficult, which would be powerful.

Yeah, Yeah, good, good! I was concentrating really hard, but shouldn’t dinner be ready by now…? Thinking that, I turned around and saw both Lily and Arisa looking at me with blank expressions on their faces. What’s wrong?

“Huh? Is something wrong?”  

“Ah… No, I was just thinking that you were doing something amazing, and…”  

“Ah, I was practicing a new attack, or rather experimenting… well, something like that.”  

“I, I see…?”  

“Lily, that’s bad, it might be hard for me to avoid or prevent that~.”  

“Eh, even Arisa?”  

“Yeah, that speed might be serious~.”  

“Eeeh…”

The two of them looked shocked.

“The situations where the magic armor can be used are quite limited… Anyway, is dinner ready yet?”  

“Ah! Sorry, my hands stopped working!…I’ll make it right away!”

Really, Lily is no good.

“Really~ Lily is no good~.”  

“Arisa, you were also frozen! Come on, don’t just stand there, come help!”  

“Yeees~.”

And there’s the usual husband-wife back and forth… Maybe they were trying to instigate?

… By the way, Kuro was still asleep in the carriage.

That was the first day of our resumed travels, the journey continued after that, with me creating equipment while moving, and test firing during breaks. Along the way, Norn and Bell rejoined us.

By the way, since then, I’ve been making a lot of chains and creating ammunition from one-handed swords and greatswords. I’ve even prepared some special bullets with different attributes for different purposes.

As a basic function, it’s set up so that if the target is not hit, the weapon is immediately retrieved into [Storage].

Next, if the target is hit, the sword bullet is immediately retrieved when it pierces the target and stops moving completely. However, this setting can be turned off at will.

Furthermore, when automatic retrieval is turned off, if the target tries to fight back or cut the chain or steel thread while its still stuck, the threat level of the attack is automatically determined, and if there is a risk of damage, the item will be immediately retrieved.

This is because the sword bullets are half-stored in [Storage] via chains, because they were in a state of pseudo-contact with me through [Storage], it was then just a simple application of [Appraisal]. Although it’s not possible to make a detailed appraisal due to having too many things in between, it seems like I can get a vague idea of the strength of my target.

Then referring to the sensations felt, the function then automatically recollects the item based on the automatically calculated threat level of the opponent’s attack. It’s all so convenient, I’m honestly having trouble commenting.

And from here, let me explain the various special ammunitions.

First up, the Burst Dagger, now called the “Burst Bullet”.

This doesn’t simply spread the explosion when it goes off, the skill [Final Strike] can be adjusted, allowing the explosion to cover the desired range. By narrowing the range, it increases the destructive power, making it a special bullet with maximum firepower. The explosive force itself is made differently along several stages, but when using an All-Attribute Magic Sword, which boasts the maximum firepower, the target will likely be completely burned to ashes. This makes it impossible to recover materials, meaning it should be considered a last resort and shouldn’t be used lightly.

Next, a special bullet with enhanced bullet speed and penetration power, used for long-distance sniping, the “Penetrator.”

This bullet has been imbued with the weapon skill [Penetrate], which allows projectiles and piercing attacks to bypass defenses. [Penetrate] is a magical enhancement based on the concept of a ‘recoilless hammer,’ forming an artificial cutting edge at the weapon’s tip using magical energy. By creating a slight gap between this magical edge and the actual tip, the impact’s kinetic energy is focused into the target, allowing it to pierce through without losing force or leaving residue behind.

Additionally, the skill amplifies kinetic energy, further increasing its penetrative power. On top of that, I applied [Attribute Enhancement: Wind] to boost the projectile’s speed, effectively turning it into a specialized sniping bullet.

Finally, there’s the automatic tracking type “Tindalos.”

Anyone familiar with the name will know what it mean, the bullet is imbued with the weapon skill [Hound of Tindalos][3](https://re-library.com/translations/not-sure-another-world-reincarnation/volume-3/chapter-160-equipment-restrictions-lifted/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-117762), which, once it locks onto a target, will relentlessly pursue it until impact. The effect of [Hound of Tindalos] is exactly what the name implies.

However, because this skill consumes a large portion of the weapon’s available capacity, the levels of other imbued skills had to be reduced to compensate. As a result, the bullet is less lethal compared to standard bullets when it comes to raw damage output.

I’ve thought up a few others that may or may not be effective, but my time’s up for now. From here, we’ll be heading to our destination, the hot springs, on foot… Or rather.

“Now that I think about it, I never asked properly, but what kind of place is this hot spring? Is it a village or a hot spring town somewhere?”  

“Ah, I didn’t explain the details. Our destination is a hot spring that wells up deep in the mountains. It’s said to be at the end of the mountain path, next to that landmark rock.”

Lily pointed to a large rock on the river bank, next to a small river that runs alongside the road. Looking closely, I can see a frequently travelled mountain path beside the rock, which branches off, leading into the forest, and a very thin stream that runs parallel to that path, which merges with the river.

“I see, is it the source of that stream…?”

In that case, we’ll have to make some adjustments to make it more comfortable… Alright, this uncle is going to make whatever he likes.

And just as I was feeling motivated, we put the carriage away and started walking through the forest, which turned into a mountain climb.

Yeah, I feel that by the time I reach the hot spring, I’ll be so exhausted that I won’t want to do anything…!

---

### Translator Note:

She compares herself to Gilgamesh, but I’m seeing more similarities to her and Pinhead. All she had to do is bait people to open a puzzle box, then send the chains after them.

# Reborn as a Transcendent - Chapter 677 - Trifold Preparation of [Death of Love]

At the Rosen Hotel, in this very moment.

“Princess says she’s on her way!” Nangong set her phone down, her voice full of excitement. The entire group lit up with joy, each of them smiling brightly.

“Should we invite Rakshasa and Little Fairy too?” Yunuen asked.  

“It’s already quite late. It might not be appropriate, and they live far from here,” Nangong replied, shaking her head.

Although her relationship with Rakshasa wasn’t the best, Nangong wasn’t the kind to exclude someone out of personal bias.

“It’s too late now. Let’s plan it for another time,” Mylene agreed.  

“Exactly. We don’t know if the Small Sword Group has something else planned. Better to stay cautious,” Snowy added.  

“I didn’t think of that…” Yunuen said, clearly embarrassed.  

“It’s fine,” Nangong said, gently patting her shoulder. “We’ll find time for everyone to meet next time.”  

“Okay!” Yunuen nodded enthusiastically.

“Snowy, have your people keep a close watch on Little Fairy,” Nangong said, her tone turning serious. After what had happened to Yunuen, she had no intention of letting history repeat itself. If Little Fairy were abducted, she wouldn’t be able to face Princess.

“Of course,” Snowy replied, nodding before pulling out her phone to send a message.  

“I’ll have my people monitor things too,” Mylene offered.  

“As for Rakshasa—”

“She’s perfectly safe where she is,” Mylene interrupted before Nangong could finish.  

“The higher-ups must value her a lot,” Nangong said, pursing her lips. “Do all Closed Beta players get this kind of treatment?”  

“Her case is a bit unusual. I can’t share the details,” Mylene replied.  

“I see.” Nangong didn’t press further. Instead, she turned to Sachiel. “Lil’ Sachiel, did you let the kitchen know?”  

“Yes. I told the general manager. They’re already preparing everything,” Sachiel said, putting her phone away with a smile.  

“Great. Now all that’s left is for Princess to arrive,” Nangong said cheerfully.

She had only seen Princess recently, but as the saying went, days could feel like years. Time passed differently when you missed someone, it dragged in a way that ordinary moments never did.

Just then, a soft noise came from the window. Everyone turned and saw a breathtakingly beautiful girl floating outside in a pure white dress, waving at them. It was Yaeger, radiant as ever.

“Princess!” they exclaimed, nearly jumping to their feet in unison.

Nangong was the first to act, rushing to open the window. As soon as she did, a gentle, comforting fragrance drifted in. Yaeger floated into the room and gave everyone a quick glance. “Good evening, everyone.”

“Good evening, Princess!” Sachiel practically bounced toward her with excitement, followed closely by Yunuen and the others. The entire suite was suddenly filled with warmth and energy.

But while things were joyful here, elsewhere the mood was far gloomier. At the Adventurers’ Guild in Jade City…

Taurus looked furious. “What have you all been doing? It’s been a full day, and you still haven’t found Black-hearted Princess!” he roared, slamming the table in rage.

‘Useless trash,’ he thought, though he kept those words to himself. Everyone present lowered their heads without saying a word.

Everyone in the room was a core member of the Death of Love Guild. In other words, they were all paid professionals. They were paid to get results, and they had delivered nothing. None of them dared speak up, unless they wanted to quit on the spot.

‘The Jade Empire is enormous. If she really wanted to hide, finding her would be like searching for a needle in the sea,’ S.K.Y. thought. In his view, Taurus was just venting.

Watching everyone lower their heads like scolded children only fueled Taurus’ rage. But rather than explode again, he forced himself to cool down and reevaluate their situation.

“How many more have reached Level twenty recently?” he asked, forcing down his irritation and speaking with measured calm.  

“Another two thousand. At this rate, the main force will be fully formed after one more day of leveling,” S.K.Y. replied steadily. By now, there was an invisible wall between them, and it felt unbreakable.

“Very good,” Taurus said with a nod, satisfied by the report. The fire of his anger began to cool. His guild was already among the top five in Cathay. Once the entire main force surpassed Level 20, Death of Love would not only become the most powerful guild in the nation but also break into the top five globally.

‘Heh… by then, every player across the world will know the name Taurus Zhang.’ The idea of becoming an international icon among players made him grin.

When the others saw him smiling, a wave of relief swept through the room.

“Good work,” Taurus said, giving S.K.Y. a firm pat on the shoulder.

S.K.Y. offered a faint smirk, his expression calm and unreadable. In that moment, Taurus sensed the distance that had grown between them. His heart skipped slightly before he pulled himself together and began to reflect.

‘So he’s still bitter over that slap. We used to be so close, like brothers… Is it really worth holding onto something so petty? If he just stays loyal, he’ll achieve greatness and wealth.’ Taurus clenched his jaw. He had already decided, once his plan was complete, S.K.Y. would be removed. Someone like him couldn’t be left unchecked.

Taurus slowly withdrew his hand and continued. “Are you telling me we still have no idea where Black-hearted Princess is?”

The room fell silent. After a moment, someone stepped forward. It was a young male Priest in his twenties, average-looking, with the in-game tag [Big Bowl Noodles]. “Young Master Zhang, I might have something,” he said. “We’ve been investigating for the past few days and have pieced together her general movement pattern.”

“Then why haven’t you found her?” Taurus snapped in frustration.

His expression shifted slightly as he paused to think, then finally spoke. “Young Master Zhang, it’s not from lack of effort. Her range of activity is just too vast.” As he spoke, he unrolled a rough sketch.

The diagram outlined Yaeger’s movements, from Jade City, to the wastelands, then the docks, the swamps, and finally the Canyon of the Dead.

Looking at the diagram, Taurus finally grasped the scale of the issue. ‘This is worse than I thought. She’s practically crossed half a province.’ Finding someone across that much terrain was no different from searching for a needle in the ocean.

“Here’s what we’ll do. Split into two teams. One will search around Jade City, the other near the docks.” After some thought, Taurus decided that populated areas offered the best chance.

“Young Master Zhang, there’s a new report,” S.K.Y. said. “A plague is spreading near the docks. It’s unlikely Black-hearted Princess would be there.”

Taurus was about to agree, but something clicked in his mind. “S.K.Y., that reasoning is flawed. You know what they say, the most dangerous place is often the safest. Normal people might avoid a plague zone, but we’re players. Why would we care?”

His words struck like lightning, snapping everyone out of their daze. Of course—they weren’t NPCs. Why should a plague matter to them?

“I was too caught up in the game’s logic and forgot the bigger picture. That was careless.” S.K.Y. instinctively reached to adjust his glasses, only to remember they didn’t exist in this world.

“As expected of Young Master Zhang. You spotted what none of us could.”  

“You’re incredible, sir!”  

“Truly sharp, as always.”

The room filled with praise and flattery, which brought a satisfied smile to Taurus’ face. After letting the praise continue for a while, Taurus finally raised a hand, signaling everyone to quiet down.

“The docks are more dangerous,” he said. “Only send people above Level twenty. If you find any clues, report to me immediately. Do not alert her before I give the order.”

“Yes!” S.K.Y. and the core members responded together.

“We also need to prepare a backup plan,” Taurus said, tapping the table rhythmically with his fingers before continuing.  

“What are you planning, Young Master Zhang?” S.K.Y. asked.  

“If we still can’t locate her, then we’ll need to draw her out,” Taurus replied coolly, casting a glance around the room.  

“How do you suggest we do that?” a core member asked.  

“The simplest method would be to take a hostage,” S.K.Y. replied.  

Taurus nodded. “Indeed.”  

“But her subordinates, Mahou Shoujo Yunuen and Little Fairy, left Jade City a while ago,” the core member added, looking hesitant.  

“What? And you’re only telling me this now?”

Taurus’ right eyelid twitched sharply. If they hadn’t been in public, he would’ve kicked off his boots and stabbed the man with the pointed heel.

Everyone fell silent.

Someone had definitely brought it up the day before, but Taurus hadn’t been paying attention. Now he was blaming them for it. If he weren’t their boss, several of them might have already jumped him.

“Forget it. Just keep tracking their movements. Once we capture one of them, Black-hearted Princess is bound to appear,” Taurus said, waving his hand impatiently.  

“Young Master Zhang, I might have another way to lure her out,” S.K.Y. said, leaning in.  

“Let’s hear it,” Taurus said, stepping closer.

S.K.Y. leaned in and quietly whispered the third plan into his ear. Taurus’ eyes lit up with delight, and a satisfied smile slowly spread across his face.

---

In the real world, inside the Rosen Hotel suite, the girls sat around the table chatting as they enjoyed their meal. The atmosphere was warm and full of laughter.

“Princess, you have to try this one!” Nangong said enthusiastically, continuing to serve Yaeger with unrelenting zeal.

At first, Yaeger tried to refuse, but Nangong’s persistence wore her down. Eventually, she allowed herself to be doted on.

Sachiel, Mylene, and Yunuen watched with a mix of amusement and envy. Across the table, Pixie began doing the same. Nangong glared at her, so irritated she looked like she might punch her square in the chest.

Once supper was over, the group lingered around the table, sipping tea and chatting casually. Eventually, Mylene brought up the real reason for their gathering. “Sister, there’s something I need to tell you…”

Yaeger listened quietly, then paused in thought before replying.

“Personally, I don’t think it’s dangerous at all. But if it’ll ease your minds, Mylene and Lil’ Pixie can come with me.”

+++

# 678 – Another Enemy Makes a Dazzling Entrance

“Well, alright then. We won’t go,” Nangong Lin said, sounding somewhat disappointed. She immediately turned to Pixie. “I’m entrusting you with my best camera.”

“Huh?” Pixie looked at her in confusion.

“Princess’ heroic moments must be recorded by you!” Nangong Lin placed one hand firmly on Pixie’s shoulder and spoke seriously.

The other girls who couldn’t go to the scene looked on expectantly.

“Sister, just to be safe, how about I ask the higher-ups to dispatch a fishery patrol ship?” Mylene suggested. Considering that the other party might hire a small nation’s military force to stage an ambush, she thought it would be best to increase their deterrence.

“You mean the ship with a displacement of sixty-seven thousand tons?” Pixie asked jokingly.

Everyone looked confused for a second, then immediately turned shocked. If that fishery patrol ship really sailed out there, the surrounding small countries would probably panic to death.

“No need for that. I have my own ways to monitor the surroundings. If there’s even the slightest sign of trouble, we’ll immediately leave,” Yaeger shook her head.

“Sister, it’s always good to prepare for emergencies. If not the patrol ship, how about I ask the higher-ups to send two submarines instead?” Mylene persisted, sounding uneasy.

Listening to her talk about giant fishery patrol ships and submarines, everyone’s faces started twitching involuntarily. Just what kind of scenario was she preparing for?

“No need. Even if something like that really happens, I still have ways to handle it,” Yaeger firmly declined Mylene’s kind intentions.

In her eyes, it was just a trivial matter. All she needed to do was go to Baiding Island, defeat Lucky, and then return, as simple as that. There was no need to make such a fuss about it. Besides, she didn’t want to get overly entangled with the higher-ups.

(Being carefree is much better.)

“Alright then, I’ll listen to you,” Mylene nodded gently.  

“I don’t think they’ll actually go to such extremes,” Pixie commented.  

“It doesn’t matter if they go that far or not; either way, it won’t affect me,” Yaeger replied calmly. She could teleport herself back anyway. Even if the entire island ended up surrounded by fleets, it wouldn’t bother her at all.

Seeing her so relaxed, everyone finally felt at ease. Thinking about it carefully, up until now, nothing had truly troubled Princess. This time, it would definitely be settled easily as well.

“Sister, on the day of the duel, will you go there with us on the patrol ship?” Mylene asked.  

“No need. I have a special method to get there,” Yaeger waved her hand dismissively. As for what method exactly, she didn’t elaborate.

Though Nangong Lin and the others were curious, they refrained from prying since Princess didn’t explain.

“Let’s not talk about this anymore. How about we discuss the game instead?” Yaeger quickly shifted the topic.

“Hehe, Princess, I’ve been working really hard recently!” Nangong Lin said proudly. She really had been putting in effort recently, and her level was close to catching up to Rakshasa.

“Princess, I also…” The girls immediately started chattering excitedly, one after another, competing to speak. Yaeger, however, didn’t find it bothersome at all, and happily listened to their lively accounts of their adventures in the game.

Occasionally, she even gave them helpful pointers.

---

Under the same sky, at a certain bar in the inner district. Stanley, second son of the Lin family—one of Roc City’s four great families—sat drinking gloomily, his face swollen and bruised.

“Damn it, even Dad has never beaten me like this!”

He had merely mentioned [Princess] to his elder brother, and casually revealed some impure desires he’d harbored. In return, his brother had nearly broken his legs. Only then did Stanley realize just how frightening an existence [Princess] truly was.

He had nearly dragged the entire Lin family into a bottomless abyss!

“Taurus!” Undoubtedly, the person responsible for him being beaten by his brother was that arrogant young master from Huadu!

**Beep, beep, beep!**

Right as he cursed that detestable name with a belly full of resentment, his phone suddenly rang. When he glanced at the caller ID, his eyes widened in shock. The person calling was Taurus himself!

Stanley’s hand holding the phone shook uncontrollably. His trembling was caused by extreme fury!

**Beep, beep, beep!**

The ringing continued, becoming increasingly loud. Taking a deep breath to steady himself, Stanley swiped the screen to answer the call. From the other end came Taurus’ cheerful voice: “Young Master Lin, any updates on that Princess?”

“Screw your ancestors for eighteen generations!” He had barely suppressed his anger until now, but upon hearing “Princess,” Stanley’s rage exploded instantly. After cursing, he decisively hung up and immediately blocked Taurus’ number.

Meanwhile, inside the Zhang family’s mansion in Huadu, Taurus stared blankly at his phone. After a brief hesitation, he finally reacted. “He actually cursed me for no reason? Does he have a death wish?”

His expression changed dramatically, and with rising anger, he called back immediately. However, all he heard from the other end was a busy tone. He tried several more times, but the call wouldn’t go through.

“He blocked me?” Staring at the phone screen, Taurus was fuming. Being cursed so severely without even being able to retaliate felt extraordinarily infuriating. The more he thought about it, the angrier he became. Taurus quickly dialed another number.

In a hotel in Huadu.

S.K.Y. had just been about to shower when his phone suddenly rang. Initially, he didn’t want to answer. But when he saw the caller was Taurus, he reluctantly picked up.

“Screw your ancestors for eighteen generations!” Immediately, a furious curse came from the other end, followed swiftly by the beep of a disconnected line. Clearly, the caller had cursed and then immediately hung up.

“…” S.K.Y. was left speechless, anger and resentment welling up simultaneously in his heart. “Taurus!” He ground out the name through clenched teeth, his voice dripping with venomous fury, instantly making the room feel colder.

On the floor, S.K.Y.’s shadow abruptly sprouted a pair of crimson blood-red eyes and a wide, gaping bloody mouth!

---

“Ha, that felt great! A rich man’s stress relief sure is easy, carefree, and enjoyable.” Taurus tossed his phone onto the bed, laughing with childlike innocence. He wasn’t worried about how S.K.Y. might respond. After all, he was just a dog he’d raised himself. Could a mere dog bite back after a few insults?

“Ha… I’m really sleepy. Tomorrow will be busy again.” Feeling a strong wave of drowsiness washing over him, Taurus slowly lay down on his bed, switched off the bedside lamp, and closed his eyes, quickly falling asleep.

Meanwhile, Yaeger had already returned to the City of Chaos, carrying several large and small bags.

“Master!” Little Blue flew over like a bullet. This time, she didn’t aim for Yaeger’s neck. Her target was clear—the bags filled with delicious food!

“You greedy little glutton.” Yaeger shot her a look, mildly annoyed. Then she passed the packed food over. “Make sure Vera 2, 17, and 18 get some too.”

“Of course! Share the blessings, share the burdens!” Little Blue immediately activated her ability, levitating all the food boxes to follow her as she joyfully floated towards the dining area.

Not far away, the three Veras waited eagerly, eyes practically sparkling in anticipation.

“Truly a group of little gluttons.” Yaeger shook her head slightly with a wry smile. Nevertheless, she was very fond of these little creatures. If she weren’t, she wouldn’t pamper them like this.

Leaving the main hall, Yaeger returned to her own room. “I have to head out to the town where Layna is tomorrow morning. Better rest up a bit now.” Lying on the soft bed, Yaeger completely relaxed her body, closing her eyes to rest.

At the same time, in Roc City’s inner district, at the Black Horse Club.

The lavishly decorated club, opulent and dazzling, had already opened for business. Numerous wealthy, bejeweled ladies came and went, creating a lively atmosphere.

“Sister Red!” Suddenly, a respectful voice rang out clearly from outside. Upon hearing this, the previously bustling atmosphere suddenly froze, and everyone immediately turned to look.

+++

# 679 – On That Day, People Once Again Recalled the Terror of Being Dominated by Fate

Outside the Black Horse Club, eight burly men dressed in black suits escorted a woman in a red dress along the red carpet, like stars orbiting around the moon.

This woman in the red dress was tall, with fair skin, straight long black hair, and delicate features partially hidden behind a pair of sunglasses. Her entire presence radiated an aura that warned strangers to keep their distance. One glance was enough to reveal she was no ordinary figure.

“Sister Red!” The male hosts greeting guests at the entrance bowed simultaneously and spoke respectfully.

This woman in red was none other than the very culprit who had once victimized Yaeger. If it hadn’t been for her desire toward Yaeger, the latter would never have been forced by Wenzel, nearly reaching a dead end. One could say that without Sister Red, the current Yae-hime wouldn’t have existed.

Numerous wealthy ladies greeted her warmly. Sister Red simply responded with a polite nod. As the owner of the Black Horse Club, Sister Red remained a deeply mysterious figure. No one knew where she was born, her real name, her age, nor her place of residence. Everything about her was shrouded in mystery.

With her bodyguards leading the way, Sister Red quickly arrived at her own office. Since this club was the main branch of the Black Horse Club chain, she occasionally visited to check on operations.

Seated on her office chair, Sister Red gazed at the plump young man standing before her. He was dressed in a black suit, shaped almost like an egg due to his round physique.

Though not particularly good-looking, he had exceptional business acumen and was one of Sister Red’s most capable assistants.

“No recent troubles, I hope?” Sister Red leaned back in her chair, crossed her slender legs, and spoke to the plump young man. Her voice was slightly husky, carrying a uniquely attractive charm.

“Everything at the club is operating as usual, Sister Red,” the plump young man replied respectfully, bowing his head slightly.

“That’s good then,” Sister Red nodded approvingly. “Did Wenzel manage to catch that boy for me?”

Hearing this question, the plump young man felt slightly puzzled: Wenzel’s funeral rites had already passed, why was Sister Red still asking about him?

Logically speaking, the news of Wenzel’s murder and the destruction of Cathay’s Small Sword Group should have reached everyone by now. But after thinking it over carefully, he realized it was normal. A prominent figure as busy as Sister Red wouldn’t have time to keep track of the fate of local gangsters.

After a brief hesitation, the plump young man spoke, “Sister Red, actually, this is what happened…” He succinctly summarized recent events.

Listening silently, Sister Red maintained a blank expression, though inwardly she was quite astonished. How had so many things occurred in such a short time while she was abroad?

“Since their leader is dead, our cooperation with the Small Sword Group ends here officially. Additionally, find another suitable organization to collaborate with. You must capture that boy, Yaeger, for me within this month,” Sister Red instructed indifferently.

“Understood,” the plump young man responded promptly.

Sister Red uncrossed her legs and placed her hands on the table, leaning forward slightly and resting her smooth chin upon her right palm. “Does the club have any new ‘goods’ recently?” she asked casually.

“We have a few new male escorts with decent appearances,” the plump young man smiled.  

“No notable backgrounds or social connections?” Sister Red questioned further.  

“None whatsoever.”  

“Excellent. Arrange for them to go overseas tomorrow. Use the same ship as usual and ship them out secretly,” Sister Red ordered.  

“Yes, Sister Red,” the assistant nodded vigorously.

He was extremely familiar with this procedure by now. After all, Sister Red routinely dispatched groups of individuals overseas to expand her business abroad every so often.

“You may leave now,” Sister Red said lazily, waving her hand slightly.  

“Yes.” The plump young man turned to leave but suddenly remembered something and looked back at Sister Red again.  

“Anything else?” Sister Red asked.  

After hesitating briefly, the assistant spoke again. “Sister Red, actually… something strange happened in the club yesterday.”  

“Oh? Do tell.” Hearing the phrase ‘something strange,’ Sister Red’s curiosity was immediately piqued.

“Last night, after the kitchen staff had left, one of the male escorts sneaked into the kitchen looking for food. Then he witnessed something utterly horrifying!” the plump young man recounted with exaggerated fright, as though he’d personally witnessed the scene himself. With such acting talent, it was truly a waste for him not to pursue a career in film.

“What exactly did he see?” Sister Red asked eagerly, her interest thoroughly aroused.  

“That escort saw a green cockroach devouring a rat alive!” The plump young man shuddered involuntarily, his face turning slightly pale.  

“What? A green cockroach eating a live rat?” Sister Red was momentarily stunned, utterly baffled by such absurdity. It sounded like complete nonsense!

“Yes. At first, I didn’t believe it either…until I saw that terrifying cockroach myself in the kitchen! It was huge, extremely fast, and glowed green! I summoned many staff to catch it, but it evaded us every time!” Recalling that strangely intelligent cockroach, the plump young man couldn’t help but shiver, fear creeping into his heart.

He wasn’t even sure if the creature could truly be classified as a cockroach anymore. It was eating rats now; who knew if it might start devouring people next?

After hearing this, Sister Red’s expression shifted dramatically. Behind her sunglasses, a sharp gleam flashed in her eyes. “Take me to the kitchen right away!” she said, her voice suddenly charged with excitement.

Although slightly confused by her reaction, the plump young man obediently led the way. They quickly made their way to the kitchen, swiftly dismissing all staff members inside.

“No one enters without my permission,” Sister Red commanded as she closed the door behind them.

Once the kitchen door closed, the plump young man’s confusion only deepened. Nonetheless, he obediently remained standing guard outside.

Inside the kitchen, Sister Red’s lips curled upward slightly. She could sense a faint yet peculiar presence nearby. It was hidden underneath the cabinet.

Slowly removing her sunglasses, Sister Red revealed a charming face, ripe and delicate as a peach. Yet even more striking were her unusual eyes. They were emerald-green compound eyes!

“My dear little pet, you’d better come out obediently.” Sister Red approached the cabinet with graceful steps.

From beneath, a subtle rustling sound could be heard. Suddenly, a cockroach emitting a faint green glow, as large as a human palm, burst out from its hiding spot and rapidly flew toward the door, trying to escape.

Seeing this, Sister Red smiled elegantly. Opening her red lips slightly, she emitted a series of soundwaves inaudible to human ears, instantly covering every corner of the kitchen.

The large cockroach was undeniably swift, yet no matter how fast it moved, it couldn’t outpace sound itself. In the very next moment, the cockroach abruptly froze mid-air, completely immobilized.

“Hehe, indeed, it’s quite the oversized cockroach.” Sister Red walked over, picking up the motionless green insect and scrutinizing it carefully with her compound eyes.

At that instant, a startlingly human-like expression of fear emerged within the insect’s eyes!

“So, you’ve gained sentience,” Sister Red murmured thoughtfully. “I initially assumed this was a natural mutation, yet it seems this was artificially induced. But who could have done this?”

Gazing intently at the cockroach, her expression became grave. “This person has abilities similar to the [Matriarch]… I need to return immediately and report this discovery!”

After retrieving a plastic food storage bag from the countertop and sealing the green cockroach inside, Sister Red quickly exited the kitchen. “Contact our smuggling contact immediately, we’re heading out to sea at once!”

Before the plump young man could speak, Sister Red had already given her command. He swiftly fell in step behind her, pulling out his phone to hastily make the call.

---

Meanwhile, within the game, deep in the boundless ocean far beyond the Jade Empire, an island floated high in the sky.

Its name was Celestial Island.

At that moment, from inside a majestic palace swirling with ethereal mist, charming laughter echoed like silver bells. “Hehehe, as expected of myself! So effortlessly, I’ve created an external avatar capable of escaping the Heavenly Law’s restrictions!”

An exquisitely sculpted young girl, as delicate as jade and porcelain, gazed with satisfaction at another girl, equally beautiful, like her mirror image.

“Main body, will everything truly be alright?” the clone asked with a hint of concern.

Presently, Celestial Island was entirely confined by the Heavenly Law’s restrictions, resembling a vast, heavenly prison. When those restrictions might be lifted, no one knew.

Being outsiders, the island’s Celestials had little grounds for complaint. Surviving that great calamity had already been an enormous blessing for them. Demanding more might provoke merciless punishment.

“Everything will be fine. Relax. After all, I’ve already latched onto Heavenly Law’s thigh. There’s no reason for Heavenly Law to harm me,” the barefooted girl in a flowing, silk-like garment confidently assured her avatar, gently patting her shoulder.

“I sincerely hope so,” her clone nodded cautiously.  

“From now on, your name shall be Zerene. Alright, Zerene, quickly sneak away from here and capture that individual connected to Heavenly Law for me. With a tenth of my true strength, you’ll face no real opponents in this world. You have nothing to fear!”

The young girl stood proudly, hands resting on her waist, her face beaming with confidence.

“Understood,” Zerene replied calmly, smiling softly. “Main body, wish me a speedy return.”

“Good luck, return quickly.” With a wave of her hand, a glowing portal instantly materialized beside her. “I’ve already opened the passage for you.”

“I’m off, main body.” Zerene nodded and swiftly leaped into the portal. In an instant, the portal vanished, and the young girl felt her clone’s presence disappear entirely.

“Hahaha, everything went so smoothly! It appears Heavenly Law is taking a nap,” the young girl laughed delightedly. Her avatar had successfully evaded Heavenly Law’s constraints, escaping Celestial Island entirely.

Meanwhile, outside Celestial Island, a flash of white light suddenly appeared in mid-air, revealing a petite, stunningly beautiful young girl cloaked in celestial energy.

“Hmph. Heavenly Law, so this is all you’re capable of?” Standing in an unfamiliar environment and savoring the taste of freedom, Zerene sneered contemptuously, the corner of her mouth curling slightly upward.

However, before her words had fully faded away, the space around her suddenly trembled. Immediately afterward, the air seemed to solidify completely.

Zerene instantly became alert. Looking upward, she saw that the starry night sky had suddenly been obscured by ominous black clouds.

‘No, these aren’t ordinary clouds…they are thunderclouds!’

Silver lightning twisted violently within the dark storm, emanating an ancient and overwhelming aura.

“A… A heavenly tribulation!? How can this be possible? I belong to the Celestial Race! Why am I facing a heavenly tribulation!?” Zerene cried out in fear.

**Boom!**

Responding to her panicked cry, a massive bolt of lightning as thick as a water barrel crashed down.

“Aaaahhhhh!” With no possibility of escape or defense, the lightning directly struck Zerene, immediately eliciting a heart-wrenching scream.

In that instant, she was forcefully reminded of the terror of being dominated by the Heavenly Law. As the first lightning bolt dissipated, another golden-colored bolt swiftly descended.

“Heavenly Law! Big sister! I was wrong! I promise to never belittle you again, please forgive me!”

Yet no matter how desperately Zerene pleaded for mercy, lightning bolts, each stronger than the last, continued relentlessly striking her small figure.

Finally, a black wall of electricity thundered down from the heavens, scorching Zerene until she was charred outside and thoroughly battered within, barely clinging onto life. Immediately afterward, the tribulation clouds dispersed completely.

A small, frail figure fell silently into the endless ocean below, drifting southward with the ocean currents.

+++

# 680 – May the Holy Light Bless You ♂

Early morning. Yaeger got out of bed and made a point of visiting the guest room to enjoy the pitiful wails of Vera 1 and 3, a little spiritual cultivation, as she called it.
