It wasn’t just his gear that changed. The system also reallocated his base stat points.

“Hehehe, this suits me way better!” Clenching his fists, Ronald felt an incredible surge of power course through his body.

Just then, the system’s voice chimed in:

Ding!

Congratulations, you are the first player globally to switch to the Pugilist class.

Rewards: 2x Random Rare Equipment Crates and 10,000 Gold Coins.

Hearing the announcement, Ronald broke into a huge grin, looking as delighted as a child.

“Jackpot!”

In his mind, five million was nothing more than pocket change. The true prize was the two equipment crates. Because inside those crates, there was a real chance of obtaining rare Pugilist-specific gear. Something no amount of money could currently buy!

Meanwhile, on the Yanjing server…

Jolorie had also successfully Job Changed. The difference was, she received no reward. Two other young men had also made the switch with her.

“Heh, who would’ve thought there’d be a Pugilist class?” Jolorie said with a charming smile, her tone laced with a strange, seductive undertone. But those who knew her real age couldn’t feel the allure at all.

On the contrary, they felt…

Just as the other four were about to fake gagging, Jolorie had suddenly launched a flurry of punches at them. The next moment, the other players watched as four screaming figures flew like rockets into distant walls. Then, they slid slowly to the ground.

She plastered them against the wall like paintings! Clearly, Jolorie was no stranger to fisticuffs, she was a true martial arts master!

The new Job quickly became the hottest topic on the forums. At the same time, the outrageous five-million gold job-change fee sparked a wave of furious complaints. Even so, more and more players began switching classes.

At that point, people finally realized just how many rich players were in Saint Demon World.

“No way… there are actually that many suckers?” Yaeger muttered as she opened the forums and saw a slew of posts about players changing to the new class. “Having money really is nice,” she sighed with a hint of envy, then closed the interface and continued browsing the rest of the update notes.

The second update was the Live Broadcast feature. But this wasn’t external streaming, it was in-game live streaming! This had never existed before.

Even more surprising, the feature allowed for simultaneous broadcasting both in-game and on external platforms.

“The era of streamers is about to arrive,” Yaeger said with a wry smile. This feature didn’t really surprise her. In her past life, it had been introduced in version 2.0.

Her gaze dropped to the third update: Bloodline Synthesis System.

“Whew!” She sucked in a sharp breath the moment she saw the bold title. Because the Bloodline Synthesis System was a major feature introduced in version 3.0!

“This is way too early…”

Bloodline Synthesis had been the most important feature of 3.0. It spanned the entire game and changed its core dynamics.

“Could it be because Pixie and the others all drew top-tier bloodlines, causing the system to make some internal adjustments?” After thinking for a while, she suddenly recalled recent discussion threads speculating that the chances of getting rare bloodlines from draws had been stealthily lowered.

At this stage in the game, many players had come to realize just how influential bloodlines and character identities were. As a result, many wealthy latecomers had started dumping cash into gacha draws before even entering the game.

However, very few seemed to have drawn high-rank bloodlines. That imbalance had sparked a heated debate online.

Yaeger had noticed this trend while lurking on the forums herself. “But seriously, this synthesis system is a total scam…”

In fact, she had already used the system once before. Back when she fell to the bottom of that cliff, the system had forcibly merged her bloodline. And the cost? Absolutely brutal.

As expected, the synthesis system was quickly flamed to oblivion on the forums by the “keyboard warriors,” who cursed it out across three thousand digital miles.

“For Yunuen and Little Fairy, this system is actually pretty helpful.” But for her and Pixie, it was nothing more than a decorative feature.

She continued scrolling and reached the final update: Faction Shop.

“This one was introduced in version 2.0.” At this point, she was no longer surprised by early updates. Her heart barely stirred. What’s more, these updates had little to no impact on her directly.

The initial shock passed quickly.

“Light, Dark, and Chaos… On paper, all three factions offer perks. But in reality, only Chaos and Light are truly viable options.” As she looked at the familiar trio of factions, Yaeger murmured to herself.

If this were just a regular game, it wouldn’t matter which side you chose. But unfortunately, this wasn’t just a game. Once the real world and the game world fully merged, your faction choice might affect you for the rest of your life.

Naturally, Yaeger had no plans to join any faction.

“I’ve got an artifact and the highest-tier Celestial bloodline. There’s no need to tie myself down to a faction. The benefits they offer aren’t even worth as much as a few lucky draws.”

Likewise, she didn’t want the girls in her guild joining any factions either.

“Freedom is better.”

Because once you picked a side, your life would no longer be your own. After all… there’s no such thing as a free lunch.

+++

# 691 – The Impact of the Version Update

Overseas, on the Dorado server of the United States.

After reviewing the update notes, Mira’s shock was written all over her face. “This update is insane!”

She was especially struck by the Bloodline Synthesis System. Just recently, she had been fretting over not having a top-tier bloodline. Now, with this version update, the game had handed her a chance to perfect her lineage.

“It’s pricey, sure, but at least I get to make up for it!” The corners of her lips curled into a smile, the astonishment on her face gradually replaced by joy.

Like a small handful of players back then, Mira had participated in the bloodline lottery. Unfortunately, after spending eight million, she only managed to get a second-tier bloodline.

Barely a few days into the game, she had already experienced firsthand the benefits of a powerful bloodline. But by then, it was too late to reroll. But now, with a chance to fix it, a chance to ascend to the highest tier, how could she not be delighted?

“Hehe, once I patch up my bloodline, I’ll be a perfect being!” At this moment, Mira was so excited she could barely contain herself.

And she wasn’t alone, many players across the game shared her elation.

“Excellent. I must obtain the highest-tier bloodline!” Taurus slapped the table in excitement.

Before officially entering the game, he had spent five million, but still didn’t land a particularly strong bloodline. Now that there was an opportunity to upgrade it, he definitely wouldn’t let it slip by. To Taurus, any problem that could be solved with money wasn’t a real problem.

Compared to the bloodline system, S.K.Y. was more intrigued by the Faction Shop. ‘Joining a faction not only unlocks access to the corresponding shop, but also grants bonus experience and status effects. The higher the favorability with the faction, the greater the benefits. This is actually pretty solid.’

He reflexively adjusted his imaginary gold-rimmed glasses, a rare ripple of emotion surfacing in his mind. At this point, S.K.Y. had already made up his mind about which faction to join.

“This new Pugilist class costs five million to switch to? Are they out of their minds?” Vanessa had just logged in and raised her brows at the update log, her voice tinged with surprise.

Everyone turned to look at her with oddly amused expressions. Taurus and S.K.Y. had the same thought in sync: This Job was basically made for you!

On the other side, the [Princess Alliance] guild was also discussing the patch in their guild chat.

Nangong Lin: This update doesn’t seem all that special.

Sachiel: Just another new Job.

Pixie: The Bloodline Synthesis System should be pretty helpful for Snowy, Yuenen, and Little Fairy.

Yuenen: Looks like it can enhance our bloodlines.

Little Fairy: Yeah, it’s definitely good for us.

Snowy: Agreed.

Rakshasa: The new Job isn’t for me.

Nangong Lin: The in-game livestream function is neat!

Pixie: Yeah, now we can watch without logging out. Super convenient.

Sachiel: We can sneak a peek at Princess when we’re free…

Yuenen: But lately she’s been doing her own thing, huh?

Little Fairy: That’s right.

---

At that moment, Yae-hime[1](https://re-library.com/translations/reborn-as-a-transcendent/volume-3/chapter-691-the-impact-of-the-version-update/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-110478) entered the guild chat.

Everyone: Princess!

As expected, the moment she appeared, she immediately became the center of attention for all the girls.

Yae-hime: Good evening, everyone.

Nangong Lin: Good evening, Princess!

Rakshasa: _Muah!_

Sachiel: Rakshasa, why are you blowing kisses?

Pixie: Mhm, I smell something suspicious.

Little Fairy: Good evening, Princess.

Snowy: Good evening, Princess. I’m Snowy, the new member. We’ve met once before.

Yunuen: Good evening, Princess!

Yae-hime: Mm, looks like everyone’s here. Snowy, right? Welcome to our family.

Alright, let’s keep the chit-chat brief.

Since time is limited, I’ll get straight to the point.

As you’ve already discussed, the only useful part of this update for us is the Bloodline Synthesis System.

Livestreaming… maybe just barely counts.

As for the new Job, does anyone want to become a Pugilist?

Snowy: I do.

Yae-hime: So it’s useful after all, haha.

Snowy: Yes, I’m more proficient in hand-to-hand combat. The Pugilist class suits me well.

Pixie: I’ve trained in swordsmanship, no need to switch.

Yae-hime: Mm, let’s put the new Job aside for now. Let’s talk about factions.

As you all know, the game is divided into three major factions: Light, Chaos, and Dark.

Joining a faction grants access to the Faction Shop, as well as bonus experience and status effects.

For most players, joining a faction comes with plenty of benefits.

But for us, it’s different… we already have top-tier bloodlines, high-grade gear, and distinguished identities.

There’s absolutely no need to join a faction and be bound by its restrictions.

Besides, those so-called perks aren’t free. Once you join, you’ll incur obligations in return.

And afterward, you’ll be dealing with all sorts of trouble.

---

As for the matter of the two worlds merging, Yae-hime couldn’t tell them just yet. She would wait until the time was right before making it public.

Nangong Lin: That’s true. Those perks seem free, but really, they just come at a different cost.

Pixie: Nothing is more expensive than “free.”

Yunuen: Yeah.

Rakshasa: I just want to follow Princess.

Little Fairy: Me too.

Snowy: Same here.

Sachiel: Count me in as well!

Yae-himei: Good. I won’t let you down!

---

Seeing this, everyone was filled with joy.

After chatting with them a little longer, Yae-hime left the guild chat. She then exited the living room and headed to the village chief’s house to find Angelica.

At the same time, in Yanjing, at the top floor of the Mo Family Mansion.

**Splash—**

In a sleek and minimalist bathroom, warm water cascaded from the showerhead, streaming down a figure as pale and flawless as jade, both beautiful and alluring. A slender hand swept through damp black hair, revealing a face so delicate it seemed almost too perfect.

Droplets ran from her cheeks to her chin, trickling down twin peaks, over smooth plains, and into hidden valleys. The water continued to flow, endless and rhythmic, like a downpour powerful enough to wash away the world.

After bathing, the stunning woman, now exuding a gentle peachy fragrance, reclined against a luxurious sofa, sipping a glass of chilled water while reviewing an urgent report sent by one of her subordinates.

This woman was none other than Mylene’s mentor, the top-ranked figure in Cathay, Lisa of the Mo (Black)[2](https://re-library.com/translations/reborn-as-a-transcendent/volume-3/chapter-691-the-impact-of-the-version-update/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-110478) family.

“The update rolled out rather quickly,” she murmured as she stared at her phone screen. Her tone carried a chill that exuded an unusual sense of pressure.

“A new Job: Pugilist. Interesting. Might be fun to give it a try.”

After placing her glass on the table, Lisa sat upright and crossed her long, elegant legs. Had anyone been present to witness this casual gesture, their blood would have surged uncontrollably, their rational mind overwhelmed by primal instinct.

In the end, they’d have become little more than a beast, lunging forward without a second thought.

“Bring me a terminal.” With a snap of her fingers, a neatly dressed woman in her mid-twenties appeared in the living room.

“Yes, Madam.” Before long, the woman returned with a brand-new gaming terminal.

“Don’t let anyone disturb me tonight.” With those words, Lisa left the living room, terminal in hand, heading back to her private quarters.

That night, Cathay’s number one finally entered the game.

+++

# 692 – A Half-Step Grandmaster, How Terrifying!?

* **Aoma Village.**

Angelica had just finished her bath and stepped out, a gentle warmth and fragrant steam still clinging to her body.

“Mggh!” She stretched lazily upon entering the living room. “So tired…”  

At that moment, Angelica was like a sleepy cat basking after a long day.

“Good evening.” Suddenly, a melodic voice came from nearby, giving her quite a fright.  

“Waaah!”  

“Hehe, look how startled you are,” Yae-hime said with a soft laugh. “Just like a little kitten caught off guard.”

Angelica blinked, then pouted in mock protest. “Princess, you scared me to death!”

“Sorry, sorry,” Yae-hime smiled, touching her rosy lips with a graceful finger as she approached. “That was my bad.”

Then, she reached out and gently ruffled Angelica’s still-damp hair. The gentle gesture left Angelica’s cheeks slightly flushed, but her heart was undeniably warm.

“You’ve been working hard these past two days,” Yae-hime said warmly.  

“It’s nothing!” Angelica responded with a content smile.  

“Even though I’d like you to rest right away, there’s one more thing I need to trouble you with,” Yae-hime added with a hint of apology.

She was hoping to gather the final ingredient for the Berserk Drug tonight, so Layna could start synthesizing it right away.

“It’s no problem! I’ve still got plenty of energy!” Angelica balled her fists and her eyes lit up with resolve.

“I’m looking for something called a Demon Lotus,” Yae-hime said.

“Demon Lotus… I’m not sure if Aoma Village has it, but we do have a trading guild. I can check with them,” Angelica replied, clearly unfamiliar with the item.

“Is it convenient to go now?”

“Should be fine. After the chaos caused by those outsiders, no one in the village is sleeping anyway.” Angelica gave a cheerful laugh.

“Alright then, I’ll leave it to you.” Yae-hime retracted her hand and smiled.

“Mhm! I’ll be back soon!” With a skip in her step, Angelica left the house and headed straight for the merchant guild.

“What should I do in the meantime…?” Seated on a bench, Yae-hime opened her game interface, a bit at a loss. With nothing urgent to do, she decided to check the forums and see what players were saying about the new update.

The top post caught her eye.

«Trash Game Company! What an Ugly Cash Grab!»

Opening it, she was met with a wall of profanities.

“Yep, just as expected…people venting their frustration,” Yae-hime muttered.

From the surface, this update really did seem like nothing but a money pit. Switching to the new Job cost 5 million gold, and synthesizing a single bloodline started at a million. It felt like a direct slap to the face for regular players.

(“Our goal is to create joy, with a giant middle finger to the poor!”)

The silent mockery of the game developers rang loud in everyone’s minds. And yet, to this day, no one even knew who actually owned the company.

Closing the thread, Yae-hime kept browsing trending posts.

«Hahaha, I Just Made 5 Million!»

Clicking in, she saw a new player proudly showing off their Job panel. Sure enough, it was the new Pugilist class, worth five million gold to Job Change.

Scrolling down, the comments rolled in:

> [Barbie Burpee]: Free 5 mil? I’m jealous!

>

> [Vinnia’s JO]: Look at you, grinning like a kid.

>

> [Scumbag]: Ughhh I’m so jealous!  

> (sneakily posts Level 20 stats.JPG)

>

> [Bermuda CarpKing]: Tsk, must feel good to earn 5 mil just like that.

>

> [Bluefist Envoy]: Oh ho, this guy’s kinda cute. Interested in joining our [Blue Fist] guild?  

> All male Pugilists only! ���

>

> [White Cloud]: Idiot, most of us are already level 10–20. You’re still in the Novice Village, completely left behind!

>

> [Huehuehue]: Someone sounds salty, hehe~

>

> [Carefree Junior]: Jokes aside, this class is crazy strong on paper.  

> One combo = massive damage.  

> Too bad the defense is kinda meh.

>

> [George Tank]: But Pugilist has high mobility, so the low defense makes sense.

>

> [Platinum Star]: Too bad the Job Change fee is 5 mil. That price tag is just brutal for us common folk.

>

> [Fishmonger Stronk]: Are they insane for wanting that much?  

> But wow, there really are a lot of rich players in this game.  

> I checked the statistics thread just now, dozens have already switched classes.

>

> [Elina]: If you count global servers, even more people have Jobs changed.  

> Rich people… they’re terrifying!

---

The further down the thread she scrolled, the more normal the comments became. Yae-hime found herself losing interest. With a flick of her finger, she closed the page.

At that moment, a sound came from the direction of the door. A moment later, a beautiful girl walked in. Who else could it be but Angelica?

“Princess, I found it!” she called out excitedly, holding up a small pouch in her right hand.

Hearing that, Yae-hime immediately rose from the bench and walked quickly toward her.

“There were only ten of them,” Angelica added.  

“Ten is more than enough.” Yae-hime gave her a pat on the shoulder. “You’ve done well.”  

“It was nothing. Really, just a small errand,” Angelica replied, looking a little bashful. She then handed over the pouch in her hand.

Yae-hime took it and asked, “How much did it cost altogether?”  

“Nothing at all. The guild master gave them to me,” Angelica replied, blinking.  

“Demon Lotus isn’t exactly cheap. The guild master’s that generous?” Yae-hime asked, puzzled.  

“I think it was probably because of you, Princess,” Angelica said.  

“What makes you say that?”

“He asked me what I needed the Demon Lotus for, so I told him it was for the Lord Angel.” Angelica paused, then continued, “After that, he immediately packed up the ten he had in stock and told me to bring them to you.”

“I really shouldn’t…,” Yae-hime said, though not even pretending to refuse.  

“Princess, you saved our whole village. This little gift…please don’t be modest,” Angelica said earnestly.  

“All right then, I’ll gladly accept.”

With that, Yae-hime stored the Demon Lotus in her spatial ring.

Something she had been trying to get her hands on for so long had landed in her lap so easily, it both surprised and delighted her. But on second thought, considering Demon Lotus was an aquatic plant, finding it at a port town like this wasn’t entirely unexpected.

After chatting a while longer, Yae-hime urged Angelica to get some rest. She herself then left Aoma Village alone and flew off in the direction of Aureole Town.

---

Elsewhere—America, San Francisco, headquarters of the Small Sword Group.

A thunderous sound suddenly erupted from within the training chamber, startling the two guards standing watch outside. They nearly jumped where they stood.

Right after, the sound of wild laughter rang out.

“Hahahahahahahahaha!”

There was no mistaking that familiar voice, it was Lucky.

“My power has finally stabilized. It’s time to head to Cathay!” He slowly rose to his feet, eyes gleaming with razor-sharp light. His entire body radiated a deadly aura.

There was also an overwhelming presence about him, one that could force others to their knees. This was the terrifying pressure of a Half-Step Grandmaster.

+++

# 693 – Widespread Invitations, The Duel Draws Near

* **Aureole Town, Layna’s Home.**

“I’ve never made a Berserk Drug before,” Layna said.

When Yae-hime suddenly returned, Layna hadn’t even finished expressing her joy before Yae-hime brought up a new request.

“That’s fine. Just give it a try, this concoction should be easy for someone like you.” Yae-hime smiled as she laid out a pile of ingredients on the worktable.

For a Rank 9 Apothecary[1](https://re-library.com/translations/reborn-as-a-transcendent/volume-3/chapter-693-widespread-invitations-the-duel-draws-near/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-110488), brewing a Berserk Drug was practically effortless.

“Alright, leave it to me,” Layna nodded. “By the way, are you hungry? Want me to whip up some noodles for a midnight snack?”

Yaeger hesitated briefly, then nodded lightly. Since there was nothing pressing to do at the moment, taking a break sounded just fine.

“I’ll get started right away!” Layna said cheerfully.

Fifteen minutes later, the two sat together enjoying a steaming bowl of shrimp noodles. The taste was quite good.

“What did the church in Aoma Village say?” Layna asked after sipping the savory broth.

“There’s no way to solve the bottle issue for now. But tomorrow, a few people from the church will show up to display a so-called _miracle._” Yae-hime spoke with a wry smile.

“Hehe, a miracle, huh?” Layna chuckled softly. Of course she knew the so-called holy water had been created by the impossibly beautiful Princess sitting across from her.

‘Still, calling it a miracle isn’t wrong either. After all, a plague is one of the deadliest natural disasters known.’

Looking at Yae-hime, Layna’s heartbeat began to quicken. Before this girl who could dispel a plague like it was nothing, she felt both admiration… and a deepening affection.

“As long as the problem gets solved, the method doesn’t matter much,” Yae-hime said lazily, having finished her shrimp.

“Mhm. I think so too.” Layna nodded.

After that, neither of them spoke again. They quietly polished off their bowls. Once they were done, Layna cleaned up and began preparing the Berserk Drug.

“I’ll need to research the formula first. I’ll probably finish brewing it by morning.”  

“No need to rush. We won’t need it until then anyway,” Yae-hime replied.  

“It’s fine. I’ve been staying up late recently anyway.” Layna smiled faintly.

That smile tugged at Yae-hime’s heart just a little. She reached out and injected Layna with a dose of life energy, instantly restoring her physical state.

“Mmh! Warm all over… it feels sooo good~” Layna blushed faintly, her body quivering as her legs went weak.

Seeing her in that state, Yae-hime’s eyes twitched.

‘Please don’t say things that are so easy to misinterpret! And that expression, what even is that supposed to be?! What do you think I did to you?!’

After a short while, Layna finally recovered and cheerfully went to begin her work. Yae-hime, meanwhile, went to lie down in the guest room. She remained there until her in-game prison timer ran out.

“Time to log out,” she murmured, tapping the logout button and vanishing in a flash of white light.

* **In the Real World. Cathay, Jinxi Province, Mt. Dragonbane.**

Dominus stared at the latest intelligence gathered by his subordinates. A smirk of disdain curled across his lips.

“An eighteen-year-old Grandmaster. Talented, sure, but still far too green.”

Even that decrepit old Ronald, half a foot in the grave already, had easily beaten her. One could imagine how shallow this so-called young Grandmaster’s strength really was.

“Now… Lucky’s strength has already stabilized at the Intermediate[2](https://re-library.com/translations/reborn-as-a-transcendent/volume-3/chapter-693-widespread-invitations-the-duel-draws-near/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-110488) Grandmaster level. He truly deserves the title of a once-in-a-generation master.”

Leaning back in a chair carved from premium golden cedar wood, Dominus’ expression grew a touch more serious.

Lucky was now on equal footing with him in strength. And with his younger age and greater vitality, Lucky could be a dangerous opponent in a real fight.

“Thankfully, it seems more likely we’ll end up as allies.” He picked up a finely crafted invitation card and chuckled. “Hah. I suppose I’ll do you a favor and attend the match on Baiding Island tomorrow.”

Looking at the embossed invitation in his hand, Dominus’ lips curled into a meaningful smile.

In his mind, tomorrow night’s Grandmaster duel had no suspense whatsoever. A crushing victory for Lucky was all but guaranteed.

* **Korea, a certain dojo.**

A middle-aged man dressed in a white training robe with a black belt tied at his waist also received an invitation.

Just like the one Dominus received, it had been sent by Lucky.

“Very well. I’ll definitely be there tomorrow.” His tone was flat, neither warm nor cold. But then, a dangerous gleam suddenly flashed in his eyes. “Let me witness how that b̲a̲s̲t̲a̲r̲d̲ who killed my disciple gets crushed and dies on the spot!”

As he finished, a thunderous roar erupted from his mouth.

---

At the same time, grandmasters and S-rank Transcendents from nations like India, Japan, Britain, Europe, France, and the United States all received invitations from Lucky.

However, as Little Blue had already predicted, not many would actually show up on Baiding Island. Most simply sent disciples or subordinates in their stead, treating it as a gesture of goodwill toward Lucky.

In the underground world, activity spiked. Countless fiery gazes now turned toward Baiding Island. To most of them, this so-called duel between grandmasters was nothing more than a stage for Lucky to flaunt his dominance.

As for Princess? Merely a pitiful offering.

---

At that moment, atop the City of Chaos.

Yae-hime arrived at the great hall and was greeted by the sight of her four little assistants diligently at work, a sight that filled her with satisfaction.

“Master, Master!” Little Blue dropped her work and dove into her arms, clinging to her neck affectionately.  

“Anything unusual?” Yae-hime asked, gently pinching her chubby, rosy cheeks.  

“All quiet as usual,” Little Blue replied.  

“And Baiding Island?”  

“The plaza and the dock are nearly finished,” she said, releasing her grip and tapping the air.

Instantly, a livestream appeared before them, construction was still ongoing with blazing intensity. From the looks of it, they had clearly entered the final phase. By early tomorrow morning, the work would likely be complete.

“That’s impressive. Which country’s crew is this?” Yae-hime asked, curious.

“Cathay.”

At that answer, Yae-hime blinked, her mouth twitching slightly. “Figures. Infrastructure maniacs, the lot of them. Even on contested territory… Wait, if Cathay’s engineering teams are already on Baiding Island, that must mean negotiations are nearly done. That’s great!”

When she thought about her country finally being able to reclaim land and begin development again, she felt genuinely happy from the bottom of her heart.

“Master, everyone out there thinks you’re doomed now,” Little Blue said with a mischievous grin.

“Heh, that’s fine. By the way, are the odds still rising?” Yae-hime asked with a smile.

“Nope. After it reached seven to one, it fluctuated a little, then returned to normal,” Little Blue replied, shaking her head.

“Seven to one, not bad,” Yae-hime remarked. Then she let out a soft sigh. “Sigh, it’s a shame I don’t have more money to bet.”

Hearing that, Little Blue said, “Master, don’t you have a few very wealthy friends?”

“You’re right. I nearly forgot about them,” Yae-hime’s eyes lit up as she suddenly remembered the three wealthy girls in the guild. “Let’s have them place a few bets too. Free money, might as well grab as much as we can.”

Little Blue nodded. “Besides, everyone already knows how close they are to you. Them betting on you wouldn’t raise any eyebrows.”

“Mm. I’ll message them right now.”

Yae-hime quickly pulled out her phone and sent a message to Pixie[3](https://re-library.com/translations/reborn-as-a-transcendent/volume-3/chapter-693-widespread-invitations-the-duel-draws-near/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-110488) and the others. After waiting five minutes, a reply came in from their side.

Looking at the new message, Yae-hime couldn’t help but chuckle in silence.

+++

# 694 – Proof of Loyalty

Nangong Lin had bet one hundred million.  

Mylene put down fifty million.  

Pixie wagered fifty million.  

Sachiel staked fifty million.  

Snowy contributed ten million.  

Rakshasa offered five million.  

Xina added 1.6 million.  

Yunuen gave fifty thousand.  

Little Fairy chipped in ten thousand.

The total came to a staggering 266.66 million!

They had all placed heavy bets on Yae-hime! Even Yunuen and Little Fairy, whose financial situations weren’t exactly great, had scraped together their last reserves to chip in!

“Master, your odds just dropped by 0.5!” Little Blue said in mild surprise.

“That’s expected.” With over two hundred million flooding in, it’d be strange if the other side didn’t react at all.

“Wow, your friends are real rich ladies,” Little Blue traced the source and immediately understood what had happened. That 266.66 million had all been funneled under Nangong Lin’s name.

“Master! The odds bounced back to seven-to-one!” Little Blue exclaimed excitedly as she watched the update.  

“Maybe they’ve already investigated the relationship between Nangong Lin and me,” Yae-hime replied coolly.  

“Heh, do they really think that rich lady is brainless?” Little Blue chuckled.

“Hardly. They’re probably assuming Nangong Lin just wanted to show me some support this way. After all, for the Nangong family, tossing two or three hundred million is no big deal.” Yae-hime explained calmly.

“The power of a rich woman’s wealth, how terrifying!” Little Blue feigned a shocked expression. In truth, if she wanted money, she could generate astronomical figures with ease.

But Yae-hime had forbidden her from using those methods to make money.

“How are those two little ones doing?” After replying to Nangong Lin and the others, Yae-hime suddenly asked.

“Vera 1 and 3? I gave them two steamed buns two hours ago,” Little Blue replied, tapping a virtual screen. With a swish, the space before them returned to normal.

“Just buns?” Yae-hime asked.  

“Yep. Their attitude wasn’t exactly nice,” Little Blue said, shrugging.  

“Let’s go take a look.” With that, Yae-hime took a step forward, her long legs moving gracefully.

Little Blue waved toward Vera 2, 17, and 18 in the distance. The four little ones quickly fell in behind Yae-hime.

“Ugh, I’m so hungry. I’m going to die…” In the guest room, Vera 1 lay on the floor, clutching her stomach in pain. She had eaten a bun earlier, but it had only made her hungrier and more miserable.

On the other side, Vera 3 leaned weakly against the wall, face pale, eyes dull and unfocused, she looked half dead. She knew clearly: if she hadn’t eaten that bun, she could’ve held out much longer. But once she had tasted food, the hunger within her had completely lost control.

Now her body and mind were both suffering immensely!

**Tap, tap, tap!**

Just then, footsteps echoed from outside the room. The two of them tensed up immediately, their bodies trembling uncontrollably.

After going hungry all day, they had personally experienced just how terrifying that demon was. No, not just that one, there was also that little demon, who was equally horrifying!

With just two buns, they had been pushed into such a miserable state. Thinking about the crueler torments that might be coming next, Vera 1 and 3’s little faces turned even paler.

“Sniff… smells good… something smells amazing!” Vera 1 suddenly said excitedly, sniffing the air.

Hearing that, Vera 3 sniffed as well, and her stomach let out a thunderous growl. She could tell instantly, it was the scent of roast chicken!

At that moment, the hunger within them was fully awakened.

The door opened, and that rich aroma surged in, intoxicating and irresistible. Vera 1 and 3, like soulless zombies, automatically began crawling toward the doorway.

“Hehehe, want some?” A pleasant voice rang out, snapping their attention back to the present.

Looking up, they saw that demon standing in the doorway, holding a tray in both hands. On it were two steaming, fragrant roasted chickens.

**Gulp!**

Even though they were terrified, they couldn’t help but swallow hard, eyes filled with longing. A deep, desperate hunger for those two roast chickens.

“Do you want to eat? Do you want to taste this delicious honey-roasted chicken?” The demon’s voice rang out once more. There was a strange, seductive quality to her tone. As if simply obeying her would grant them anything they desired, including those two roasted chickens.

“I—I’m not eating your food!” Vera 1 barely clung to her last shred of reason and shouted with all her might, using every ounce of strength she had. But her voice was feeble and weak, nothing like her usual self.

“I…” Vera 3 wavered violently inside, unsure of how to respond.

“Don’t want to eat?” The demon, Yae-hime, retracted her smile. “Then go ahead and stay hungry. Keep starving until you fall into despair.” As soon as she finished speaking, she turned and made it seem as if she was about to leave.

Seeing this, Vera 1 and 3 looked like helpless souls on the verge of being swallowed by darkness. They stared at the last sliver of light and cried out in unison, “Don’t go!”

Yae-hime immediately stopped in her tracks and turned around to look at them, a radiant smile blooming on her face.

Little Blue and Vera 2, 17, and 18 all poked their heads out to peer at Vera 1 and 3. Sinister smiles curled across their faces.

Seeing those smiles, the sisters felt their scalps tingle and their hearts sink. It was as though they’d accidentally fallen into the depths of hell, face-to-face with a horde of terrifying demons!

“It’s not impossible to get food,” Yae-hime said, retracting her smile. “Pledge your loyalty to me. I mean real loyalty.”

“Real loyalty?” Vera 1 asked nervously. The moment she had called out to stop Yae-hime, she knew there was no going back.

“What kind of loyalty?” Vera 3 asked. She seemed to have already made up her mind.

“Before that, let me tell you the price of betrayal,” Yae-hime said calmly. “The first time, since it was your first offense, I let you go with just one day of no food. The second time, it’ll be seven days. The third time, forty-nine days. And as for a fourth time… sorry, there isn’t one.”

Hearing this, Vera 1 and 3’s eyes widened. Their pupils contracted, and their hearts lurched violently. They might barely survive a second betrayal. But the third time… they would absolutely die.

‘No! I don’t want to starve to death! I absolutely don’t!’ Vera 1 hugged her arms tightly, her body trembling uncontrollably. Just one day of hunger had already pushed her to the brink of despair.

“I—I will never betray you!” Vera 3, usually the calm and composed one, hurried to assure her.

“Very good. Vera 3, come here and swear your oath.” Yae-hime extended her smooth, fair, flawless bare foot with great satisfaction.

Vera 3 blinked her big eyes, her expression filled with confusion as she looked at that overly beautiful jade-like foot, ‘What does this mean?’

Vera 1 was equally baffled.

“Master wants you to lick her foot as proof of your loyalty,” Little Blue floated over, grinning cheekily.

“Lick her foot?!” Vera 1 looked as if she had just suffered the ultimate humiliation. She nearly jumped up in outrage. Unfortunately, she didn’t have the strength left to make such a dramatic move.

On the other side, two tears slipped from the corner of Vera 3’s eyes. Then, with a pained expression, she said, “I’ll do it!”

+++

# 695 – Mmm… Pretty Girl, Smells So Good!

“Number Three!” Vera 1 could hardly believe what she had just heard. That calm, clever Vera 3 had actually chosen to lick the enemy’s foot, for roast chicken! It was unbelievable. Shocking. Infuriating.

And especially when she saw Vera 3 crawling over like a dog, the shame and anger in Vera 1’s heart reached a boiling point. In her mind, she could already see herself crawling the same way… And licking that outrageously beautiful, jade-like foot!

By now, Vera 3 had already crawled to Yae-hime’s feet. Her whole body trembled slightly, her face filled with visible struggle. She had thought she was mentally prepared, that she could just go for it. But when the moment came, she realized how impossibly hard it was.

Overcoming that mental barrier felt like climbing to the heavens.

“Regretting it?” Yae-hime lifted her right leg and gently placed her bare foot on Vera 3’s face. “Is this all your so-called resolve amounts to?”

The touch of her smooth bare foot against Vera 3’s skin was cool, almost pleasant. It should’ve been a tolerable sensation, but inside, Vera 3 felt a wildfire of rage ready to explode.

Humiliation. Raw, blistering humiliation. Even worse than being stripped naked.

“Tch. What’s with that look in your eyes? Is your so-called loyalty fake after all?” Yae-hime pulled her foot back and gazed down at her coldly, her eyes sharp as blades. That piercing stare sliced straight through Vera 3’s heart, leaving behind a strange, stinging pain.

On the other side, Vera 1 was seething with fury. Even though she was furious at Number Three for surrendering so disgracefully, the demon’s continued humiliation was even more infuriating.

Just as she was about to erupt, she heard Vera 3’s voice.

“No—no, it’s not fake. I’ll lick… I’ll lick Master’s foot!”

That sentence struck Vera 1 like thunder on a clear day, blowing her mind into chaos. The next thing she saw was Vera 3 holding that demon’s beautiful leg as if it were the most precious treasure in the world.

‘No… no! Don’t lick it!’ Vera 1 wanted to scream and stop her, but her mouth felt frozen. Somewhere deep inside, a voice resisted her.

Vera 3, her hands trembling, cupped Yae-hime’s bare foot. Her face turned pale, her eyes quivering. She knew very well: if she licked the demon’s foot in front of everyone… Some fundamental part of her humanity would vanish forever.

Behind her, Little Blue, Vera 2, 17, and 18 were all watching with eager anticipation. This was their first time seeing someone submit like this in real life, and a beautiful girl at that. They were thrilled.

Especially Vera 2, 17, and 18. As they watched Vera 3, it was like watching themselves.

‘Ah… it’s as if I were the one licking Master’s foot~’ Their affection for Yae-hime was so high that they didn’t feel even a trace of the humiliation Vera 3 did. If anything, their hearts were beating faster.

Feeling the faint coolness of the foot in her palms, Vera 3 finally made up her mind. She slowly leaned forward and stuck out her tongue. Seeing this, Vera 1’s pupils shrank to needlepoints. Her slightly open mouth tried to make a sound, but nothing came out.

Bit by bit, Vera 3’s tongue crept closer to Yae-hime’s toes… and then suddenly stopped. She still clung to the last sliver of her dignity. But the scent of roast chicken was so alluring, so soul-snatching, it tore at her pride, gnawed at her restraint… And finally, crushed it.

**Shlick!**[1](https://re-library.com/translations/reborn-as-a-transcendent/volume-3/chapter-695-mmm-pretty-girl-smells-so-good/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-110497)　

She did it, Vera 3 finally licked. The room fell silent. Everyone felt a strange and indescribable thrill. Even Vera 1 was no exception. That was the exact moment a human being abandoned all dignity. And yet, it didn’t feel disturbing. That scene… was like a painting. Beautiful beyond belief.

Vera 3 lingered on the experience. The humiliation vanished completely. Because the toes she had licked were… fragrant. That scent brought a strange sense of comfort. Peace.

‘Why does this demon… smells so good?!’ As if entranced, she licked again, and found herself completely captivated. ‘I lick, I lick, I’ll lick, lick, lick!’

In that moment, she was like a girl possessed, licking Yae-hime’s foot from toe to instep, savoring the fresh scent of her skin.

Above her, Yae-hime was dumbfounded. She had told Vera 3 to do this to shame her, to break her. So why had it turned into this?

‘Where the hell did this bootlicker come from!?’

“Stop!” she quickly ordered, putting an end to the foot-licking frenzy.

“……” Vera 3 reluctantly let go, licking the corner of her mouth as she looked up at Yae-hime. Her cheeks were flushed as she softly said, “Master, Vera 3 pledges her eternal loyalty to you.”

Her voice was full of sincerity, along with a hint of longing. The kind of longing only gluttony could provoke. It was obvious now, she had completely made peace with it. There was no more burden in her heart.

Once a person discarded their dignity, many things in life lost their value. And trying to pick that dignity back up again… was nearly impossible.

Hearing Number Three’s words, Vera 1 felt overwhelmed with emotion. There was sorrow, unease, pain, and defiance. All of it tangled together and eventually melted into a blank haze.

She gazed blankly at her sisters, a heavy weariness settling deep in her bones.

“Very good, Vera 3. From now on, we’re family. As long as you never betray me, I’ll always have your back.” Yae-hime spoke with sincere gravity in her voice.

“Yes, Master. Vera 3 will never betray you!” She stared at her master intently as she said it.

Hearing that, Vera 1 stood there, stunned and speechless, unsure how to react.

“Alright, eat.” Yae-hime nodded, picked up one of the roast chickens from the plate, and bent down to hand it to Vera 3.

Vera 3 took it with trembling hands, tears streaming down her face. “Thank you, Master, for your generous gift!” Then, she tore into it with wild hunger, ignoring all decorum as she devoured the honey-roasted chicken.

The savory scent filled the air, and Vera 1 felt herself on the edge of madness.

“And you?” Yae-hime turned her gaze toward her, smiling faintly. That smile looked gentle and innocent—beautiful, even. But to Vera 1, it was nothing less than grotesque. It was the smile of a devil crawling up from the depths of hell.

“Don’t want to pledge your loyalty to me?” the demon asked softly.

Vera 1 wanted to shake her head. But deep down, her heart screamed in resistance. ‘No… I don’t want to stay hungry. I want food. I want to eat… a lot!’

“Master asked you a question,” Little Blue chimed in, floating over with arms akimbo, looming over her.

“I… I…” Vera 1 glanced at Little Blue, then at her other sisters, and finally rested her gaze on Yae-hime. “I’ll lick.” As soon as she said it, the tears burst forth, her chest filled with a sorrow too bitter to bear.

She never imagined she would fall this far, that such a pitiful day would come.

Slowly, she crawled forward and, with trembling hands, lifted Yae-hime’s other foot. That beautiful jade foot looked impossibly appetizing. She hesitated, then leaned in and lightly brushed it with the tip of her tongue.

+++
